Plan of Shaytan

We begaun with the استعاذہ ..... which is seeking the protection of Allah from the cursed Shaytan..... And what we learnt in our study of the Istiaza..... and Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas..... is that Allah identifying for us..... or rather pointing out our worst enemy to us..... which is Iblees..... and all of his followers who are Shayateen..... What Allah does is..... he discloses for us ALL of Shaytan's plans..... He tells us about his short term goals..... his long term goals..... how he sets his traps for us..... how he..... very patiently..... puts us on the path of destruction..... Because he has one single goal..... All his whisperings have one single agenda..... to get human beings to take off their clothes.....
فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا
Shaytan whispered to them..... to expose..... what was covered off their ugliness..... their private parts..... Allah honored..... and dignified Adam AS and his children with clothing..... Why?..... To elevate them ABOVE animals..... because animals don't care for clothing..... There's no reason to honor and dignify animals..... because they are base creatures..... But Allah gave Adam AS and his children..... the intellect..... made them his representative on earth..... and therefore honored them with clothing..... And Shaytan wants to get humanity to remove their clothings..... He wants them to remove that honor and degrade and humiliate themselves down to that base level of animals..... And what is the ULTIMATE humiliation?.....
رَبَّنَآ إِنَّكَ مَن تُدْخِلِ ٱلنَّارَ فَقَدْ أَخْزَيْتَهُۥ
Oh master! No doubt..... the one you entered in hell fire has been truly humilated.....
So this is what he wants..... But he does this in such a subtle way..... He doesn't just tell us to do the wrong thing..... He makes the wrong thing beautiful to us..... and then we do it ourselves.....  And we see evidence of that all around us today..... People are so happy to take off their clothes..... to show some skin as they say.....
لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا
to expose to them what was covered of their ugliness..... Human being..... Intellectual being..... Khaleefatul Allah..... Allah's representative on this earth..... the one he created to manifest His divine attributes on this earth..... reduced to the level of an animal..... We announce it..... post it on facebook..... We make fun of those who DON'T do it..... call them backward..... and cavemen..... and what not..... It's really amazing if you think about it..... But when it comes to you own beauty..... The beauty that is a manifestation of the divine essence..... AlJameel..... The most beautiful..... He gave you something from his own divine names..... and you are throwing that name around in front of the entire world.....  You value your phone more than the divine name of Allah.....  Astaghfirullah!.....  What amazing logic!!! ..... But this is what Shaytan does..... Because he's a trickster..... He'll come up with the most PERFECT logic..... He'll convince you..... and prove to you..... that fire is better than clay..... Because logic is his thing.....
Shaytan is a liar

Junaid baghdadee relates that he once had a dream in which he met Iblees..... And he has this dialogue with Iblees in his dream..... He asked Iblees..... Why wouldn't you do Sajda to Adam AS?..... Why would you disobey Allah? ..... How could you be so stupid to refuse and stand against Allah when he gave you a command?..... What's wrong with you..... And Iblees replies..... Ya Junaid..... How could I do Sajda to anyone other than Allah?..... And Junaid got completely thrown off..... He's like WOAH..... That's deep dude!..... And so he goes in this state of complete confusion..... Because now what Iblees just said to him made perfect sense..... But you see this is what Iblees does..... He's a trickster..... He presents prefect logic.....
So Junaid goes to Imam AS and tells him about his dream..... Imam AS said..... الابلیس ھو الکذاب..... Iblees is a liar..... That could not be the reason he refused to disobey Allah..... because what he's saying..... that I couldn't bow down to anyone other than Allah..... that's from the Adab..... That's from the ettiquettes..... But .....  الامر فوق الادب..... The command of Allah is greater than all etiquettes..... If you are the president of your school..... or a teacher of your class..... And the school principal tells you do something..... like repreimand a student for something he did..... That may not be the best ettiquetes..... It may not be a nice thing to do..... But you have to do it..... Because the command came from someone who is superior in rank..... So even though I wouldn't do sajda to anyone other than Allah..... but if it is Allah himself commanding me to do Sajda..... I have to do it..... I won't do sajda if you tell me to do it..... But if Allah himself is issuing a direct command..... I HAVE to obey..... because .....  الامر فوق الادب..... Command trumps etiquettes..... ..... But this is what Iblees does..... He ticks and confuses through logic.....

Be my slave instead..... worship me instead of him..... This is the striaght path.....


Allah identified our enemy for us

Sounds like a friend to me..... A friend who loves me..... who cares about me..... Someone who is genuinely concerned for my well being?..... But then you know what's more amazing?..... He didn't just point out all of this and just leave me by myself..... right?
Think about your best friend in school..... Let's say he finds out that someone is going to hurt you..... let's say he's planning to ambush you after class..... So your friend tells you..... So no matter what this guy says..... don't listen to him..........
Basically your friend tells you everything about this guy who's planning to hurt you..... Now.....  JUST doing that much for you..... qualifies him as a true friend!..... doesn't it?..... That alone will convince you that he really loves you and cares about you..... But then he says..... you know what?..... I know you're as sucker for ice cream..... And as soon as he tells you there is an ice cream truck down that path..... and they have chocolate flavor..... I know once you heart that..... you'll forget EVERYTHING I just said..... and you'll be like..... ugghh LEAD THE WAY!..... So you know what?..... If you want..... I'll walk with you..... I'll stop you from walking that path..... right when he tempts you.....  And if you still choose to walk the path..... I'll try to protect you when these guys try to jump you..... If your friend does does that..... NOW what kind of a friend would he be?.....

Allah did not just inform us about Shaytan's plots..... and then leave me to deal with it all by myself..... because he knew..... that we're dealing with an enemy that we cannot see..... and we are at a clear disadvantage against him..... So now if I have even half a brain..... after knowing all this..... after realizing that I am not going to be able to fight Shaytan by myself..... because this is an extremley powerful and ruthless enemy..... and on top of that I can't even see him or hear him when he's whispering to me..... That is precisely what we're doing with the Istiaza..... We are entering Allah's protection..... so that Shaytan does not interfere with our spiritual journey..... which is the first ayah of Surah AlFateha..... BARR.....

Tie camel first in order to protect it

This is really important to understand..... We're not going to benefit from the Fateha..... if we do not mee the requirements of the Istiaaza..... Someone came to the masjid for prayers..... He had his camel with him..... He met Rasul Allah outside the masjid..... and he asked him.....
  يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ.....  أَعْقِلُهَا وَأَتَوَكَّلُ.....  أَوْ أُطْلِقُهَا وَأَتَوَكَّلُ
Should I tie my camel first and then trust Allah..... or should I leave it untied and then trust Allah..... The messenger replied.....
اعْقِلْهَا وَتَوَكَّلْ
Tie the camel..... and THEN trust Allah to protect it..... So we need to tie the camel first..... We can't just can't leave the camel untied..... and then expect Allah to protect it..... We have to do OUR part first..... The camel is a symbol for our desires..... Because they are massive..... they are a powerful beast..... like the camel..... The camel is no ordinary animal..... It's a very massive..... very strong animal..... just like our desires and our temptations..... So we need to tie and bind this camel of our desires..... which if you remember..... is literally what the word Aqal means..... We have to empty the cup before we can fill it again..... Istiaza is turning over the cup..... emptying it out..... COMPLETELY..... Because that is literally what the heart is..... It is a container.....  and every container has its limits.....  And if the heart has reached its limits with the Haram.....  it will not have any room for the halaal to come in..... And taht would be disaster..... And this is why the sahaba..... (رضی اللہ عنھم) said ..... that the prophet litreally emtied us out .....  He emptied out our hearts.....  from the darkness of ignorance.....  and filled it with light..... 
So there is an emptying that has to take place BEFORE the filling.....  Just like you have to exhale before you can inhale.....  Just like the heart has to be contracted before it can be  expanded.....  This is the nature of creation..... right?.....   the diastolic the systolic.....  this is the very nature of human beings.....  The pupil expands in order to take in light.....  and then it contracts to prevent light from coming in..... These are all signs..... These are all ayaats..... Because this is the very nature ..... Allah has created us on..... Because He is AlQabid and AlBasit.....  he is the expander and he is the contractor.....  so the more we expand for Shaitan the more we contract for Al-Rehman.....  And the more we expand for the AlRehman.....  the more we contract for Shaytan..... That's La Ilaha ..... Illa Allah.......... La Ilaha..... There is no Ilah..... That's contraction..... That's tying our camel at the doorstep of Allah..... And then there is Bismillah..... that is entering the masjid of Allah.....
That's the entire concept of the Istiaaza..... We are emptying out our hearts..... We're emptying it out.....  from the whispers of Shaytan..... from all desires of the haraam..... from all forbidden temptations..... why? ..... So that we can now fill it with the Fateha..... We are closing the doors on the cursed Shaytan..... so that we can walk through the doors of Allah's mercy ..... and this is how we get to.....  بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم

The next thing I want to talk about is the استعاذہ which is what we commonly recite before we begin reciting the Quran itself .  اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم. This ayah is called the استعاذہ. It is not a part of Surah Al-Fateha itself.  but it is certainly linked to the Fateha. and every other surah of the Quran for that matter.  The Fateha actually starts with the Basmallah. which is بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم . In the Arab world. this ayah بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم is referred to the Basmallah. with a fatha or a zabar. But one thing to remember is that this basmallah is an ACTUAL PART of Al-Fateha itself. but it is NOT a part of the remaining Surahs. I'll say that again. The Basmallah is an actual part of Surah Al-Fateha. but it is NOT a part of the remaining Surahs. The Basmallah is recited before all other surahs to honor those surahs. because it contains the primary name and attributes of  Allah and AlRehman and AlRaheem. and through that we begin the recitation of Allah's holy book .  but it is not the first ayah of any of the other surahs.
But when it comes to Surah AlFateha. it IS a part of the Surah itself. it is the first ayah.  It is the leader and the king of all remaining ayats of Surah Al-Fateha. As we know Surah AlFateha has 7 ayats and the Basmallah. is the highest ranking ayah of  those 7 ayats. If you skip this ayah. you lose all the power and majesty of Surah AlFateha.  and InshaAllah when we study this ayah. you'll understand why.

So what I want you to remember is that أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم is called the استعاذہ . and بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم is called the Basmallah! Now before we being the استعاذہ . let's get an idea of what topics we are going to cover over the next few sessions.
Since this استعاذہ is used to seek refuge or protection of Allah from the cursed Shaytan. So InshaAllah as part of analyzing this ayah. we will try to get an in depth understanding of who Shaytan is. what made him a Shaytan. What is the difference between Shaytan and Iblees. Are they two separate entities? Or are they both the same? What is Shaytan's real agenda. and why he is so bent upon getting us into trouble. What is this guy's problem.? How does he attack? What are his whisperings? What is this thing called وسوسۃ. InshaAllah we will cover all these topics over the next few sessions.
As part of our analysis and study of the استعاذہ we will also study two surahs. Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas. And the reason for that. is that these 2 surahs are in reality the explanation of the details of the استعاذہ. We will look at the true meaning of the word protection. and why we need Allah's protection against Shaytan. why is it that we are not able to protect ourselves. why do we need a higher power. and we will also see why it is ONLY Allah . and no other power other than Allah. that is capable of protecting us. We will see what the requirements of coming under Allah's protection are. How do we make ourselves worthy of His protection.  these are some of the things we will InshaAllah cover in the study of this ayah. and trust me. once we are done with the study of this ayah. the استعاذہ will take on a whole new meaning for us . We will never be able to say the استعاذہ . in the casual superficial way that we do today. Today when we recite the استعاذہ against Shaytan. he probably laughs at us.  because he knows that our استعاذہ is an empty shell.  It's a fake bullet. an empty cartridge. a blunt sword. that does nothing against him. except maybe tickle him a bit. But InshaAllah after we are equipped with the knowledge of  this ayah. our استعاذہ will become an extremely powerful strike against Shaytan. because it will be backed up with the comprehension of not just the ayah itself. but also SurahAlFalaq and Surah AnNaas. and also because we will have met the requirements of gaining Allah's protection . أنشاء اللہ تعالی.

So let's begin بأذن اللہ .

 

Meaning of ISTIAAZA


What is the استعاذہ? and where did it come from? The استعاذہ comes from the ayah of the Quran itself. Allah commands us in Surah Al-Nahal:
فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ
When you are about to recite the Quran. then seek refuge of Allah from Shaitaan AlRajeem. Also in Surah Aeraaf Allah says
وَإِمَّا يَنْزَغَنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ نَزْغٌۭ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ
And before the shaitaan. whispers his evil into you. seek refuge of Allah
 إِنَّهُۥ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ . because he is the all listener and the all knower.

Therefore. before we begin studying the actual ayaats of Surah Al-Fateha. I want us all to gain a really good understanding of this استعاذہ. and how it is linked to Surah AlFateha and the rest of the Quran.

Spiritual protection
So what does the word استعاذہ mean? The word استعاذہ comes from the word ، عاذ ، یعوذ، أعوذ . which means to turn to someone for protection. to turn to someone seeking their help. to tell somebody that you are in danger and you cannot defend yourself on your own. It is an acknowledgment that I need the protection of another entity. that is more powerful than myself. to help me spiritually. not to help me physically. You don't use the word عاذ or أعوذ  in arabic for physical help. you ONLY use the word أعوذ when you require spiritual help.
When is it that we need physical help? When we are dealing with the seen. And when do we need spiritual help? When we are dealing with the unseen. Physical help are things. for which we need to dial 911. or call someone by saying. Please help me I'm being attacked. In such situations in Arabic. we would NOT say عاذ .We would use other words such as نجد or نصر . You understand?

SO عاذ is used exclusively to solicit spiritual help and protection. whose protection? Protection of a diety. a god. a divine power. an entity that is all powerful.
So these are the 2 requirements of the word عاذ . It is used to seek spiritual protection. and ONLY from a diety.  Only when these two requirements are fulfilled. the word عاذ is used in Arabic. If I turn for spiritual guidance to a religious leader. or a psychologist or a therapist. I CANNOT use the word عاذ. because it's not the same thing. I am not turning to them with the intention of seeking their protection. I am turning to them for gainnig knowledge. seeking guidance and help. not protection. And they are not a diety. therefore I cannot use the word عاذ for them. even though the guidance and help I need is spiritual in nature. you understand?

So who is that diety that we are turning to for spiritual help? أعوذ باللہ . That diety is Allah! Turning to an entity in this manner is done EXCLUSIVELY for Allah (SWT). Now why is that important? It is important because. this act of the  استعاذہ . this act of turning to Allah seeking His spiritual protection. itself becomes an act of worship. Why is that? Because we are obeying Allah's command. Allah commanded us.
وَإِمَّا يَنْزَغَنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ نَزْغٌۭ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ;  إِنَّهُۥ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ
BECAUSE we are turning ONLY to Allah for our spiritual protection in compliance and obedience to his command. the act of  استعاذہ itself becomes an act of worship. And this is important to understand. Because if I turn to another entity for spiritual protection in this way. other than Allah. then that act in itself.  becomes the very definition of Shirk. which is to hold a partner with Allah. Because that means. I believe that someone other than Allah has the power to protect me spiritually from the enemy I seek protection from. That would be equivalent to prostrating or submitting before an idol. And this is something that people before Islam used to do.


In Pre Islamic Ignorance. (دور الجاھلیۃ) when a man would travel through the desert. and he would camp for the night. he would be scared of the attackes of jinns and deamons. He would be scared that they would attack him in the night. so he would stand up on a high cliff and announce loudly :
أعوذ بِسَیِّدِ ھٰذا الوادی
I seek refuge and protection  from the leader of the jinn of  this valley that I'm spending the night in.

And what would this do? Would the jinns protect them? No! In Surah Jinn . Allah mentions on the tongue of the jinn . that when those people did this. it only increased the jinn in their arragoance and in their efforts to mislead mankind.
وَأَنَّهُۥ كَانَ رِجَالٌۭ مِّنَ ٱلْإِنسِ يَعُوذُونَ بِرِجَالٍۢ مِّنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَزَادُوهُمْ رَهَقًۭا
And no doubt, there were men among human beings . who took shelter with the leader of the jinns, but they only increased them in sin and disbelief.

So we do not seek this kind of spiritual protection from any other entity except Allah. so the words  اعوذ باللہ means.  that I turn for spiritual help and for spiritual protection . to a diety who is Allah. who is powerful. acknowledging at the same time. that I am NOT powerful. 
So when I say اعوذ باللہ . I am saying. I am accepting. that I have no power to protect myself. THERFORE I am turning to Allah who is the all powerful. I am incapable. therefore I am turning to the capable. I am weak. I am ضعیف. therefore I am turning to the strong . the قوی the عزیز. I am a slave. who needs protection of his master.  therefore I am turning to my master.

So my reciting the استعاذہ . in and of itself. contains 2 acknowledgments. the acknowledgment of my weakness. and my incapability to protect myself against the attacks of Shaytan. AND the acknowledgment of the power of my protector. my diety. my Allah. who is strong. who is powerful. and who IS capable of protecting me from my greatest enemy . Shaytan AlRjaeem. the cursed devil. And therefore my act of reciting the استعاذہ . my act of turning ONLY to Allah seeking his protection . BECOMES  an act of worship.  And every act of worship has a reward. So the next time you recite the استعاذہ think about this. and it will change the way you approach Allah's protection.  and InshaAllah. we'll look at this further in much more detail.

3 version of ISTIAAZA


But before we do that. let's talk a bit about the semantics and the usage of the استعاذہ. and why is it placed before the recitation of Quran? There are 3 common ways in which the استعاذہ is recited. The first is the short version of the istiaaza    . أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم   .which means. I seek Allah's protection from Shaytan AlRejeem. the cursed devil. that's the simple one.

The second is one which Rasul Allah sometimes used to say even during his salaah
أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم مِن ھَمزِہِ وَ نَفْخِہِ وَ نَفْثِہِ
I seek refuge of Allah from Shaitaan AlRajeem. from his whispering. from his prodings and from his blowings.  Let's examine these words.

The first word ھَمزِہِ comes from ھُمَزَہ which means to prod and to poke. You know how sometimes people do that too. with their words. they hurt people. they poke. they prod. kick them when they are down. They verbally stick a knife in the heart and then twist it around a bit. And they do it under the disguise of being a wellwisher. So for example. someone is already worried about their survival because they lost their job. and the ھامز will go . Oh really? You lost your job? O thats so bad. especially when the economy is so horrible right now. its almost going to be impossible for you to find another. I know this family. the guy lost his job. they eventually lost the house. his wife divorced him. his kids left him. he ended up committing suicide. It's SO bad out there. but don't worry. you'll be fine.
Ever met or interacted with such people? This is one meaning of Humaza. . And Allah says.
وَيْلٌۭ لِّكُلِّ هُمَزَةٍۢ لُّمَزَةٍ
There is destruction for those who prod and poke. Shaytan is constantly proding and poking us. constantly urging us to do bad things .He is constantly pushing our buttons. Instigating us. making us angry and mean. forcing us to over react. that is all ھَمزْ .

Nafakha means to blow. As Allah says in the Quran in the story of Adam AS's creation.
فَإِذَا سَوَّيْتُهُۥ وَنَفَخْتُ فِيهِ مِن رُّوحِى
Once I completed the creation of Adam. I blew my soul into him. this is nafakha. to blow. Shaytan is constantly blowing his thoughts. his ideas. desires and temptations. fear and anger. jealousy and envy. He is contantly blowing these things into us. and that is all نَفْخَ.

And then there is Nafasa. (not with a س but a ث) which is also a type of blowing. but it's one in which a little bit of spit comes out. and this worse than just blowing. This tactic is mentioned in the Quran in Surah AlFalaq
من شر النفاثات فی العقد
InshaAllah we'll look at this word in much more detail when we study the Surah. So Shaytan pokes us. prods us. blows on us. spits on hus.  He uses all these tactics and mechanations to harm us. And that's why Rasul Allah SAS would seek Allah AWJ's protection from all these tactics of Shaytan by saying.
أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیمِ ۔  من ھَمزِہِ وَ نَفْخِہِ وَ نَفْثِہِ

 

This is another varition of this same أستعاذہ . which was used by Rasul Allah. in which he added السمیع العلیم to it.
أعوذ باللہ السمیع العلیم من الشیطان الرجیم ۔ من ھَمزِہِ وَ نَفْخِہِ وَ نَفْثِہِ
I seek refuge of Allah who hears all and who knows all. from Shaitaan AlRajeem. from his whispering from his prodings and from his blowings. So this is the longest version of the أستعاذہ that our prophet would sometime use. Now two attributes of Allah السمیع العلیم are used in this version. and we also use these two attributes. in every Fard namaz when we recite Wajjahtu Wajhee before we begin AlFatiha. What is the last sentence of that dua?
علی ملت ابرھیم و دین محمد و ولایت علی و أبرؤ الیہ من أعدائہ الظالمین ۔
وَ أعوذ باللہ السمیع العلیم من الشیطان الَّعین الرجیم
and then we recite the Basmallah and Surah AlFateha.

Now the question is. why these 2 names of Allah?. Out of 99 names of Allah. why these 2 names in particular? Its very interesting. What is the meaning of السمیع ?. . It means the one. who hears everything! and what is the meaning of العلیم? The one who knows everything! So السمیع العلیم is the one who hears everything and knows everything.
Can you and I hear the Shaytan when he whispers to us? When he pokes us. prods us. tempts us. can we hear him speak? We cannot! But السمیع can hear. You and I cannot hear. Even though a Shaytan a Jinn is whispering to us. we cannot directly hear anything. the mental thought of that evil he is proding us with. comes in our minds. the evil thought he is blowing into us. that comes in our mind. but we do not actually hear him speaking. But a السمیع  can hear him in the very act. So when se say:
أعوذ باللہ السمیع
We acknowledge that Oh Allah. I cannot hear Shaytan. But YOU CAN. because you are السمیع . and that's why YOU can protect me when Shaytan whispers to me.

and then we say العلیم . because Allah knows everything. What does he know in this case? He knows the level of our sincerity. our اخلاص! He knows that when we recite the أستعاذہ . are we saying it with sincerity?. or is it just a parroted phrase that rolls off our tongue without any comprehension or intention of actually seeking His protection?. Allah العلیم know whether we truly intend to turn towards him for protection or not. because He knows what's in our heart. He knows if we truly want to submit ourselves before his majesty.or if we are just saying it for the sake of saying it.  And only when the علیم finds us to be sincere. the سمیع protects us from the whispers of Shaytan.
Therefore when we recite the أستعاذہ . we should make sure we say it sincerely. and with the intention of actually seeking Allah's protection . We shouldn't make these merely parroting phrases that roll of our tongues without meaning. and the need for his protection must come from the heart . with sincerity. because he is السمیع العلیم .





Now why do we recite the أستعاذہ BEFORE we begin reciting the Quran? or even before reciting the Basmallah.

The reason for that is that. any time we need to create something new. we must first deconstruct. and get rid of what's already there. If you need to put up a new building. you have to bring down the existing structure. clean out the rubble. remove the old foundation. and even the land out. Only then new construction can begin. Similarly before we recite the Quran. we cleanse our heart. we purify our intentions. we humble oursevles before Allah. by accepting our weakness. by accepting our incapabilities. by admitting our need for his protection. and accepting his ultimate power over us. We completely submit ourselves to him. We admit to Allah. that O Allah I am weak. I am helpless. I am turning to you for YOUR help and YOUR protection . because I lack the capability and the capacity to protect myself against the temptations and whispers of Shaytan.

Another reason is. that we use the أستعاذہ to purify our tongues. we use it to purify our speech. from the filth of anything and everything inappropriate that we might have said earlier.   It is like performing wudu before the salaah. in which. we first empty out the filth from our bodies. and we cleanse ourselves.  before we stand in front of Allah in prayer. أستعاذہ is the same way. it is the wuzu of our tongue. because we want to cleanse ourselves from the evil and the filth of Shaytan AlRajeem. his teachings. his whispers. his concepts. his prods. We want to cleanse our hearts from all of that. right before we mention the glorious name and attributes of Allah AWJ. We want to empty the cups of our heart. so that it can be filled again with what Allah is about to give us. especially during Salaah.

Now why do we receit the أستعاذہ . specifically before reciting the Quran? The answer to that is. because Allah commanded us to do so.
فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ
When you begin reciting the Quran. seek refuge of Allah from Shaytan AlRajeem. So the the first reason. is obedience. But why did Allah give us such a command? Because Shaytan can corrupt and contiminate our understanding of the message of Quran. And how does he do that? He does that by interpreting the wrong meanings of the ayats for us. Through Qiyaas. Through induction. and deduction. We. especially as Sulemani's. we do not use our own logic when interpreting the Quran. We follow the interpretations that have been prescribed by Maulana Ali and the Aimma Tahireen from his progeny. Now why is that? That seems counter intuitive. Why can't I use my own logic? Because when you and I use our logic. it will always be based on the information we currently have access to. mixed in without our experiential biases.  And then as the information changes. our logic deduction will change to accomodate the new information.

I'll give you an example. You see the still image of a video. in which a black man is pushing or shoving an old lady. And you can tell by the still image. that he is pushing the old lady quite hard. because she is almost flying through the air. Now mix that in with any negative experiential bias you may have about black people. and you reach a certain negative conclusion based on this information. Now if you rewind the movie. you see that a man is trying to hrul up a huge piano from the window of his apartment on the 4th floor. And the rope connected to the piano snaps. And this black man sees the rope snapping. He rushes towards the old lady who was standing under the piano. and pushes her out of the way and saves her life. Now. with access to this new set of data. our conclusion about the black man changes. So what changed? our view of the big picture. When we just saw the still image of the man pushing the old lady. we reached one conclusion. when we zoomed out and gained access to the unseen. we reach a different conclusion.
So the only possibility. the only scenario in which we can make the perfect logical deduction. is when we have access to ALL the information. what we can see. and what we cannot see. And also when that information is not contaminated by our experiential biases. ONLY then we are able to make an accurate logical deduction. When we have all the content placed within the complete context. only then we can produce accurate logical deducations.

Now if you study the Quran. you will find that it always delivers the content. But what does it NEVER provide? The Context. The ayah states what Allah commands Rasul Allah (SWS) to say. but it does not describe the surrounding situations. It does not say. Rasul Allah was standing in the market. it was day time. the sun was shining bright. A beduine came to Rasul Allah. asked this question. and these were the conditions of that person when he asked the question. and now based on all this information. I am issuing the following command. and if you notice this command is also applicable in the following 20 scenairos. The Quran does not do that. The Quran simply issues the command!

Content vs context

But what did we just say is the most important thing for content? CONTEXT! Content placed out of context is disasterous. So where can we get that complete context to place that content in?  The Imams are the only ones who can provide the complete context of the Quran. Not just from what can be seen. but also from what can NOT be seen. not just within physical context. but also spiritual context? Why? Because they have access to ALL the information. and their interpretations are not polluted by experiential biases. Therefore ONLY they know know the true interpretations of these ayats. that balance perfectly on both. the physical and spiritual scale.  and when this content is placed in its proper context. the essential goal and purpose of Islam is achieved. which is PEACE.

And what Shaytan does. is he deduces logic based on incomplete context. and mixes it in with experiential biases. which results in chaos and destruction. And we see examples of this all around us. The ayats that are meant to promote peace and tranquility. many muslims. misguided by the whisperings of Shaytan. analyzing content out of context.  they use the very same ayats to promote violence and terror. And that's just once area. There are many many other areas of the Quran. where Shaytan has been VERY successful in corrupting the thought process of mankind. And why does he do that? What does he prod us. why does he whisper to us to reach these inconclusive and inaccurate deduction? Because that is EXACTLY what he did himself.  InshaAllah we'll talk about this when we talk about Iblees.

So now we know the purpose of this command that Allah issued in the Quran.

فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ

Therefore throught our أستعاذہ we want to seek Allah's protection from the cursed Shaitaan. from corrupting our understanding. and contamination our concepts of the message of the Quran. We say أعوذ باللہ to indicate to Allah our sincerity. that O Allah! We wish to seek guidance from your message. Oh Allah! I want this book to help me on the straight path. on Sirat AlMustaqeem.  I do not want to be deluded and deceived by Shiataan. in straying away from your straight path.   I don't want him to stand between me and your guidance. Because ONLY you can protect me from him. because you are  السمیع العلیم. . And once I surrender myself into YOUR protection. no harm can come to me from any Shaytaan. no matter how powerful he is. in his whispers . his prodings and his mechanations. Because now I have YOU to protect me from my greatest enemy. Shaytan AlRajeem.


And how do we know that he is our worst enemy? And why do we need Allah's protection? Because in the words of Quran. Iblees promised Allah that he will misguide each and everyone of us. He said to Allah:
قَالَ فَبِعِزَّتِكَ لَأُغْوِيَنَّهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ
I swear by your might Oh Allah. I will make it my job. I will make it my ONLY purpose in life.  to misguide each and every one of your creation.
لَأُغْوِيَنَّهُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ
He promised Allah!. Imagine that. Just imagine the hatred and his enimosity in his words. Oh Allah! I promise you that I will misguide them. I will deceive them. But then even Iblees had to put a clause. Even he had to put a disclaimer in his promise . He said. I will misguide each and everyone of your slaves.
إِلَّا عِبَادَكَ مِنْهُمُ ٱلْمُخْلَصِينَ
Except the slaves who YOU have chosen . Except the slaves who turn to YOU sincerely . with Ikhlaas. those I will not be able to misguide.
So by the أستعاذہ . by reciting  أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم . we reach out to Allah who is السمیع العلیم  . and we beg Him . to make us among His chosen ones. To make us among those He protects. and the ones Iblees has no control over.

Linquistics of Shaytan

OK so now that we've talked about. seeking the protection OF Allah. let's understand who are we seeking protection FROM.  We are seeking protection from the cursed Shaytan. أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم. So let's look at this word Shaytan. The very first thing to understand.  is that Shaytan is not the name of a person.  There is no entity NAMED Shaytaan. Shaytan is an adjective. It is a word that describes the traits of an entity. It's not a proper noun. You cannot name a child Shaytaan. You know. first name Shaytan last name Rajeem. you cannot do that. You can call a child Shaytan. when he sets fire to the living room. of the guest who invited you over for dinner.  but you cannot name a child Shaytan.

Now linguistically speaking . the word Shaytan has several meanings.

The word shaitaan comes from the root word Shatana. which means "That which is far removed". Shaitaan is someone that is far removed from Allah's mercy. from Allah's rehma! He is far removed from righteousness. he is far removed from piety. He is far removed from the straight path. He is far removed from الصراط المستقیم . In Urdu we say. دھتکارا ہوا . There is also another word in Arabic which holds the same meaning. لعنۃ. which means "Removal from Allah's mercy".  When we talk about Shaytan. and also the tyrants of history who hurt the people of truth. we say لعنۃ اللہ علیھم . which means. May they be far removed from the mercy of Allah.  This is the worst thing that could be said to anyone in the realm of Islam. This is the ULTIMATE curse that we as Muslims can place on someone. so we should be very careful when we use this word. It is a common practice especially in our jamaat. we use this word لعنۃ very casually. We should be very careful. and really understand what it means before we say it.

So anyone. who exhibits these traits of being far removed from Allah's mercy . is called a Shaytan

From the same root word you have شَطَنْ which means rope. Why? Because Shaytan ties us and binds us. with the ropes of desires and temptations. He binds us with the ropes and chains of desires. and emotionally and spiritually we feel trapped in those desires. He also traps us in hatred. in enimosity. in contempt. in pride. in jealousies. and we cannot escape out of that place. We know what we are doing is wrong. it's wrong spiritually. morally. ethically .  but it's almost like our desires and temptations have bound us and we just can't help ourselves. that is شَطَنْ . and that's why he is called Shaytan.  Therefore anyone who tempts us. encourages us towards evil. ties us with the ropes of desires and temptations. envy. contempt. jealousy . the adjective Shaytan applies to them as well.

Shatan also means . someone who is consumed with rage. Therefore the adjective Shaytan also applies to someone who goes into the state of insane rage. and loses control of himself. such a person too is a strong candidate for the title of Shaytan.

Another meaning is that of a coward. And that is Shaytan always works in the shadows. He never presents himself openly as an enemy. He attacks from behind. and when he comes from the front. he pretends to be a friend. He pretends that he cares. he's appreciative. he's loving. while all the time he harbours hatred and enemosity in his heart against the one he is interacting with. Therefore the adjective Shaytan applies to people with such qualities as well.

So the first thing to understand is that Shaytan is a very generic term. it is an adjective.  that applies to any human being. أنس or جن . Man or Spirit. So am I saying that there are shayateen among human beings?. I am absolutely saying this. Those human beings that are far removed from the mercy and blessings of Allah . those who are far removed from the straight path. those tyring hard to remove others from the straight path as well. those who are tying others with the ropes of desires and temptations. those who are consumed with rage. those who instigate others to the point of rage. those who are cowards. they lack the courage to face someone with the truth. but instead attack in the shadows or behind their backs. whether they are men or women. regardless of their external manerisms.  regardless of their external display of piety. regardless of their visible display of love and affetion and sincerity. they are all called Shayateen.  Anyone preventing us from worshipping Allah. anyone calling us to worhsip an entity other than allah. through its various mechanations. temptations. desires.  they are all from among the شیاطین الانس والجن.

So Shaitaan is NOT the name of an individual. That is Iblees!. who is the leader and king of all Shayateen. Iblees is a proper noun. Iblees is the name of an actual entity. he is the leader. Shaytaan is a generic term. that applies to all of his followers. You understand?  Iblees is the master. the leader. and all his disciples and followers. whether they are from human beings or Jinns. they are called Shayateen. 

Linguistics of Jinn

Now Let's talk about Jinn. What is a jinn? The word Jinn literally means that which is hidden, veiled or concealed.

From this same root word we get the word  جُنون . meaning insanity or madness. and the person exhibiting this insanity is called مجنون . meaning insane. Why is that? Because a mad man is someone whose intellect has been concealed. whose intellect has been veiled. .
and from the same word we also have جَنَّۃ meaning heaven. Why? because heaven is invisible. it is hidden. it is veiled and concealed from our eyes.
Also from the same root word. we have جَنِین . a fetus . Because it is concealed and hidden in the womb of its mother.

So Jinn are called jinns because they are hidden from our eyes. they are invisible to us. they exist but we cannot see them.

Jinns are NOT a different creation from human beings. they are not a separate creation. they are simply souls that are detached from their bodies. When a human being who has the attributes of a shaytaan. an evil man.  when he dies. and his soul detaches from his body. he is no longer called Insaan. he is now called a jinn. Insaan is the seen form. Jinn is the unseen form. but they are both the same entity. When a disbeliever.  someone who is far removed from the path of Allah. during his life on this earth. when his soul is attached to his body. he is called Shaitaan AlIns. meaning the Shaytan in human form. But when this same disbeliever dies. and his soul separates from his body. he is now called Shaitan AlJinn. The Shaytan in the unseen form.  So Jinn is not a separate creation of Allah. They are the same creation as us. just disconnected from their bodies. Now just like humans. there are good jinns and they are evil jinns. So both types exist in spiritual form. just as both types exist in spiritual form.

So the Jinn and Ins. are not two separate creations. they are in essence one single creation. When connected with their bodies. in physical forms they are called Shayateen AlIns. when they die. and we know that it is the body that dies. the soul lives on forever. so when their souls get detached from their bodies. they are called Shayateen AlJinn. because they can no longer be seen. Do you understand?
 

Rajeem

So we seek refuge of Allah from what? Shaitaan! Shaitaan than exist in the physical form as human beings. and Shaitaan that exist in the spiritual form as Jinns. We seek protection of Allah from these evil entities. who is what? Rajeem! Just like the adjective Shytan. Rajeem is a also an adjective. Shaytan and Rajeem are both adjectives. so what's the difference? Shaytan is the primary adjective that describes the trait of an evil entity.  and Rajeem is a secondary adjective that describes the evil trait itself. I'll say that again. Shaytan is the primary adjective that describes the trait of an evil entity.  and Rajeem is a secondary adjective that describes the evil trait itself.

The word rajeem comes from Rajama . and Rajam means to pelt with stones. To cast aside . So AlRajeem is the one who has cast aside by Allah. Because of his actions he is pelted away by Allah. He is مطرود He is rejected and denied the mercy of Allah . In fact both the words Shaitaan and Rajeem have a similar meaning to them. Shaitaan. the one who is far removed. Rajeem. the one who has been cast away.

So an evil entity. by its NATURE is Shaytann. It is far away from the truth. and the evil entity by its ACTIONS is rajeem. it has been cast away. I'll say this again. Listen carefully. Shaitaan by his NATURE is far removed from the truth. and Shaitaan by his ACTIONS is rajeem. he has been cast away. he has been pelted away. Our thoughts. our concepts. our beliefs. they translate into actions. When thoughts are evil. the primary adjective Shaytan applies. when those evil thoughts convert into actions. the secondary adjective Rajeem applies. and Allah casts such beings away. or pelts them away from Him because of their evil actions.
So for example. a disbeliever adheres to the concept of multiple gods. That is a concept far removed from the truth. because what is the truth? The truth is لا الہ الا اللہ . there is no diety except Allah. So such a being is Shaytan . he is far removed from the truth of  لا الہ الا اللہ .because of his concept of Polytheism. and because of his concepts. he commits the act of worshipping multipe idols. He prostrates to stones. And because of this action.  Allah rejects him. and He pelts him away. and He casts him away from Him. and he becomes Rajeem.
So Shaitaan by his NATURE is far removed from the truth. and Shaitaan by his ACTIONS is rajeem. is stoned away.

So with the استعاذہ we seek refuge of Allah from Shaitaan ArRajeem. We seek Allah's protection for the safety of our souls from those who are evil in their concepts. in their thinking. as well as those who are evil in their actions. We also seek Allah's protection from becoming from among those! This is VERY VERY important to understand. We too are human beings. We too have thoughts. beliefs. concepts. we too perform actions based on those concepts. the adjective shaytaan applies to anyone in human form. We being sulemanis. we are not exempted or excluded from this adjective of Shaytan. So with the استعاذہ . we not only seek Allah's refuge. his protection from other external evil entities. we also seek his protection. for our own souls . we also seek his refuge. for our own lives. That Oh Allah! with this استعاذہ by saying أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم we turn to you for your protection. Not just from the external enemies. but also from us turning into those enemies that you cast away. Oh Allah! Protect our concepts. our beliefs. our thinking from becoming evil. Protect our concepts from becoming far removed from the truth. because if that happens we too will become from among those. who you have called Shaytan. and we know that our thoughts will inevitably translate into actions. and when that happens. we too will become from among the Rajeem. the ones that you have casts away. and you hvae pelted and stoned away from His company and mercy.

So this is the essence of the استعاذہ . that Allah protect us from the external evil entities who are shaytan because of their nature. and rajeem because of their actions. and protect our nature from becoming a shaytan. and protect our actions from become rajeem.  On the day of judgment. may we not be from among those. that Allah have descirbed.

هَلْ أَتَىٰكَ حَدِيثُ ٱلْغَشِيَةِ. Have you heard the story of the day of judgment?
وُجُوهٌۭ يَوْمَئِذٍ خَشِعَةٌ. There will be those faces that will be full of shame and abjection. faces that will be abased and degraded. faces of those far removed from the truth. faces of Shayateen
عَامِلَةٌۭ نَّاصِبَةٌۭ. with their actions of hard work (actions done in the displeasure of Allah). Actions that are Rajeem. casted away
تَصْلَىٰ نَارًا حَامِيَةًۭ. they will enter the burning fires of hell.

By the Shafa'a . intercession of Rasul Allah SAS . May Allah protect us all from being from among such people on the day of judgment.

Iblees

Now that we've talked a bit about the adjective Shaytan. let's talk a bit about their leader Iblees. Most of you already know this story.

According to the Quran. the infamous career of Iblees begins with the creation of Adam AS. He was an angel of very high ranking among the angels of jannah. and he enjoyed a lot of respect. rank and prestige. He had the title of معلم الملکوت. which means the teacher of angels. Everything was going fine in his life until one day. out of the blue Allah says.

وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ إِنِّى جَاعِلٌۭ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةًۭ
Allah says to the angels. I have decided to create my representative on earth. what do you guys think?
And right at the onset. the angels have a problem with that!
قَالُوٓا۟ أَتَجْعَلُ فِيهَا مَن يُفْسِدُ فِيهَا وَيَسْفِكُ ٱلدِّمَآءَ وَنَحْنُ نُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِكَ وَنُقَدِّسُ لَكَ
Angels respond. Seriously? you want to create someone who is going to create problems on this earth and spill blood? Why would you want to do that? Why do you need them? So that you can be glorified and praised? If that's all you want. we are enough for that! You don't need more creation to do that. 
This is what the angles reply to Allah SWT. So we learn that right at the mention of the creation of adam. the angels start having a problem. Allah says.
قَالَ إِنِّىٓ أَعْلَمُ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ
I have knowledge of things that you don't know. So Allah decideds to go ahead with his plans and creates Adam.
فَإِذَا سَوَّيْتُهُۥ وَنَفَخْتُ فِيهِ مِن رُّوحِى
After he created Adam. he blew his soul into him. Allah blew his soul into him.  and then He granted him the knowledge of all his names.
وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا ثُمَّ عَرَضَهُمْ عَلَى ٱلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ فَقَالَ أَنۢبِـُٔونِى بِأَسْمَآءِ هَٓؤُلَآءِ إِن كُنتُمْ صَدِقِينَ
and then Allah asks the angels. now tell me the names of things. if you guys think you know everything. then tell me the names of these things.  they said
قَالُوا۟ سُبْحَنَكَ لَا عِلْمَ لَنَآ إِلَّا مَا عَلَّمْتَنَآ ۖ إِنَّكَ أَنتَ ٱلْعَلِيمُ ٱلْحَكِيمُ
We don't have any knowledge except that which you have given us. You are the all knowling and the all wise. So all the angels accept defeat and they accept Adam to be superior to them in knowledge. So then Allah commands all angels to do sajda to Adam.
وَإِذْ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟
and they all fell in sajda
إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ
except for Iblees. He refused to do Sajda.
أَبَىٰ وَٱسْتَكْبَرَ وَكَانَ مِنَ ٱلْكَفِرِينَ
He became arrogant and proud and became from among the disbelievers.
So Allah asked Iblees. why do you refuse to obey my command?
قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ ۖ
What stopped you from doing sajda when I commanded you to do so.
قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
He said I am better than him. You created me with fire and you created him with clay. 

Fire is better than clay

So Iblees challenged Allahs' command. his justice. and refused to do sajda. Now let's take a moment to analyze the argument presented by Iblees. His argument was.
قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
I am better than him? Why? Because you made me from fire and you made him from clay. Now let's analyze this argument for a second. Iblees said he is better than Adam. why? Because of the material that they both were made from. their bodies were made from. He argued that fire is better than clay. Now is that true?
Let's see. fire is bright. clay is dull. and bright is always better than dull. Fire illuminates. Clay does not. that which illuminates is always better than that which does not.  Fire is hot. clay is cold. and heat is better than cold. The flames of the fire rise up to the sky. the particles of clay always fall to the earth. the one that rises to the sky is always better than the one that falls to the earth. So what did Iblees do here? He used logic! He used deductive reasoning. which in Arabic is called Qiyaas. The word Qiyas literally means mesurement. he measured the properties of fire. against the properties of clay and reached the conclusion.  أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ I am better than him.

Now on the surface.  it does seem that the argument that Iblees presented . was absolutely accurate. But then that begs the question. why did Allah ask Iblees to prostrate to Adam in the first place? Why did he ask someone of a higer rank to prostrate before someone of a lower rank? That is an unjust command! The answer given to that is. because Allah commanded Iblees. and he should have obeyed. Yes! But why did Allah give an unjust command in the first place?

So is that what really happend? Did Allah give an unjust comamnd? Abosolutely not! (نعوذ باللہ من ذالک) Allah is beyond all injustice. He is indeed the MOST just! So then what did Iblees miss here? Well if you think about it. both fire and clay. they are both properties of the body. and they are both physical. arent they? They are both different types of bodies. made with different types of material. but they're both bodies and they're both physical.  But when did Allah ask the angels to prostrate to Adam?
فَإِذَا سَوَّيْتُهُۥ وَنَفَخْتُ فِيهِ مِن رُّوحِى
AFTER Allah blew his soul into Adam. ONLY after Allah blew his soul into Adam. He asked the angels to prostrate to him. And Allah's soul is greater than any body. Soul is spiritual. bodies are physical.  and spirituality is ALWAYS greater than physicality. no matter what material the body is made from. So Allah was ABSOLUTELY just in commanding the angels to prostrate to Adam. Because the command was not to prostrate to his body. the command was to prostrate to the soul that Allah blew into him. and the soul. that held the superior knowledge that Allah himself taught Adam AS. SubhanAllah.

This is the problem with Qiyaas. this is the problem with logical deduction. Ibless placed the content in his limited context. and then mixed in his own experiential biases into it.  Because as I said earlier . these angles. they all had their problems right at the mention of Adam's creation.
قَالُوٓا۟ أَتَجْعَلُ فِيهَا مَن يُفْسِدُ فِيهَا وَيَسْفِكُ ٱلدِّمَآءَ وَنَحْنُ نُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِكَ وَنُقَدِّسُ لَكَ
Do you want to create someone who will cause problems on earth and spill blood? We are enough for your glorification. we don't need someone else.
So right at the mention of Adam. angels developed an experiential bias. Why does Allah need man? Aren't we good enough for Him? What if he ends up loving him more than he loves us? What if he turns out to be more powerful than us? Will that take Allah's love away from me. Iblees had his fears. What if he gains my title? I am معلم الملکوت . what if Allah gives him my title and he gets ranked above me. what about my position? what about my power? my authority? So Iblees mixed his emotions. his experiential biases into his limited reasoning. and he strayed from the right path. And this is why we Sulemanis. we are not the people of Qiyaas. we are not people of measurement. we are people of obedience. We put our faith in the commands of our Imam. that were taken from the commands of Maulan Ali. that were takne from the commands of Rasul Allah (SAS). that were taken from Allah AWJ. Commands that were delivered to us through the duaat. issued on the tongues of our manaseeb. And we accept their command. even if they seem unjust at times. because as Allah said to the angels.
قَالَ إِنِّىٓ أَعْلَمُ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ
I know. what you do not know. We submit to the notion. that our elders know what we don't know. As children. my parents know what I don't know. if they're asking me to stop from doing something. or if they are asking me to do something. then they must have a reason for it that I don't understand. They have lived longer. they have seen the world more. I have not experienced even a fraction of life that they have experienced and lived through. therefore they know better.
We submit to the notion. that our teacher knows better. we are students. we only have access to what he is sharing with us right now. but my teacher speaks from his vast knowledge. He sees things which I cannot see at this point. so even if he tells me something I cannot fully comprehend right now. I must trust him. I must put my faith in him. and one day. as I progress through the levels of my education. InshaAllah I will understand.

And Shaytan. because he used Qiyaas. because he himself used deductive logical reasoning. he blows and whispers and prods us with the same logic. Why? Because he knows what got him into trouble with Allah. will also get us into trouble with Allah.
Why do you need to pray salaah. It's so stupid. doesn't even make any sense. If it really is so important. why just 5 times a day. why at these specific times. why not whenever you want? Why does Allah want you to not eat in Ramadan? If he's so loving. how come he is depriving you of food? Why do you need to spend in Allah's way? Why can't he provide himself if he's so powerful? 
And he instigates. he pokes. he prods. he creates frustration. distorts the intellect. binds with the ropes of arrogange. desire. temptations. and we fall pray to his mechanations and we give up Salaah. we give up fasting. we give up the various duties imposed upon us through Dayam Al-Islam.
There is ONLY one reason to follow Dayam Al-Islam. Understand this! . There is ONLY one good reason to follow the duties imposed upon us. and that reason is the same reason that was imposed upon the angels by Allah. OBEDIENCE! That is the ONLY one good enough reason for a Muslim. for a Momin to pray. to do salaah. to fast. to give zakaat. to do everything Allah commanded. ONLY because Allah has command. and his beloved prophet Muhammad Mustafa SAS has designed these rituals for us.  Because this concept of obedience alone. separated the angels from Iblees. And what happens when we walk on the same path that Iblees took?

قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا فَمَا يَكُونُ لَكَ أَن تَتَكَبَّرَ فِيهَا فَٱخْرُجْ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلصَّغِرِينَ
Descend from here . this janna is not a place for the arrogant and the proud. get out of here. you are from among the humiliated.

When we disobey Allah. we walk on the same path as Iblees. And if you think about it. knowing what we know about Allah's justice. we can't imagine. that Allah would reject Iblees for his disobedience. but accept us for ours. That would be injustice to Iblees. Allah is the most just. He will deal with us EXACTLY as he deal with Iblees. He'll say to us. EXACTLY what he said to Iblees
قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا فَمَا يَكُونُ لَكَ أَن تَتَكَبَّرَ فِيهَا فَٱخْرُجْ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلصَّغِرِينَ
Get out of my sight. you are arrogant. I told you pray. you disobeyed. I told you to fast. You disobeyed. I told you give zakaat. You disobeyed. I told you to do Hajj. You disobeyed. Get out of my sight. you are arrogant and my Jannah is not a place for the proud and the arrogant. What will we do then? You and I can come up with all the excuses in the world. you and I can come up with all the justifications. all the inductive and deductive reasoning in the world. it will not be accepted. Just as it was not accepted from Iblees. May Allah protect us all from being from among the followers of Iblees.

So now what do we do? We have done so much wrong. We have been so disobedient to Allah. So now what do we do? Are we doomed? Are we destined to never enter jannah again.?? ABSOLUTELY NOT.  ABSOLUTELY NOT.  How do we know that for sure? Studying this same story of Adam AS . further down the line we find that Adam too disobeys Allah. he eats from the forbidden tree. and because of Allah's immaculate justice. Adam and Hawwa. they too get the same treatment that Iblees received. they too are removed from Jannah. But there is a big difference. let's take a moment to understand that.
Difference between Iblees and Adam reaction

The word Iblees comes from the root word ابلس . which means to dispair. to give up hope. When Iblees angered Allah. he incurred Allah's wrath. He got pelted away by Allah. he was removed from Allah's mercy. but Iblees gave up hope in Allah. He gave up hope in Allah's mercy. He gave up hope in Allah's forgiveness.  and he believed himself to be doomed forever. BECAUSE he gave up hope. BECAUSEof his ابلس which means to give up hope. He did not return to Allah. and that's why He is called Iblees.

Adam on the other hand. even though he did the same thing. he disobeyed Allah. and he too incurred Allahs wrath. he too was thrown out of Jannah. Allah said to him as well.
وَقُلْنَا ٱهْبِطُوا۟ بَعْضُكُمْ لِبَعْضٍ عَدُوٌّۭ
Descend from here. you are now your own enemies.  Do you remember what words Allah used from Iblees when he kicked him out?
قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا
Descend from here.

The same word is used for both Adam and for Iblees by Allah. اھبطو . descend. fall! So they both got the exact same punishment for their disobedience. But as opposed to Iblees.  What did Adam AS say?
قَالاَ رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَآ أَنفُسَنَا وَإِن لَّمْ تَغْفِرْ لَنَا وَتَرْحَمْنَا لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْخَـسِرِينَ
Oh our master. we have wronged ourselves. And if you don't forgive us. if you don't have mercy on us. we will surely become from among the losers.
فَتَلَقَّىٰٓ آدَمُ مِن رَّبِّهِۦ كَلِمَتٍۢ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ
Adam received certain words from Allah through which he begged Allahs forgiveness. He repented. And as soon as he repented. Allah forgave Adam.
إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلتَّوَّابُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ
Certainly. No doubt. Allah is the most forgiving.

SubhanAllah. what a beautiful Ayah. I want us to appreciate something here. The ayah reads.

فَتَلَقَّىٰٓ آدَمُ مِن رَّبِّهِۦ كَلِمَتٍۢ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلتَّوَّابُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ

This is one single ayah. Allah does not even go to the next ayah to mention Adam's forgiveness. He could have stated Adam's repentence in one ayah. and then in the next ayah. he could have stated his forgiveness. and in the next ayah he could have stated that he is All forgiving. NO! This ayah is so beautiful. that Allahs immense forgiveness is fused in with Adam's repentence. Meaning as soon as Adam repented. that very instant Allah forgave him. The Quran didn't even break to the next ayah. SubhanAllah!
You know what that means? It means Allah is so eager for our repentence. that as soon as the thought of repentence enters our hearts. the rain of his mercy and his forgivness begins. The second we even think about repentence. Allahs spreads his arms for us. SubhanAllah.

So If I realize today. that I have disobeyed Allah. ALL i need to do. is turn to him in repentence. and before my apology even makes its way from my heart to my tongue. Allah says.
فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ ۚ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلتَّوَّابُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ
I forgive you my slave. I am the most forgiving.

Iblees gave up hope. Iblees chose arrogance. Adam AS did not give up hope. He chose the path of repentence. We are children of Adam AS. we are not children our Iblees. we are people of repentence. we are peole of hope. We are not people of despair.
Seek Allahs forgiveness. and before your words complete. see yourself forgiven. SubhanAllah!  We may have been disobedient until today. but with the Istiaaza. by saying اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم we can seek Allahs forgiveness. we can seek Allah's refuge from walking on the same path that Iblees walked on.

And with our استعاذہ  we can declare. that from this day forth. Ya Allah! We fall into your obedience. for the rest of our lives.

بارک لی ولکم فی القرآن کریم ! و آخر الدعوانا عن الحمد للہ رب العلمین


Revenge of Iblees

So this is how the career of Iblees begins. He gets rejected. He gets humiliated. and as his first order of business. he gets Adam and Hawwa (AS) kicked out of jannah. But then he doesn't stop at that. to avenge his humiliation. he makes it his life's mission. to ensure that none of their children ever make it back to Jannah. So he begins his recruitment process and starts drafting Shayateen in . Again. who are shayateen?. Shaytan is an adjective to descibe people who are far removed from the mercy of Allah. he creates an army of those and gets down to business. So this is Iblees and his army of Shayateen for you and I. This is how the story of Iblees begins.
I just wanted to give you a basic idea of how things started. we'll study Iblees's mission statement. his short term goals . his long term goals in detail. In fact we'll revisit this entire story in a LOT more details later on. but for now i just wanted to introduce you guys to our good friend Iblees.and his buddies. the shayateen.  pun intended.



 




Shaitan has many evil tactics and mechanations. and some of them are so cleverly crafted that we don't even realize that they care coming from Shaytan. I'll talk about some of the tactics of Shaytan. so that you become aware of these.
Of the tactics of shaytan is to cause us to forget and overlook. We forget the time of our prayers. we forget that time to give our zakaats. we forget to fulfill a good intention we may have made. we forget anything good that we are suppsed to do. that is one of the tactics of Shaytan. As the companion of Moosa (AS) says
وَمَآ أَنْسَىٰنِيهُ إِلَّا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ
It was shaytan that made me forget. So we seek refuge of Allah that when Shaytan uses this tactic on us. Allah's protection comes to our help and he prevents us from forgetting. because shaytan causes to forget


Of the tactics of Shaytan is to feel sleepy. is to feel lazy in the performance of good deeds. When its time for salaah and you start feeling sleepy. that is of the mechanation of Shaytan.

Of the tactics of Shaytan is get scared and terrified of more than that which is natural. THere is a natural fear . you see a snake or a scorpion. that is natural fear. but then there is an abnormal fear . an obsessive fear. you start thinking non stop about the past or the future tot he point where you go into depression. that kind of crazy fear is a mechanation of Shaytan. So seeking allahs' refuge from the shaytan makes you optimistic and hopeful.

Of the tactics of Shaytan believe or not. procrastination. Or prophet (SAS) said
التصویف من الشیطان
Procrastication is from Shaytan. delaying a good deed until later or tomorrow . procrastination. ahhh not now. maybe tomorrow.  maybe next week. that is from the shaytan. be it of this world or the after world. because Shaytan does not want anything good to happen to us. He does not want us to worship. he wants us to waste all our good deeds. So when we seek refuge from Allah. we become more productive in our lives. SubhanAllah. 

The main thing for which we seek refuge is the whisperings or the وسواس of shaytan. Shaytan whispers. what is the whispering of shaytan? The shaytan whispers means to put thoughts in our mind that would otherwise not come there.  to put thoughts in our mind that would otherwise not come. Shaytna does not have the power to force us to act. He does not put a gun to our heads and commands us. he cannot do that. Rather he entices us. he tempts us.
because Allah says in the Quran. On the day of judgment when the people he misguided will curse him and ask Allah to punish him and throw him in hell fire. Shaytaan will reply to them
وَمَا كَانَ لِىَ عَلَيْكُم مِّن سُلْطَنٍ
I had not power over you
إِلَّآ أَن دَعَوْتُكُمْ فَٱسْتَجَبْتُمْ لِى ۖ
I merely called you . you were the ones who answered my call
فَلَا تَلُومُونِى وَلُومُوٓا۟ أَنفُسَكُم ۖ
Therefore do not curse me on this day. curse your own souls.
مَّآ أَنَا۠ بِمُصْرِخِكُمْ وَمَآ أَنتُم بِمُصْرِخِىَّ
I had no control over your actions . only you had control over your actions

Sometimes we are sitting quietly. and out of no where a vulgur thought comes in our minds. ot of no where at all. Suddently this desire to do something that would be diobedient to Allah. this is the whisper of Shaytan.


Another one is when you are angry. Shaytan increases anger to the point where our veins are about to pop out. When you are very angry. when you're furious. that is from the tactic from Shaytan

We also say istiaaza. when we enter the restroom. why? Because shayateen are filthy creatures. and they love to congregate in places of filth. so they love to be in places of najasah. and restroom is the place of najasah. thats why when we enter the restroom we say

اعوذ باللہ من الرجس نجس خبیث المخبث الشیطان الرجیم
So we seek allah's refuge before we enter the restroomm.


we seek refuge in allah when we are frightened. Rasul Allah (SAS) taught his family that when they are frightened they should recite
بسم اللہ اعوذ بکلمات اللہ التامۃ من غضبہ و عقابہ و شر عبادہ و من ھمزات الشیاطین و ان یحضرون
In other words it is a longer version of the istiaaza.  because being terrified is from the tactics of shaytan. Allah mentions in the Quran

إِنَّمَا ذَلِكُمُ ٱلشَّيْطَنُ يُخَوِّفُ أَوْلِيَآءَهُۥ فَلَا تَخَافُوهُمْ وَخَافُونِ إِن كُنتُم مُّؤْمِنِينَ
Indeed it is the shaytaan that frightens the friends of Allah. Do not fear him and fear me if you are a believer
So when we say Aozubillah it removes the unnatural fear within us and makes us brave.

Also we seek refuge in Allah when we are distracted in the salaah. if we can't concentrate. if we can't focus. we say aoozubillahi
We seek refuge in Allah when we go to a new place. from the evils that lurk there
We even seek refuge when we are inclined to act upon an evil though or an evil desire. Because as soon as the desire rises. Shaytaan gets there to put fuel on fire. therefore we seek refuge of Allah. and allah clearly states for us in the quran
وَإِمَّا يَنزَغَنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ نَزْغٌۭ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ ۚ إِنَّهُۥ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ
If shaytan urges you towards an evil. then seek refuge in allah because all is samee Alaleem
and finally we seek refuge of allah under any and all circumstances. even for no reason at all. We can say aozu billah even right now. because we don't have to have a reason to state this zikr. we can turn to allah at any time for his protection and refuge.









 

Now let's take a deeper dive into the استعاذہ ..... the call for protection of Allah FROM the cursed Shaytan... أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم which is also a prayer... ... This ayah... is commonly translated as "I seek refuge of Allah from the cursed Shaitaan"... But linguists say this is not the best translation.....  and InshaAllah we'll look at why they say that ..... and why they consider this is a poor or weak translation... But to get started... the first thing you must understand about this ayah is that it has too parts... or it deals with two entities....

There is the one we are seeking protection OF... and there is the one we are seeking protection FROM.... This is the first very distinction we need to make... We are running FROM someone... and we are running TO someone.... we need protection OF someone... and we need protection FROM someone.... So the first thing to notice is that there is a pair here.....  There are two questions here that need to be answered.... Who are you seeking protection from? and whose protection or refuge are you seeking?

Now the one whose protection you are seeking... the term for that is المستعاذُ بہ.... means the one whose protection you are seeking OF.. and that we know is Allah.... we are seeking protection of Allah... ... And the one you're trying to seek protection FROM... the one you're trying to escape from is  المستعاذُ منہ. .... who we know is Shytaan.... So Allah is المستعاذُ بہ and Shaytan is المستعاذُ منہ. So "bihi" and "minhu"... If we carefully observe the استعاذہ it contains both......

أعوذ ب اللہ من الشیطان الرجیم

So if you look at the diagram I sent... you can see it contains the بہ as well as the منہ. The ب is associated with Allah... and the من is associated with Shaytaan... Do you understand?

Now why is this interesting to know? It's interesting.... because in explanation of these two terms....... the المستعاذُ بہ and the المستعاذُ منہ  , we find two separate surahs in the Quran.... One dedicated essentially to المستعاذُ بہ and the other dedicated essentially to the المستعاذُ منہ. These two surahs are called the المُعَوِّذَتَینِ ...... which literally means the two refuges...  and these are Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas....

The Istiaaza (أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم) is basically the essence or the summary of these 2 surahs... So if we fully understand the meanings of these 2 surahs... we can fully understand the meaning of the استعاذہ ...

So the first thing I want to do .... is a linguistic analysis of this surah with you.. I want to show you the beautiful symmetry and perfection that exists in these two surahs...  and to highlight the beauty and the miracle of this amazing book.. We went over a basic definition of the word عاذ in the previous sessions... but inshaAllah we'll study this word in a lot more detail.... We'll compare the two surahs to see what connection they have with each other....... and then what connection they have with the Fateha.... We'll also look at its historical context....... we'll look at the reasons and circumstances under which these two surahs were revealed ..... And then finally we'll look at how the teachings and lessons from this surah can help us in our day to day lives...

First let's just understand the meaning of these surahs from a generic translation...

Comparison of Surah Falaq and Surah Naas

So we can see that both Surahs have the same theme.... it is seeking the protection OF Allah... FROM Shaytan... So both Surah's are المستعاذُ بہ as well as المستعاذُ منہ....
However, if you notice.... Surah AlNaas is essentially about المستعاذُ بہ ... seeking protection of Allah... and Surah AlFalaq is more about المستعاذُ منہ  seeking protection from Shaytaan.... Because if you study Surah AlNaas you can see that the protection OF Allah is mention a LOT more ..... whereas in Surah AlFalaq.... the protection FROM Shaytan is mentioned a lot more...

So let's take a look at that... In Surah AlNaas... we see that Allah is called upon 3 times... 

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
Protection OF Allah is sought 3 times... رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ ..... but the protection from shaytan.... is mentioned once
مِن شَرِّ ٱلْوَسْوَاسِ ٱلْخَنَّاسِ
From the evil of the whispering of Shaytan.... The remaining ayats that follow.... are simply the description and details of وسواس الخناس  .... Its simply an explanation of how shaytan whispers into the hearts of men...
ٱلَّذِى يُوَسْوِسُ فِى صُدُورِ ٱلنَّاسِ مِنَ ٱلْجِنَّةِ وَٱلنَّاسِ
The one who whispers into the chest of mankind... whether it is from the jinn or from the men... But it is still talking about one thing... the evil whispering of Shaytan... So you see... In Surah AlNaas.... Allah is called upon for protection 3 times.....  and protection FROM Shaytan is mentioned once... So this is primarly focused towards... المستعاذُ بہ

Now Surah AlFalqa on the contrary is more focused on المستعاذُ منہ ..... Because in this Surah.... we find that Allah is called upon just once...
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلْفَلَقِ
That's it... In all the remaining Ayats... the Surah talks about seeking protection FROM the various evils....
مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ .... وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ...  وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ..... وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ
So we see that in this Surah...... Allah is called upon just once... and refuge and protection FROM the evils are sought three times.... the first one... مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ is only the mention of the existence of evil in general... Protect me from all evil that was created.... It's all inclusive...  But the specific evils.... FROM which protection is being sough are three....
وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ...  وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ..... وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ
These are the 3 specific protections that the Surah seeks protection FROM.... And therfore we see that surah AlFalqa is primarly  المستعاذُ منہ

So in Surah AlNaas (المستعاذُ منہ).. Allah is mentioned 3 times and the specific evil of Shaytan's whispering is mentioned once...  In Surah Falaq which is (المستعاذُ منہ) Allah is mentioned once and the protection of Allah from three specific evils are mentioned.. So there is this beautiful symmetry between these 2 surahs....
 

There are also some more interesting connections between the two surahs... Surah Falaq deals with the types of problems that afflict a human being.... that are not a product of his own work.. in other words he has no control over them...

وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ
the evil of the dark night... that's not under our control
وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ
The evil of those who engage in sorcery and black magic... again something that's not under our control
وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ
The evil of the one who is acting out of jealousy against us...  ... that too is not under our control...

None of these evils that are mentioned.... are actually under our control... We are the helpless victims of all these evils... right? Evil of the dark night.... evil of sorcerers... and evil of the one acting out of jealousy... all of these we have no control over.... these evils are being done TO us....  And because we are the victims of these evils.... that are being done to us by someone.... or something else... we are not accountable for these... There is no sin against us... You understand?

Now in contrast to this... Surah AlNaas deals with actions of the human beings that we actually are accountable for...  What are we seeking refuge from in Surah AlNaas? مِن شَرِّ ٱلْوَسْوَاسِ ٱلْخَنَّاسِ ... we are seeking refuge from the evil of the whisperings of Shaytan... from his  وسوسۃ ....... And when Shaytan does his  وسوسۃ inside us... what do we do? we engage in an evil act..... but that evil act that we engage in...... Are we accountable for it before Allah? Or can we just say..... oh no it wasn't my fault it was a وسوسۃ from shaytan? No! We are actually accountable for it! We are responsible for it....

In other words what we are seeking protection from in Surah Naas is something we will have to answer for.... if we mess up... But in surah falaq..... the afflictions that are coming upon us are beyond our control...we are victimized by them.... But in both cases.... the only one who can help us..... is Allah (AWJ) ...
And that's why..... we see MORE desperation in surah Naas ... because if we end up doing an evil act based on the وسوسۃ of the shytan... if we fall victim to his whisperings... what will we end up doing?  we will end up damaging our Eman... That's why in Surah AlNaas.... Allah is called upon multiple times..

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ

So it is said....
فا الأولیٰ فی شَرِّ المصائب ؛ وَ الثَّانِیَ فی شَرِّ المعَائِب
The first deals with the evils of afflictions that will come upon us that are out of your control... but the second has to do with the evils that we ourselves may commit... Sins that we are answerable for... Therefore the second one requires more of a seeking of refuge... So when we say
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
and this actually..... from a grammatical stand point ... is what's called a  بَدَلْ in Arabic... meaning these three ayaats of Surah AlNaas.... would be similar to saying...

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بمَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بأِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
So its like (قل اعوذُ ب) is in parenthesis.... and it is being applied to all three ayats... Because we are far more desperate in losing our Eman because of the وسوسۃ of shaytaan. That's a far bigger danger ... Even though the dangers mentioned in surah falaq are pretty huge dangers... the dangers of the night... the danger of sorcerers and the one who is jealous... those are serious dangers as well... but when these happen we are not accountable... the people doing those evils are accountable... but when we ACT upon the وسوسۃ of shaytan.. we are responsible for that action... and therefore accountable before Allah for that action... and that makes it a greater and a much more personal danger to us! You understand?

Then we find this remarkably eloquent sequencing inside this surah falaq... Allah transitions in this surah from the general to the specific.... from the widely scoped.... to the narrow scoped..... and gets more and more specific.... let's see how...
