We started with the Istiaaza. اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم. We looked into the meaning of each of these words individually.  and then moved on to the two surahs. Surah AlFalaq and Surah AlNaas. And why did we do that? Because as learnt earlier. that Surah AlFateha is the mother of Quran. Umm AlQuran. Meaning it is the essence or the gist of the entire Quran. Surah AlFateha is like the summary . or index of the Quran . And the remainder of the Quran is a running commentary on the surah. You know how you have indexes in a book that just outline the chapters and topics. They gives you the summary of what is in the book. But when you need to understand the details. you have to actually turn to the chapter itself. It's the same thing here.
These 7 ayats of AlFateha. They are the index. and their explanations exist in the remaining Quan. So to understand what these ayats mean. we will need to study these other surahs that provide us with an explanation of these ayats.

Now AlFateha starts with the Basmallah. بسم اللہ الرحمن الرحیم .  But before we get to that. we are started studying the Istiaaza. because Allah commanded us.

فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ

Before you begin reciting the Quran. Seek refuge of Allah from the cursed Shaytan.  So we started with the Istiaaza which is : أعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم

So now let's quickly go over the terms to make sure you guys understand.  First of all the difference between Shaytan and Iblees. Because they both have been used in the Quran.
So we said Shaytan is a generic label. it is adjective that can be applied to anyone who fits the bills? There isn't a person named "Shaytan". Just like there is not a person named "Arrogant". Anyone who acts in an arrogant manner is called what? Arrogant! It's an adjective. Similarly there is no one named "Shaytan". Shaytan means the one who is far removed from the mercy of Allah. So anyone who acts in a manner that gets him far removed from Allah is called what? Shaytan. So anyone can be labeled as Shaytan if they act in a specific manner. It can be applied to human beings as well as jinns. Is that clear?

Iblees however is the name of an entity. He is the angel that disobeyed the command of Allah. and refused to prostrate before Adam. He is one specific entity called Iblees.

So that's the primary difference between the two. Then to understand the details of Istiaaza. we started studying Surah AlFalaq. So let's do a quick revision of that just to make sure you got the gist of it.

So the Surah begins with قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلْفَلَقِ Say! I am surrendering myself for protection to the master of Al-Falaq. 

Falaqa means. when something rips open. and something else come out. So if you have a bag of patator chips. or a bag of candy. When you apply pressure at the bottom. the top of the bag rips open. and the candy comes out.  that's Falaqa.
You see how I do this linguistic analysis of words, right? I hope you can understand why it is so important. Because it really helps us understand the message and meaning of the ayats. Because otherwise how is this ayah generally translated? Say I seek refuge from the master of daybreak. That's how it is translated. But that means what? That translation actually means nothing to me. So he is the master of daybreak. What's for me to appreciate in that? That he brings the day? Well he brings the night too. He brings the 4 seasons one after the other too. So what's so special about that? I would have no different appreciation for this ayah. had he said قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلشجر. or قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ الفاحۃI seek refuge of the master of the apple.
But when we understand what the implications of the word Falaq are. that it is how allah creates . by ripping through things to bring forth new things. Now I can truly appreciate the remaining ayats in the Quran because I can now connect it with the meaning of the word Falaq.
So this surah talks about evils. evils are similar to darkness. Allah is the master of Falaq. which means He rips through the darkness and brings forth the day. Similarly if I surrender myself to his protection. He will RIP and TEAR through the darkness of these evils and being ease and comfort for me. And you see how when seomething rips through it happens immediately. Doesn't take a lot of time. It implies hard and fast. right? When you press that bag of chips hard. the bag will rip open and those chips will come flying out. right? Just like that. Allah. who is Rabb AlFalaq can take me out of the darkness of these evils. right away. I can now have a true appreciation of this surah. just by understanding the meaning of the word Falaq. You understand?


Aoozu: means I willingly surrender. I willingly and desperately cling to. Who do I surrender to? Who do I cling to? The master of Falaq. Now when do we desperately seek protection? When we are being what? attacked! But this is not just surrendering. it is desperately surrending. And desperation comes from two things.  (1) When you understand the power of your enemy. (2) and when you unerstand your own helplessness against the enemy. That's what causes desperation.
And then we said that linguistically. the word Ao'zu suggests seeking spiritual help from a diety. It is not physical help. and it is not from human beings. That's all captured by the word Ao'zu.

Then there is
Qul: It has two things. Call for submission. Call for obedience.  By declaring. we are crushing our ego. we are openly accepting and admitting our weakness. our need for Allah's protection. So humility first.
And then also in this declaration. there is the call for obedience to Allah's command.  If one is disobedient to allah they have no right to ask Allah's protection. Even before they seek His protection. they need to come in his obedience

مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ
From all the evil of what was created
The word Sharr. it means something that is harmful. something that will always cause harm. Everything that is created. has the potential of harm in it. A knife is a great tool. It can be used to cut fruits and vegetables. But then it can also be used to stab someone. cut someone's throat. So even though knife is a great tool. It has the potential of causing harm. I cannot say the one who invented the knife is evil.
This same thing applies to all of Allah's creation. Allah did not create evil. Freedom of choice in human beings is what created evil. So we surrender ourselves to Allah's protection FROM the potential and active evil of all creation.

وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ
From the evil of the dark night when things become invisible. So we surrender ourselves to the protection of Rabb AlFalaq from the evil of times when things become confusing. When situations and circustances begin clouding our judgments. When we can no longer distinguish between who are friends and enemies are. Protection from the evil of enemies who are hiding in dark shadows. This can mean the evil spirits which we'll talk about in the next surah. but also dark emotions of people that we come in contact with.  greed. arrogance. pride. pettiness. All these emotion can be very harmful. and they are completely invisible to us. Because we don't know the person standing before us with a big smile on his face. could be holding what negative emotion against us. So in this ayah we seek protection from all of that which is invisible.


وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ
From the evil of women who blow on knots. This is a specific reference to the daughters of Labed Ibn Asim. who assisted him in casting spells on Rasul Allah (SAS). But then there are other spells that act as magic which we talked about last time. Gossip. back biting. things that can poison our minds against someone. And we remain completely unaware of the psychological changes that are taking place within us. not because of something we experienced. But because of something that was said to us by a gossiper.  That's the exact behavior pattern of the one who is a victim of black magic. Someone else puts the spell on them. but they behave as if they are the ones with the problems. They start having psychological and physiological reactions. And then when we become victims of this evil. we end up becoming the hands of the gossiper. He becomes our silent master. and we end up becoming his minion. We end up doing his dirty work for him. and WE end up getting punished. no the one who actualy cast the spell. So this is indeed a GREAT evil. And that's why Islam closed the door on gossip and backbiting.
وَلَا تُطِعْ كُلَّ حَلَّافٍۢ مَّهِينٍ. هَمَّازٍۢ مَّشَّآءٍۭ بِنَمِيمٍۢ
And do not obey every worthless habitual swearer. And scorner, who goes about spreading malicious gossip
May Allah protect us from this evil. Not only protect us FROM this evil. but also from committing this evil to others.



وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ
Finally from the evil of the jealous. when he is acting out his jealousy. So Allah boils down the root of all evil to Hasad. Jealousy. But what's interesting to note here is that the protection that we seek. is not from the jealousy itself. Rather from the one who is ACTING OUT on his jealousy. Because we as human beings will feel jealous. It's a negative emotion. but as humans we can't say that we will never feel jealous. So being jealous is one thing. but how we navigate that jealousy is an entirely different thing. So the evil we seek protection is actually from the jealous WHEN he is acting out his jealousy. Because that is when he will actually cause the harm.
So Allah in this Surah highlihgts jealousy to be the root of all these evils. The one who is acting out his jealousy.وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ.  Because what will he do? He will cast spells. whether that be black magic. or spread roumors and gossip. and poison our minds against others. Therefore مِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ.  And he will execute that hidden emotion in a manner that is not visible. He will attack us while keeping us in darkness. Therefore وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ. And since we can't keep track of everyone and every single instance when we are being attacked by evil. Therefore. مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ

And who is the one who can protect us from all these evils? Who can rip and tear through all these evils and save us? Rabb AlFalaq. Therefore. قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلْفَلَقِ


So this is why this Surah is named Falaq because it ties in with every single ayah. And it ties in not just as protection from Allah for us as victims of these evils. But also as a threat and a warning to us. IF we choose to commit these evils ourselves.  Because As Rasul Allah (SAS) stated. Falaq is also the name.  of one of the doors of hell.
بابٌ فی النَّار، اِذاَ فُتِحَت سُیِّرَت جھنَّم
It is a door in hell. when it tears open. the fire within gets excites and rips and rushes out through it.  He also said it is a prison in hell for tyrants and arrogant people.
ھُوَ سِجنٌ فی جھنم، یُحبَثُ فیہِ الجبَّارُون و المتکبرون ۔۔
And it is SO incredibly bad. that even hell fire itself seeks Allahs protection from it
و اِنَّ جھنَّمَ تَتَعَوَّذُ بِی اللہ مِنہُ




























 

Comparison of Falaq & Naas
Before we begin Surah AlNaas. Let's just go over some comparisons between the two surahs. We've already discussed these earlier. So I'll quickly pass over them.

We saw in Surah AlFalaq. that its primary focus was on protection FROM evil. Because protection of Allah is mentioned once once. قل اعوذ برب الفلق  . But protection FROM specific evils was mentioned 3 times.
وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ
ومِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ
وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ

So it was primarily a Surah dedicated to seeking protection FROM Evil. مستعاذ منہ

In Surah AlNaas on the other hand. we see that its primary focus is on protection OF Allah. Because in this surah. protection of Allah is mentioned 3 times. 
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
and protection FROM a specific evil is mentioned just once.
مِن شَرِّ ٱلْوَسْوَاسِ ٱلْخَنَّاسِ
From the evil of the whisperings of Shaytan.  The remaining ayaats are just the explanation of that central evil. the evil of waswasa.
ٱلَّذِى يُوَسْوِسُ فِى صُدُورِ ٱلنَّاسِ مِنَ ٱلْجِنَّةِ وَٱلنَّاسِ
The one who whispers in the hearts of people. whether they are from the jinn or human beings. That is just the explanation of the actual evil. which is the whispering of Shaytan.

Is this symmetry and difference between the two surahs clear?

Now. Another interesting thing about these surahs is that in Surah AlFalaq. the protection we are seeking is physical in nature.
وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ. وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ. وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ
The effects of these evil affect us physically. Whereas in Surah AlNaas. the protection we are seeking is spiritual. We are asking protection for our soul. from waswasa of shaytaan.

Also, the evils mentioned in Surah AlFalaq are outside our control. We are helpless victims of those crimes.  But the evil mentioned in Surah AlNaas is something that we will guilty of. Because when the shaytan does waswasa to us. we will end up acting upon it and committing an evil. Therefore we will be liable and accountable for that action. The liability in the previous surahs was on the criminals. but the liability in Surah AlNaas is entirely on us . We will be accountable for the action that we commit based on Shaytan's waswasa. Because as the Quran says.  On the day of judgment Shaitan is not going to take responsibility. He will say to us
وَمَا كَانَ لِىَ عَلَيْكُم مِّن سُلْطَنٍ
Don't blame me. I had no power or control over you. I did not hold a gun to your head.
إِلَّآ أَن دَعَوْتُكُمْ فَٱسْتَجَبْتُمْ لِى
I just invited you. called you to that evil. and it was YOU who responded to it.
فَلَا تَلُومُونِى وَلُومُوٓا۟ أَنفُسَكُم
Therefore do not curse at me today. Curse at your own soul. Because it was all your doing.

I didn't do anything.  I just suggested. You responded. I just sent you the email.  it was you who clicked on it.  I just sent you the link to that filthy site. you were the one who went to it.  I just made the call.  you are the one who picked it up.  I just sent you the address. you're the one who drove there.  All I did was give you an invitation.  that's all. The one acting on it was all you! You are the one that is alone responsible for your acts.

So the evils addressed in this surah. in Surah AlNaas. we are liable for it. We will be held accountable for it on the day of judgment.

The previous surah. AlFalaq. it talks about the harms of this duniya.  But the waswasa of shaytan harms our deen. our akhira. Which is more precious? Which has to be guareded more? Of course our deen needs to be guarded more. So then between the two surahs. which one do we MORE desperately need to seek protection?  Surah AlNaas.
So you see. that's why in this surah we ask for Allahs protection lot more. than in surah falaq. In Surah Falaq we just called upon him once.
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلْفَلَقِ
But in naas. we are calling upon Allah to protect our deen over and over again. 3 tims as much. 
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
Because when shaytan makes waswasa in OUR eman. When he is putting doubts in it . He is puttin jealously in it.  putting greed in it.  What is it attacking? He is attacking our faith. our taqwa. His waswasa can corrupt all of those things. therefore we ask for allahs protection a lot more in this surah.
 


we already talked about Qul. it is in obedience to allah's command. and the lesson here is that you cannot enter allahs protection unless you are obedient to him. If one is disobedient to allah they have no right to ask allahs protection. they need to come in allahs obedience first
Qul is a declaration. you have to declare that you are seeking refuge . you have to get your ego out of the way and admit that you need help. you need allahs' protection. Allah did not say
استعیذ برب الناس
Seek protection from the master of people. he didn't say that. because that could be done secretly. You could secretly seek allahs refuge. but allah says
قل اعوذ برب الناس
meaning openly declare allahs' need . say it out loud. when you say it out loud . youv've slammed your ego and you've humbled yourself before Allah saying I can't protect myself. you can protect me. and this is part of the lesson here. . part of the lesson is humility before Allah swt. and a crusing of ones own nafs

Why Rabb AlNaas?
Now why does Allah call himself Rabb AlNaas in this Surah? And what's the relation of Rabb AlNaas with the remaining ayats? We understand now why he called himself Rabb AlFalaq in the previous surah. Because it had to do with tearing through. and ripping through all the evils mentioned in it. That's why Allah called himself Rabb AlFalaq.
Now why does Allah call himself Rabb AlNaas? The word Naas means people. all of mankind. Notice he did not say Rabb AlMomineen. Rabb AlSulemani. Rabb AlSunni. Rabb AlShia. He did not identify himself as the master of one specific group. He identified himself as Rabb AlNaas. The master of all mankind. So that's the first thing to appreciate.

But then he could have referred to his mastery over many other things. Like even in so many places in the Quran he associates his mastery and lordship over other creations.
رب السماوات والارض
Master of the skies and the earth.
رب العالمین
Master of the worlds.

So why in this Surah did He extend his mastery.  his lordship. specifically towards peopel (naas)?
It is because it is only people. it is only mankind. that need protection of Allah in this surah. The skies and earth dont need protection from shaytan. The worlds and universes don't need protection from Shaytan. Who needs protection from shaytan and his whispering? It is people. So allah extended his mastery his lordship towards people.  So It is.  as if it is being said that I seek Allah's protection from the evil of the one.  who is the worst enemy of all mankind. And I seek protection with the master of mankind.  the one who has authority over them.  and all of their affairs.


Why is Naas repeated every time?

Now a bit of linguistic and grammatical analysis of these ayats.

In this surah. Allahs asked us to seek protection of Allah.  using 3 of his names.
رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
And then notice. that the word naas is mentioned 3 times. He didn't have to do isn't it? From a grammatical point the word Naas is redundant.
If I say. Nadia is a girl. Nadia is my friend. Nadia attends my sessions regularly.  Is that the best way to speak? No! What can I say instead? Nadia is a girl. She is my friend. She attends my sessions regularly. Once I've said Naida. I don't need to repeat it again and again. I could just use a pronoun. right?
So Allah could have done the same thing. Linguistically. he could have said
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ; مَلِکِھِم، اِلٰہِھِم
He could have used a pronoun. But allah used Naas specifically with each ayah. seems redundant! So now why is that?

Let's first talk about a psychological progression. A child for example. You know for a child. one of the first realization a child has is that his needs are taken care of by his parents. Someone who has control over them. someone who takes care of their tarbiyah (their training). As a child. when you have a need.  you go to your parents. That's why parents are also called Rabb in Arabic. becuase they do Tarbiyyah or training of the child. So in that sense they have mastery over the child. Just like when a slave has a need.  he goes to his master.  thats captured in the word Rabb

But then sometimes.  there is a problem that your parent can't take care of. The one who has mastery over you cannot take care of that problem. It is a problem bigger than that. Then you know who you go to? You go to the government. you go to the sovereign. you go to the king.  you go to the Malik. You make that next progression.

But then you have such a big problem that your rabb cannot solve it. Your malik cannot solve. even your king, your government cannot solve it. No one on earth can solve it. Where do people turn to when they have that kind of a need? Where do people turn to then? Ilah AnNaas! You can only ask god for help now. So these are the three psychological progressions in these ayats.

But Allah is teaching us something very unique here. He's teaching us that if you have a problem. no matter what age you are. You always ONLY turn to allah. Because your rabb is Allah. Your king is Allah. and your Ilah is Allah. Always turn to Allah from the very beginning.  and this realization is the height of intellectual progression. The height of intellectual progression.  is that you understand that from your most BASIC needs.  to your GREATEST needs. you turn for everything to allah.  He is مسبب الاسباب . He will create the causes and sources for me through parents. teachers. jobs. bosses. kings. But in the end He is the one doing everything for me. Nothing can. and nothing will happen without his command. Therefore for every single one of  my needs I must turn to him alone .
فھو ربی و ملکی و الہی Because he is my master. He is my king. and He is my god. That's why the word Naas is mentioned specifically with every single ayah.

Your parents can be your Rabb. Your teachers can be your Rabb. But I am your true Rabb. So before you submit yourself to the proection of your parents. before you submit yourself to the protection of your teachers. submit yourself to MY protection. because I am رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ. I am the king of all mankind.  If I don't choose to protect you. your parents can't protect you. your teachers can't protect you.
If you have a need that those having mastery overy you can't solve. and you need to go to the next level. be it the boss of your company. the principal of your school. the state ministred. the president of a country. Seek MY protection first. Because even though I have placed them in positions of authority.  I am مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ. I am the king of all mankind.
And finally if you have a need.  that neither those having mastery over you. nor the people in power and authority can solve. then surrender to my protection. becuase I am الہ الناس . the god of all mankind. That's why we see the word Naas mentioned with every single ayah.

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ

How the names of Allah progresses


We see that the names of Allah in this Surah progress from Rabb to Malik to Ilah.  So what's the connection between these three words? To understand that. let's look at the meanings of these words.

Let's start with the word Rabb. رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ. Rabb is a very comprehensive word. and InshaAllah we'll study the word Rabb in GREAT detail when we study the ayah الحمد للہ رب العلمین . But for now. just understand that the word Rabb means owner. And ownership implies value. And value implies love.  So Rabb means the one who owns something that he loves. and because he loves it. he finds it valuable. Value does not necessarily mean monetary value. For example if my daughter owns a doll that she loves. then because she loves it. she values it. So in that case she is the Rabb of that doll. You understand? The doll itself could be very cheap. in the monetory sense. But because she loves it. that's why she values it. and that makes her the Rabb. So Rabb means the one who owns something that he/she loves and considers valuable!
Now this kind of ownership. automatically contains certain implications. When someone owns soemthing they love and consider valuable. they will take care of it. they will be concerned about it. they will always try to set it straight. So for example. if you own a nice phone. and you really value it. you will always take care of it. you will be concerned about it. You will not just leave it anywhere. you'll try to keep it close to you. And when you can't.  you'll make sure you keep it safe.  So if there are young children in the house, you'll make sure you keep it in a place so that they don't damage it. You'll always protect it. You'll get a nice protective cover for it.  to protect it from damages. You'll you'll make sure you get a case that looks beautiful. elegant. in order to enhance the beauty of the phone. You'll make it stand out. right? You'll also set it straight when there is a problem. So if it gets dirty. you'll wipe it clean. If something is damaged. you'll try to get it fixed.  So all of this is included in the meaning of the word Rabb.

So you can see. that the word Rabb can be used in the worldly sense. Even though Allah is the ultimate Rabb. but the word Rabb can be used in the worldly sense as well. Just because the definition of the word Rabb can apply to wordly relationships. Let's look at the definition of the word Rabb again in a worldly sense.  Rabb is the one who owns something that he loves and consideres valuable. His ownership includes care and concern for the property. and it also includes setting it straight when necessary.
Now if you think about it. These attributes. of love, care, concern and setting straight. these are all attributes of training. Tarbiyyah. which means Training and Nurturing.  A Rabb is someone who trains and nurtures. You understand?
That's why parents are called Rabb. Why? Because they have ownership over you. They have Rububiyyah over you.  Let's say you're in a group and you get lost. When they try to find your parents what will they announce? . Who does this child BELONG to.  In other words who has OWNERSHIP over this child? You understand? And because your parents have ownership. which means they love you and consider you valuable (atleast until you become a teenager). They take care of you. they're concerned for you. they set you straight meaning they correct you when you go wrong. All elements of Tarbiyah and therefore that qualifies them for the word Rabb.

So Allah is Rabb AlNaas. He is the owner of mankind. Why? Because he loves them and He considers them valuable.And because of that He takes care of them. He is always concerned about them. And He tries to set them straight when they stray

Now what's مَلِک ? The word مَلِک means king. A king is someone who has authority over you. Is it possible for somone to be an owner but not have complete authority? Sure! I own a car. but I do not have complete authority over it. I cannot drive it on the side walk or drive through when the light is red. Even though I own it. I do not have complete authority over it.
But Allah is not just Rabb. He is not just owner. He is also Malik. He has COMPLETE authority over his property. He can do whatever He wants. when He wants to.

So while Rabb is the ownership of allah. مَلِک goes a step further to describe the authority of allah. So what was missing in Rabb is captured in مَلِک . and in the final one the combination of both is used. The ONLY one who can have both . ownership and authority. both at the same time is Ilah. So the third one is almost a result of the previous two.  This is called عطف بیان in arabic . means explaining the first two with the third. Because Allah is  رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ and becahse he is مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ. both at the same time. The natural conclusion of those two realities is what? That he is إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ . Because Ilah is the only one who can be رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ and مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ at the same time. And that is Allah AWJ

So there is a physchological progression when it comes to Naas or people. We humans. for our needs. we first turn to our Rabb. They can be teachers, parents, uncles, aunts, grand parents, bosses. But then when we have a need that the Rabb cannot fulfill. We turn to the Malik. someone in authority. like a city or state official or the king or president of a country. And when they too cannot fulfill our needs. we finally turn to the Ilaah. who can take care of ALL our needs.

So there is this psychological progression. but then there is also this literary progression that takes place in the names used for Allah. Starts with the one who has ownership رب الناس . progresses to the one with ultimate authority . مَلِکِ الناس . and then finally concludes in the sum of those two attributes. which is الہ الناس . The god or diety of people. Meaning Why is He Ilah AlNaas? Because he is Rabb AlNaas and Malik AlNaas. We'll look at the word Ilah in much detail later on InshaAllah!
 

From General To Specific

Now I want to show you something really amazing. Check this out. From a literary point. If we analyze these first 3 ayats. or rather the mentioned names of Allah. رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ .   we'll see that they progress from more to less. From general to specific. Now what does that mean? Let's take a look.

Let's start with the word Rabb. رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ. Who is Rabb again? The one who has ownership. and who loves and values that which he owns. He cares for it. He is concerned about it. and he sets it straight.  Now based on that definition. many people in your life could be called Rabb? . Isn't it? . Your parents. your grand parents.  your uncles.  your aunts.  your siblings.  your friends . Your teachers. your bosses. your doctor? They all could be labeled Rabb. Right? Becaues they have some ownership over you . they care for you. they are concerned for you and they set you straight. So you can have many  أرباب. which is the plural for Rabb. correct?

But for any society or any country.  how many kings can there be? How many ultimate soverigns can you have for one country? Only one!
In any society.  you can have multiple ارباب in the worldly sense.  but you will only have one king. one president. Right? But then.  if you take the entire world into consideration. If you take all the countries in the world. do they each have a king or a president or a soverign body? They do! So even though you will only have ONE king. one soverign body for one country. or one society. but overall.  as a whole.  there can be multiple kings. Yes?

But as you go further. and you reach the name Ilah. How many Ilah can you have? across the board?. You can have only one Ilah.  The word Ilah can never be taken in a worldly sense. Rabb you can take in a worldly sense. You can say رب البیت ، owner of the house. رب الولد. owner of a child.  You can also take مَلِک in a worldly sense. For example the king of Saudi Arabia. Malik Salman Ibn Saud. So Rabb and Malik can both have worldly implications.  but the word Ilah can only have one implication and that is Allah AWJ.
أَنَّمَآ إِلَهُكُمْ إِلَهٌۭ وَحِدٌۭ
No doubt. Your diety. your god can ONLY be one

So when we look at the 3 words used for Allah. Rabb, Malik and Ilah. we see there is a progression from more to less. from general to specific. until it comes down to the one and only Allah.

But now when you observe the word Naas. which means people in general. or mankind.  It is actually a progression from less to more. Think about this. When someone takes care of someone.  in the worldly sense.  They can only take care of a few. Your parents how many children can they take care of all at once? A few. Once the number goes beyond 3. now the older siblings have to pitch in to take care of the younger ones. But the parents themselves can only take care of a few. How may students can a teacher do justice with at one time? Only a few. How many patients can a physician have under his or her care? A few. If there are too many. A Rabb cannot manage. correct?

But what about a king? What about a مَلِک ? Does he take care of more than a few? He does. He has an entire kingdom to take care of. He's got a lot more people under him. So the number of people that a king has to protect.  and take care of.  are a lot more than what a parent or a teacher. a Rabb has to take care of. Yes?

Now what about an Ilah?? How many people does Allah take care of? The entire creation! SubhanAllah!

So you see the words used for Allah. Rabb, Malik and Ilah. they carry an implication of more to less. But at the same time the implications of the word Naas. as in رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ .  they are going from less to more. SubhanAllah! That's why the word ٱلنَّاسِ each time has a slightly different meaning. The repetition there isn't just for beautificiation or rhyming. It actually has a different implication each time. both from the point of the one giving protection. as well as the one seeking protection. رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ can be many people (parents, teachers, company owners). each of them taking care of and protecting a small group.  مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ on the other hand. is a much smaller group. protecting a much larger group.  and then the most comprehensive one is إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ.  a single diety. taking care of the entire universe. Therefore there is this incredible progression in eloquence inside these ayats.

Now what was the surah we studied before this? Surah AlFalaq. Do you remember seeing a similar pattern in the previous Surah? What did we see in Surah AlFalaq?? . In that surha. the evils mentioned.  were progressing from generic to specific.

مِن شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ. From all evils that were created. Very general
وَمِن شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ. From the evils of the dark night. It's no longer everything. Just the evils of the night.
وَمِن شَرِّ ٱلنَّفَّثَتِ فِى ٱلْعُقَدِ. From those who blow on knots. A specific group performing magic within the darkness of night
وَمِن شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ. From the jealous who acts upon his jealousy. Down to a single entity. The jealous

SubhanAllah. In Surah AlFalaq. which is primarly a Musta'az minhu. focused on the protection FROM evils. the mention of evil goes from generic to specific. And Surah AlNaas. being primarily Musta'as bihi. focused on the protection OF Allah. the call to Allah. goes from generic to specific. SubhanAllah! And this is spoken text. How do you do this with spoken text?

You see how perfect and precise the text of these surah's are? Can we as human beings talk like this? Can we in a moment's notice. say. OK. magic has been performed on Rasul Allah. so let me put together 2 surahs containing 11 ayats. because there are 11 knots on this device used to do magic against him. In the first one I'll seek protection FROM evil. keeping the ratio of 3:1 in protection from evil vs the call to Allah. The next one since it's protection of Allah. I'll maintain the ratio of 3:1 between calling Allah 3 times and mentioning evil once. In falaq. being a surah of protection FROM evil.  I will transition the mention of protection of evil from general evil to the specific evil of jealousy. In Surah AlNaas. being a surah of protection OF Allah. I will transition the names of Allah from generic Rabb specifically to Ilah. I'll keep the Falaq entirely about the protection of the body. and I'll make Surah AlNaas entirely about the protection of the soul. I'll start Surah AlFalaq with the mention of the name Falaq. which means to rip through and tear through the darkness of night to bring forth the day. so why don't I make sure I mention darkness in all the remaining ayats so they can perfectly tie in with the word Falaq. Let me use the word as glad tidings of relief for the victim. and at the same time use the exact same word as a warning from the criminals. And since I'm calling the next Surah. AlNaas. which means people. let me tie everything I say after that with mankind. And I'll do all of this in-promptu. without any hesitation. without any editorial process or revision. SubhanAllah! If this is not a miracle. then I don't know what is. If this doesn't bring me down to my feet. does not leave me incapable of a response. then I don't know what else can.

And we haven't even looked at Surah AlNaas yet. There is still a treasure of miracles yet to be seen from this Surah. and then the relationship of these surahs with AlFateha. It is simply incredible.

Psychological progression from Rabb to Malik to Ilah. From owner to king to God. Owner is someone who loves his property and consideres it valuable. as a result of which he cares about it. is always concerned about it. and always sets it straight. The king has authority. so what was excluded from the word Rabb. is captured in Malik. Allah is not only the owner. he also has complete authority. and then both these words together lead to the natural conclusion. that He is Ilah. He is the creator, controller and sustainer of everything.
And because the word Rabb and Malik can be used in the worldly sense. that's why Allah presides over all these terms and establishes his dominance over these terms. He declares that even though there are people that I have granted ownership over you. but I am the ultimate Rabb. Even though there are people who I have given temporary authority over you. but I am the ultimate Malik. And then I am Ilah. and no one has partnership with me in that respect.

Then scholars point out something very interesting. As we saw. the word Rabb is associated purely with love. And the word Malik is associated purely with authority. And this surah BEGINS with the word Rabb. قل اعوذ برب الناس . It begins with love. and THEN proceeds to authority. So the first relationship Allah has with his creation is based on love. The need for authority comes into play when? When love is not being appreciated. When love is not being recognized. When we as ungrateful human beings. when we start taking love for granted. that's when authority is brough into action. This is exactly similar to parents with kids. No parent wants to start off with authority. Every parent wants to start off with love. All prents want love to be the emotion that they want the child to accept. But then when that does not happen. they are forced to switch to authority.  We see this same principle in this surah. where Allah beings with Rabb. He begins with love. but then when that is not enough. he has to resort to authority. And then He finally uses his ultimate identity which is Ilah. Which also is a VERY beautiful word.  InshaAllah! we'll study this word soon when we study the word Allah. With the combination of the words Rabb and Malik. He wants us to appreciate this word Ilah. I'll come back to this InshaAllah when we study the word Allah. Anyway. So Allah wants us to accept Him as Rabb first. He wants us to recognize his love first. When we fail to do that. He progresses to his Authority. And together they establish his ultimate identity of Ilah.
Then the word Naas is used with all three roles. As we studied the word Naas comes from Nisyaan. meaning forgetfulness. And this is why out of all the words. the word Naas is used because we as human beings tend to forget that Allah is Rabb. that he loves us. We tend to forget that he has authority over us. that he is Malik. And we tend to forget that he is our creator. He is our Ilah. And that's why naas is used with all these roles SO perfectly.
Then from a alternate view point. studying the example of Firon. we saw that his arrogance. which in turn is nothing other than the whisperings of Shaytaan.  misled him to believe that He is Rabb. He is Malik. and He is Ilah.  And the purpose of that story.  is a warning to us. Because in our lives. we tend to do the same thing. We forget that we are Naas. and we start thinking ourselves as Rabb. We forget we are naas. and we tend to start thinking of us as Malik. and forgetting we are Naas. we make our desires and our passions our diety. and we start worshipping them. So at the same time these three ayats are a warning and a threat to us that we should always remember our place. And where we stand in relation to these three words. Rabb Malik and Ilah.
 

Meaning of Naas

Now let's look at the word "naas". As we've seen. the wordings of Quran are very precise. Every word is like a brick in a beautiful architecture. You cannot move one word from its place. So now why does Allah use the word Naas. because many other words could have been used here. Nations أقوام for example.  قل اعوذ برب أقوام. Dawl. Umam. many words could have been used. all of which mean a group a people. Now why Naas? And especially because this Surah is named after this word.
The word Naas. in its origin.  comes from the word nisyaan. which means forgetfulness! . One of the reasons human beigns are called Naas is because they are forgetful. Because they forgot the promise they had made to Allah in the spiritual world before being born in his physical world. And you know what that promise was?

When Allah created human beings in the spiritual world.
وَإِذْ أَخَذَ رَبُّكَ مِنۢ بَنِىٓ آدَمَ مِن ظُهُورِهِمْ ذُرِّيَّتَهُمْ
When their Rabb. their master. their owner. When He gave existence to souls from nothing.
 وَأَشْهَدَهُمْ عَلَىٰٓ أَنفُسِهِمْ.
And he made them witness Him. Meaning all these created souls were made to witness Allah AWJ. they all stood before Allah.  and then He asked them.
أَلَسْتُ بِرَبِّكُمْ ۖ
Allah said. Am I not your master? Am I not your rabb? even then he introduced himself  as rabb. we all said
قَالُوا۟ بَلَىٰ ۛ شَهِدْنَآ ۛ
Of course you are. we all testify!

When he created us.  and we were all standing before him. Allah asked. أَلَسْتُ بِرَبِّكُمْ Am I not your master? You know what he didn't ask? Do I exist? Do I exist? He didn't ask that. why? Because He's right there. we as souls are seeing him. that would have been a stupid question for us to ask our maser.  when we are seeing him. Ya Allah Do you really exist?
So he asked أَلَسْتُ بِرَبِّكُمْ Am I not your Rabb?  We all. every single one of us. testified ! بَلَىٰ ۛشَهِدْنَآ . Of course Oh Allah we are witness that you are our Rabb. You are our owner. But then when we came to this world we forgot.

Now let's think about that for a second. We witnessed Allah in the spiritual world. We obviously couldn't have had any doubts about His existence. or His majesty. or His glory. at that point. He made us bear witness that He is our Rabb. Not Malik. Not Ilah. but Rabb. But then we are born in this world. our memory is wiped clean. isn't it? None of us remember that day when we saw him standing before us in the spiritual world. correct? So why is that? Wouldn't it be so much easier to believe in Allah. if we could just remember that one day? So then what's the point of this forgetfulness?  Well stay tuned for Season 2 of Sunday Sessions. Hahaha. I'll explain that when we study AlHamdu Lillahi Rabb AlAalmeen.  Because we need to study a few more things in order to really understand this concept.

But for now. just understand that the word Naas comes from Nisyaan. which means forgetfulness. And we as human beings tend to forget. Parents tell us not to do something. we end up doing it and when they ask us why we did it. our answer is what? I forgot! We forget things all the time. We forget birthdays. we forget appointments. we forget prayers. we even forget our master and our lord. And this is all thanks to the waswasa of Shaytan.

One of the ONLY powers Allah has given shaytan.  is the ability to make us forget. And what's the biggest thing that he makes us forget? That Allah is there. he makes us forget that. And then when we do remember that Allah is there. he makes us forget that He is our master. I don't mean you forget it for life. like you have amnesia or something.  Thats not what I mean. What I mean is that he makes us forget Allah. it in the moment when we needed to remember him. when we needed to remember his ownership of us. That's when he makes us forget Allah.
In those 5 minutes.  when we were acting out your desires. When we were acting out our agression.  we forgot. For that evening.  for that weekend we forgot.  When we took that turn to the place we should not have gone. we forgot. When we raised our eyes.  and looked at what we were not supposed to look.  we forgot.
In all of these moments. we forgot that we have your master. Shaytan can make us forget AT that very moment when we needed to remember allah. Listen to his ayah.
ٱسْتَحْوَذَ عَلَيْهِمُ ٱلشَّيْطَنُ فَأَنسَىٰهُمْ ذِكْرَ ٱللَّهِ
Shaytan got a hold of them. and he made them forget the rememberance of Allah. THAT is all shaytan wants to do. Make us forget the remembrance of Allah.
This is why the word naas is used in this surah. قل اعوذ برب الناس .  Because Naas means pepole who have the tendency to forget. And when they forget whose waswasa is it that makes them forget? Shaitan's! So part of the lesson of this surah is that we seek Allahs protection.  from becoming forgetful. We are asking allah. to help us become people of remembrance.  and not people who forget. make us not from people who are heedless. And that's why Allah reminds us.
فَإِذَا قَرَأْتَ ٱلْقُرْآنَ فَٱسْتَعِذْ بِٱللَّهِ مِنَ ٱلشَّيْطَنِ ٱلرَّجِيمِ
When you recite the quran seek allahs protection from shaytan. because he will make you forget . Does that happen to you? You are reciting quran. or you are physically in salaah. but mentally you are on a completely different planet already? You're shopping at the mall. replaying that last episode of breaking bad in your head. You're in the middle of Salaah. but you've already changed the channel. You're now on a completely different frequencey at that point. You have no idea whats going on. You don't remember where you are. what you're doing. who you're standing before. You even forget what raka you're in. That's why whenever you recite quran, seek allahs refuge.

Even in surah Kahaf this lesson was mentioned in passing. you know how the servant of mossa AS forgot?
فَإِنِّى نَسِيتُ ٱلْحُوتَ وَمَآ أَنْسَىٰنِيهُ إِلَّا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ أَنْ أَذْكُرَهُ
NO one except shaitan made me forget.

The lesson from this is that one of the greates tactics of shaytan is to make us forget the remembrance of Allah. So now these two things. forgetfulness and getting caught with the shaytan. are the same thing now. And remembering Allah.  and being protected from Shaytan is also the same thing now. If the heart is filled with Allah's remembrance. then shaytans has no room to get in. But when the heart is empty from Allahs remembrance. theres a big sign hanging out now. Vacancy available. And shaytna goes in. The only way he can go in is when you and I are not remembreing Allah.

So because of this tendency of human beings to forget. the word Naas is used so perfectly in this surah.رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ. The owner and master of Naas. because people will forget that Allah is their owner. They will forget that Allah has ownership over them.  ِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ. Because people will forget that Allah is their true king. has complete authority over them. إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ. Because people will forget that Allah is their God. They will forget that Allah is the ONLY one to be worshiped. They will forget that and start worshipping other things.
 

Firon Taking Place Of Allah

Now the flip side of this coin.  When we studied Surah AlFalaq. we saw that the word Falaq was being used in two ways. based on the audience it was speaking to. When talking to the victims of evil. it was a glad tiding to them. saying. Don't worry. I am the Rabb AlFalaq. I'll tear open the darkness of your afflictions and bring you out of them just like I tear open the darkness and bring out the day. But then at the same time it also talks to the criminals. and warns them. and threatens them  saying. Falaq is also the name of a door in hellfire. So you better not be doing these kinds of evils to others. So Surah AlFalaq is a double edged sword.

Now let's see if the same pattern exists in Surah AlNaas.

In the Quran a LOT of bad peole are mentioned. Lots of Shayateen are mentioned. But who is the greatest of enemies mentioned in the Quran? After Iblees himself.  who would you put at number 2? Firaon! You would have to put Firon at number 2. And I want you to note something about Firon. But before that. very quickly. what are the three names of Allah mentioned?
رَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ

Now look at what the Quran says. Let's take the first word "Rabb". What did Firon say about himself in the Quran.
فَقَالَ أَنَا۠ رَبُّكُمُ ٱلْأَعْلَىٰ ‎
I am Rabb. and not just rabb.  I am the greatest of all rabbs  أَنَا۠ رَبُّكُمُ ٱلْأَعْلَىٰ ‎    .  The greatest waswasa of shaytan.  What you're supposed to attribute to Allah he attributed to himself. Rabb.


What was the second name that Allah mentioned for himself after Rabb? Malik. King! And we find another statement of Firon in the Quran.

وَنَادَىٰ فِرْعَوْنُ فِى قَوْمِهِ. Firon said to his nation
قَالَ يَقَوْمِ أَلَيْسَ لِى مُلْكُ مِصْرَ . Am I not the king of Egypt?
وَهَذِهِ ٱلْأَنْهَرُ تَجْرِى مِن تَحْتِىٓ ۖ أَفَلَا تُبْصِرُونَ
Don't these rivers flow beneath my feet? Don't you see all of this?

What did he call himself this time? King! he mentioned himself as Rabb first.  and then he mentioned himself as king. What's left? Ilah! Now let's see if he committed this crime too? He turns to his chiefs and he says
وَقَالَ فِرْعَوْنُ يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلْمَلَأُ مَا عَلِمْتُ لَكُم مِّنْ إِلَهٍ غَيْرِى
My generals! listen up! I don't know of any other Ilah for you. other than myself.

In the story of Firon. we find him declaring 3 things for himself. Roboobiyah, Mulk and Uloohiyah. all 3 for himself. He calls himself Rabb Malik and Ilah. Now this sampling that allah has given us in the quran is very important. It shouldn't be overlooked . and its not just for you and i to say. . Man Firoon! He's such a horrible person. What a loser ! No!!
There is something here. There is a lesson to be learnt here. That this is what the whisperings of shaytan can lead to.

What was the biggest problem of Iblees himself? What made him Iblees? Arrogance!
أنا خیر منہ. خلقتنی من نار و خلقتہ من تین
I am better than him because you created me from fire. and you created Adam from clay. So Iblees's problem was arrogance. which got him into trouble with Allah. So to get us human beings into trouble. what is the greatest thing he can instill within us? Arrogacnce! And who is the worst manifestation of arraogance in the quran? Firon!
But you don't have to reach that level. to worry that you are headed down the same road that leads to firon. Today we are not living in a time where people declare themselves god over others. But we are living in times where people declare themselves god over themselves. They declare that their own master.  I am my own man! I am my own king!  I am my own master! I am king of the house! I am king of my domain. we declare ourselves as our own Ilah. And the Quran says.
أَرَءَيْتَ مَنِ ٱتَّخَذَ إِلَهَهُۥ هَوَىٰهُ
Did you see the one who takes his desires. and turns them into his Ilaah. We let our desires become our gods over it and we start worshipping them. Desire says. Smoke! it'll make you look cool. And we say "Yes Master". Desire says. "Forget salaah. watch a movie". we say Yes Master!.  Desire commands. and we obey.
Wwe're living in times. where we have all turned into mini Firoons. without even realizing it. You don't have to have large castles and fight with messengers. and be arrogant and outspoken against allah AWJ. We don't need to do that to become Firon today. Our Egos have made us all Firon's today.

And that very ego is crushed in the beginning of these surahs by us openly declaring. I need protection.  I need allah's protection. I am coming into his obedience. this is a very powerful lesson in submission. In fact. Iblees himself recognizes the lordship of Allah.  but he wants human beings to forget it. He himself said to Allah. YOU are the one who created me.
خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
What stopped you from prostrating to me? He said I am better than him. You created me from fire and you created him from clay. He admites that YOU created me. He accepts being Allah's creation. He accepts that Allah is his Rabb. His Malik and is Ilah. Even when he is disobeying Allah.  he is giving credit to allah. You created me.  خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ   . Even then he acknowledged tawheed himself. but he wants the human being to forget that tawheed. . He wants the human being to become ungrateful. may allah protect us all from the waswasa of shaytan.

So we see that this surah like the previous one is a reminder and a warning at the same time. It is reminder to the one seeking Allah's protection. that don't worry. I am your Rabb. your owner. I am your Malik (your king). and I am your Ilah (your God). But at the same time a warning and a threat. That don't you dare try to become Rabb. If I have given you ownership. it is ONLY a trust. Don't let that delude you into arrogance. If I have given you authority over a country. Don't forget that I am the ultimate authority. don't oppress people I have placed under your control. And don't let your desires become your god. because I am the ultimate Rabb. the ultimate Malik and the ultimate Ilah.
 

RECAP


 

من شر الوسواس الخناس

So now that we've talked about the protection OF part.
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ
Which to summarize is. قُلْ I openly declare. I put aside my ego. and I openly and willingly submit in obedience . أَعُوذُ for spiritual protection of my diety. بِرَبِّ ٱلنَّاسِ to the owner of people.,.  مَلِكِ ٱلنَّاسِ . the king of people. إِلَهِ ٱلنَّاسِ . the God of people. And now that I've submitted TO the protection of Allah. what am I seeking protection from?
من شر الوسواس الخناس
From the evil of the retreating whisperer . So there are two words here we need to understand. الوسواس  the one who whispers and الخناس. the one who retreats.

Let's begin with الوسواس   . the whisperER. And what does a whisperer do?.  He does  وسوسۃ. He whispers
Now. there is another word in arabic that is sued for whisper. and that is ھمسۃ . . which is also used in the Quran
وَخَشَعَتِ ٱلْأَصْوَاتُ لِلرَّحْمَنِ فَلَا تَسْمَعُ إِلَّا هَمْسًۭا
On that day of judgment. everyone will stand silent before AlRehman. and you will not hear anything except faint whisperings

Now the first question is what is the difference between ھمسۃ and وسوسۃ ?

The first difference is that the word ھمسۃ means to whisper anything.  it doesn't matter whether it is good or bad. I can whisper something good. or I could whisper something bad. So such a whisper. where the intention is irrelevant. the word ھمسۃ is used.  But وسوسۃ is ONLY and ALWAYS used for evil whispering. You understand? ھمسۃ can be used for both good and evil whispering. but وسوسۃ  is ONLY used for evil whispering. Thats the first difference.

The second difference is what is called.  تکرار الَّفظ. This may get a bit technical. but its a REALLY interesting science of the Arabic language. If there is a repetition of a syllable inside a word. it actually rhetorically alludes to the repition of the act itself. If a sound is repeated more than once in the word itself. then that alludes to the repetition of the act itself.  Now in the word وسوسۃ  which syllabel do you hear repeated? The sound وس is repeated twice in the word. وس . وسۃ. So when a word in Arabic contains such repeating syllables.  that automatically implies the repetition of the act itself. It's VERY interesting.

So ھمسۃ is someone who whispers. Listen carefully. ھمسۃ . NO syllabels are not repeated. That means the ھامس whispers only once. But Was-Wasa. because the syllabel وس is repeated. that implies that a وَسوَاس. the whisperER.  is somone who whispers. and then whispers again. and then whispers again. and then whispers again.
So الوسواس   is someone who whispers all the time. continuously.  until its purpose is achieved.   wass -wassaa wass-wasaa wass -wassaa. That's how that act of whispering is. it is constantly repeated until the goal is acquired.
A similar example is the word zal-zala. which means the shaking of the earth. and earthquake. But you notice the syllabel "ZAL" repeated? So zalzala means shaking of the earth. but its not just the earth shaking once. It is when the earth shakes. then it shakes again. and then shakes again. that is zal-zala. 
A series of mountains. one after the other. sil-silaa. Not just a mountain but a series of mountains one after the other.

So when a syllabel is repeated within a word. it describes continuity of the act itself. it implies repetition. You understand? So just studying the root of the word وسواس tells us.  that this whispering that is mentioned. is first of all taking place with evil intent.  and secondly. it is not just happening once. but repeatedly. And by repeatedly I don't mean a few times.

Now here's another subtle difference we need to understand. When I say several times . that could be a few random times and that's it. right? .  And this is why you see. Arabic is such an eloquent and sophisticated language. If the act of whispering would be repeated only a few times. then the word would have been  المُوَسوِس. which is the active participle.  But allah did not use the word الموسوِس. or وِسواس. The whisperer.  Notice both words الموسوِس. or وِسواس. they contain Kasra. A kasra would mean just a few sets of whispers. He would repeat his deed a few times and then walk away. But in the ayah. وَسوسۃ . is used. with a fatha or a zabar. This is called صیغۃ المبالغہ . meaning.  The one who whispers NON-STOP. The EXTREME whisperer. one who is obsessed with whispering.  You understand?
If he was just a whisperer. he would have been وِسواس. But a وَسواس is an obsessive compulsive whispere. he's a whisperer with OCD. He doesn't stop. He keeps going and going and going. till he accomplishes his goal.

So now you see what just happened here?. Just the word whisper. وسوسۃ . itself implied continuous reptition by the repetition of the syllabel in it. But now tack on top of it. the hyperbolized form of the whisperER. with the Fatha (وَسواس and not وِسواس). That adds further strength to the act of continuous whispering. And this makes it A VERY VERY. EXTREMELY.  powerful word to use.  to describe the CONSTANT. NEVER ENDING. RELENTLESS. whispering of shaytan. This is not an easy enemy we are dealing with. We are dealing with a VERY POWERFUL enemy. and this is VERY important to appreciate. Because ONLY AFTER we truly appreciate the power of this enemy. we can understand the need of our submission to the protection of Allah. When you are afraid of an enemy that you think you might be able to take on yourself. your desperation of seeking protection against that enemy is of a differentl level. But when you know that there is NO way you can defeat an enemy. the level of your desperation in seeking protection completely changes. doesn't it?

So that's the first thing to undertand from this word. الوسواس. that Shaytan is someone who whispers.  and will continue to whisper non stop till the end of time.  The second thing I want you to notice is that this ayah seeks protection from the evil of the constant whisperER. Not the whisperING itself. The ayah does not say. من شر الوسوسۃُ الخناس . Protection from the evil WHISPERING of Khannas. After all isn't it the whispering that is bad? . Aren't we seeking protection from the evil whispering. So why did Allah specifically mention the whisperER and not the whispering itself?. This is because the one who does the whispering.  can do more evil than just the whisper itself. You understand?
Whispering is just ONE of the tactics of Shaytan. Therefore when we ask allah.  for protection against the whisperER. we realize that his constant whispering is only ONE of the ways in which he can harm us. He could harm us in numerous other ways. the greates of which is his whispering. So we're submitting to Allah's protection against ALL of it. We're asking for protection against his whispers and also ANY other things he may do to harm us.  If the ayah just said protect me from the whispering. then that's all we would be protected from. But we are asking for protection from his whispering AND any other acts he may try to do against us. Basically we are seeking protecting against HIM. from EVERYTHING he does.  including his whisper. So it is way more comprehensive. and all inclusive to say من شر الوسواس الخناس than to say  من شر الوسوسۃ الخناس.

Khannas

Then there is the adjective that has been added to the whisperer wich is  الخناس . Literally the word means "The RetreatER". The one who retreats. This word is also used elsewhere in quran.
‏فَلَآ أُقْسِمُ بِٱلْخُنَّسِ ‎
ٱلْجَوَارِ ٱلْكُنَّسِ
It is used to describe stars.  that seem to the eye that they would twinkle.  and then step back and disappear.  Thats what the word خَنَسَ means. To step back. to Retreat.
But the ayah is not
من شر الوسواس الخَانِس .
Khaanis is the one who steps back.  خَنَّاسَ . The one who KEEPS stepping back.  And if he keeps stepping back. then that in itself implies.  that he keeps stepping forward as well.  and then again steps back. You know what this means? It means that he's not only constantly whispering. and where did we get that from? From الوسواس. the one who constantly whispers. But then as soon as he whispers. what does he do? He steps back. So if somebody does that to you. Someone calls out your name from behind .  and then when you turn around he's not there.  he stepped back. That's  خَنَّاسَ . And then.  the moment you show him your back.  what does he do again? He steps forward and whispers again. And you would think that after several times of doing this. he would stop. right? But not according to the word الخناس . Because it is once again.  صیغۃ المبالغہ. It is used in its hyperbolized form. just like الوَسواس.

You know the word khabbaaz. means the one who makes khubz. He makes bread over and over and over again. he does it for a living.  He does not just make one pita bread and give up. He keeps making bread day in and day out. that's why he is called al-khabbaaz. He is going to do it for a living all the time. 
Similarly someone who KEEPS on giving gifts. never stops. Keeps giving gifts over and over and over again. وھَّاب.  Hiba means a gift. وھَّاب.  one who gifts over and over and over again. And this is actually one of the names of Allah AWJ.  Another name غَفَّار . 
غَافِر . someone who forgives . غَفَّار . someone who keeps forgiving over and over and over and over again. Its not that Allah just forgives once. or that He's forgiving.  He is غَفَّار .  because He CONSTANTLY forgives.  over and over and over again. Even for the same crimes that we keep repeating. as long as our intention is pure when se seek His forgiveness. So there is this hyperbolee used in these words.

So الوسواس الخناس. is someone who keeps coming at you from behind. whispers a thought in your head. and then retreats. Comes to you again. whispers a thought in your head. and then retreats. Comes again. whispers a thought in your head. and then retreats.
Now what do you think. From a pshychological point of view. What do you think happens when someone keeps doing that to you? Someone keeps whispering to you over and over again. and keep retreating over and over again. What do you start thinking? You start thinking that these thoughts. are YOUR OWN thoughts. He instigates you. and ou think it is YOU who actually wants to do it. It is YOU who wants to see it. It is YOU who wants to feel it. You end up taking responsibility of committing the evil act. which started off with someone else's whisper. How many times in your life have you caught yourself saying. I can't believe I did that. I can't believe I said that. I can't believe I thought that?. We do it all the time.
Shaytan with his CONSTANT. Never ending whispering. with his constant retreat. He makes us do things.  which at one time we had said. I'll NEVER EVER do that. And then we end up doing those EXACT same acts. that we detested in others. And it's all because of  الوسواس الخناس.

So that is الوسواس الخناس. . He keeps whispering. retreating. and then coming back. over and over and over again. He NEVER EVER quits.
So his offense is الوسواس . and his defense is الخناس. And that's why Allah calls out to us. to give ourselves willingly . in submission to our Rabb. our Malik. and our Ilah. Because when someone tries to hurt a child. who comes between the child and his enemy? Parents stand in between. The Rabb AlNaas comes forth for protection. When civilians are being attacked by invaders. who comes forth to protect the civilians? The king does. That's Malik AnNaas. And when an enemy SO powerful. physical or spiritual. when such a powerful enemy.  that neither the Rabb nor the Malik (in the worldly sense) can protect against. When الوسواس الخناس attacks. who comes to our protection? Ilah AnNaas. SubhanAllah!  So we have both his attacks. of وسوسۃ as well as خنس covered inside these 2 words.

So from this ayah. we are learning that Shaytan.  plants himself.  right in the heart of human beings. of the sons of Adam AS. And then as soon as the human being gets lexadazical. As soon as he becomes heedless. He becomes forgetful.  Shaytan hits him with waswasa. But then as soon as he remembers Allah. As soon as he remembers his Rabb. his Malik. His Ilah.  Shaytan retreats back.  He takes a step back. 
So when we remember allah . shaytan takes a step back. and when we stop remembering allah.  Shaytan takes moves forward. and he NEVER EVER stops.  Its not like he sees an opening and says. Aaaah I'm tired today.  don't feel like it.  mood nahee hai.  I don't feel like doing waswasa today.  had a long busy few thousand years. NO !!! He doesn't do that. because he is  الوسواس الخناس. He never takes a break. You and I will take a break from remembering Allah.  Shaytan NEVER takes a break. He works hard at his job. he is working harder than any of us. And to defend ourselves against such an enemy. what do we need to do? We have to fight back HARD. This is not something that comes casually. This استعاذہ from shaytan. It does not come easily. He is really GREAT at what he does. And to be protected. we really have to appreciate the hard work he is putting in. .  to throw people into hell fire. This is serious stuff. These ayas really give us a true appreciation of what the level our defenese against him should be like.

Now what is the end goal of his constant whispering? What goal is he trying to achieve? What did we see his own problem was? It was Kibr. it was arrogance and pride. right? And thats what he wants to instill in the hearts of people. Because he knows. that's what got him into trouble. Therefore it will surely get others into trouble as well. And the easiest way to do that is anger. Anger is a manifestration of what? Of Anger. Of Ego! And shaitaan is very good at making us angry. He will work so tactfully to make you angry. He'll work on you. And then at the same time he'll work on the one he wants you get angry with. And then put you both together. and BOOM. It is CRAZY how this guy operates. He'll tell the thief to commit robbery. and at the same time tell the guard to be careful tonight. He is the greatest double agent you will EVER encounter in your life.

Even if you try to help someone. You see someon getting angry.  you go and try to remind him. Asif Mamu! please don't get angry. Calm down. say اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان ارجیم. He'll get me mad right back at you.

What do you mean? Are you calling me shaitan? Are you saying I am posessed by shaitan?

He'll get that person even more angry. And then you'll get mad. I'm trying to help you and you're yelling at me??? What the hell? . And you and I are going at it.  and shaytaan is sitting there laughing. Saying.  I got them good! I even got him to stop saying   اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان ارجیم  SubhanAllah.

So make no mistake. Shaytan is REALLY good at what he does. and it takes humility and a lot of courage to take a step back and say.  this is not me. This is shytan whispering to me. I need to take a step back and humble myself before allah.  And realize that anger is something that is be-fitting ONLY to Allah.  and it is not something befitting to me. It is not something I should be taking upon myself. So if I'm feeling angry. I should take a step back and say اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان ارجیم. . And Quran warns us to be constantly aware of Shaytan's presence
مَا مِنکُم مِن احدٍ اِلَّا قَد وُکِّلَ بِہِ قَرِینُہُ
There is not one of you , but there is a constant partner assigned with him.

Now notice the word QAREEN is used. which means associate. This hadees does not use the word shaytan. so you have to be careful about your associates. The friends you hang out with. if he can't get to you directly.  he'll get to you through your friends. Through your associate he will whisper to you.

And you know. this waswasa. is not just against Allah. Shaytan also does waswas about Rasul allah (SAS) and his Awliya. Maulana Ali. about the Imams duaat, manaseeb. Your parents. He'll do waswas about everyone. The easier attack is not to attack our eman ABOUT allah. You know what the easier attack is? Attacking our Eman IN the MESSENGER of allah. the friends of allah. he can attack those kinds of eman very easily. because shaytan brings ego in the way. 
بشرٌ یَھدُو لَنا؟
This man is going to guide us? Come on! Hes just like us. They said about Eisa AS . یمشی فی الأسواق . he walks in in the market just like us. He goes shoping too. How is he a messenger?. I saw him at the grocery store the other day. Hes a messenger? یأکل الطعام . He eats food just like I eat food. what makes him so special? Come On! You really expect me to take authority from him??
And this is the root of ego. human beings refuse to accept the authority of another human being. Thats just ingrained inside our heads. Employees can't stand listening to their bosses. The only time you say you have a good boss. is when he doesn't give you any work to do. You get pulled over by a cop. he shows you his authority.  you get irritated. you have to go before a judge. you get irritated. human beings just don't like another human being having authority over them.

من شر الوسواس الخناس


In the previous session we studied the meaning of the ayah. من شر الوسواس الخناس. we know in this surah. we specifically seek Allah's protection.  from ONE specific evil.  from the evil of  الوسواس and الخناس. The one who is constantly whispering.  and constantly retreating. We understood how relentless and incessant and oppressive Shaytan is in his whispers. Therefore we must constantly seek protection of Rabb AlNaas, Malik AnNaas and Ilah AnNaas from the evil of this الوسواس الخناس .

Now after describing this evil entity. shaytan itself. Allah proceeds to describe his evil actions.  So the surah continues to say.
الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس. The one who constantly whispers into the chests of people.
من الجنۃ و الناس . They are from among the jinn and mankind

Let's look at the first ayah.
الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس. The one who constantly whispers into the chests of people.

The first thing to notice here.  is that Allah mentions whispering again. He had alread mentioned that in the previous ayah.  من شر الوسواس الخناس . But now again he's saying  الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس. So let's begin by understand the reason for this repetition.
In the previous ayah we see.  that Allah mentioned the IDENTITY of this evil entity. and here He is mentioning the ACTION of that evil entity. And he used the present tense یُوَسوِسُ for it too.

So we saw that Shaytan is الوسواس. that Shaytan is someone who whispers.  and will continue to whisper non stop till the end of time. The next thing I want you to know is that الوسواس is an Ism. its a noun. الاسم یدُلُّو علی الدوام . a noun signifies permanence.

In the arabic language. just like any other language.  you can use nouns and you can use verbs.  What is the difference betwen a verb and a noun? Between nouns and verbs, which has tenses? You know present tense, future tense, past tense? Verbs have a tense . Nouns do not have a tense . There's no past tense noun or present tense noun or future against noun . Is that clear? When I say I am eating. it means I'm eating now. but at some point I will stop. a verb is tied in time. it has happened. it is happening. or it will happen. but it is temporary. it will not happen at some point. But a noun is permanent. It doesn't change state. A book is a book. was a book. is a book. will always remain a book. It's not going to change state. You understand?

Job if Shaytan is WASWASA
Let's understand identity first. When I say to you.  I am a teacher. you know what means ? It means THAT is who I am.  thats what I do. Shaytan has been identified as الوسواس الخناس. Someone who constantly. incessantly. relentlessly. whispers and retreats. That is his identity. That's why in the previous ayah.  the noun. الوسواس is used. But in this ayah. Allah uses a verb. یُوسوِسُ . Why? Because Shaytan actually lives up to that title too. It's one thing to get the title.  but its entirely another thing to earn that title by actually doing it.
That's what the present tense یُوسوِسُ . tells us. Because in ancient Arabic when a present tense was used. future tense was implied within it. So this word یُوسوِسُ tells us.  that not only is Shaytan known for being a whisperER. for his constant, unrelentless whispering. but he is actually doing it now.  and he will contine to do it in the future. So you better be ready!. You better always be prepared. He's never going to stop. There is never going to be a time or a moment.  when you can think that you are free from his whispers.
Which in turn also means. that there is never going to be a time. when you and I will NOT need allah's protection. We're constantly under attack. therefore we constantly need Allah's protection.  Even when you we engaged in religion activities. like salaah, fasting. zakaat hajj. He will whisper to us . every single moment.

But then allah added something quite remarkable. he said فی صدور الناس.
. in the CHEST of people. The word صدر . CHEST. according to the Arabic lexicon. it is ظرف مکان. It is actually a place. In the Quran. Sadar is always used in the context of a place or a space. رب الشرح لی صدری. Master! expand my chest. Again in the context of space.
In contrast to that.  there is the word قلب . which is a thing. Allah did not say.  الذی یوسوس فی قلوب الناس. He constantly whispers.,.  and will continue to constantly whisper in the hearts of people. Allah did not say that. He did not use the word heart. He used the word chest.  Now what's the difference?

There is actually a big difference.  between saying that he whispers in the heart.  versus saying.  he whispers in the chest. In the previous sessions. we talked about.  how the heart is the center of all human activity. Everything a man does. the desire first originates in the heart. and is then converted into action. with the help of the intellect. But the origin of desire is always the heart.

Now the imagery this ayah creates . think of it like this.  . The heart. think of it like a castle. and around the castle there is some open real estate. there is a front yart. side yard.  backyard. So there is all this real estate around the castle. The castle is your heart.  and the surrounding real estate is your chest. The heart is inside your chest.  Allah says he gave shaytan access to what? The chest.  but Allah did not give Shaytan access to the heart!

So Shaytan is chilling in the front yard. or he's sun bathing in the backyard. Basically he's all around. but he's not where yet? he's not in the heart.  the heart is locked. And the only one who has the key to the door of your heart. is You! Hes constantly knocking on the door with his whispers. He's waiting outside. patiently. He's ALWAYS there. الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس. He is constantly knocking on the door of your heart. hoping one day you will open that door for him and let him enter your heart. 

Now think of  استعاذہ as a security guard.  that you've placed outside the door of your heart. The second you say  اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم . the guard appears. and does not let the shaytan come close to the heart. He throws him back in the frontyard. But if you do not keep calling upon that guard for protection. Shaytan will keep knocking. keep knocking.keep knocking. And what will happen? Eventually you will open the door and shaytan will step inside.

So now Allah classifies the whisperERS into 2 categories. Jinn and Human beings. Now the first thing.  is the order in which these two categories are mentioned. Allah mentioned jinn first and mankind second.  Now why is that?. 
Because there are other places in the Quran. that when it came to shaytan. Allah mentions human beigns first and jinn later.
وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِىٍّ عَدُوًّۭا شَيَطِينَ ٱلْإِنسِ وَٱلْجِنِّ
And this is how for every prophet there has been an enemy. from the devils of mankind and Jinn. There are several reasons. The obvious reason.  is that in the ayah I just mentioned
وَكَذَلِكَ جَعَلْنَا لِكُلِّ نَبِىٍّ عَدُوًّۭا
the ayah is talking about prophets. And when it comes to prophets. the animosity against them. always originates from human beings first. Human beings go outright against the messenger of Allah. Since they take precdence in their animosity against the prophets. human beings are mentioned first in this ayah.
But because the context of our surah. Surah AnNaas. is not animosity against prophets . it is وسوسۃ. against human beings. Who takes the primary role? the jinn. That's why in this surah Jinn is mentioned first and human beings later.

Another reason why Jinn is mentioned first and human beings later. is because one is spiritual and the other is physical. The jinn is just a soul without a body. it is in the spiritual form. While Naas. human beings are in the physical form. And we see that this surah is all about the attack on our soul. Surah AlFalaq was about seeking protection from physical attacks. But Surah AlNaas is about seeking protection from spiritual attacks. And because of that.  Jinn. the ones in spritual form are mentioned first . and Nass. the ones in physical form are mentioned second.

Another reason is that it is the corruption of the soul that leads to the corruption of the body. It is the evil desire. that feeling of arrogance.  contempt. of jealousy. that comes first. And what is the place in which these evil desires and feelings originate? It's the heart. which is placed where? in the chest! Which is where Shaytan attacks. That's why the spiritual form (jinn) is mentioned first. and the physical form (Naas) is mentioned second. because corruption will happen. first in the soul.  and will then proceed into actions.

Another reason why Jinn is mentioned first. is because scholars comment. وسوسۃ الجن، ھو الاصل . the whispernigs of the jinn is primary.  Meaning that if a human being is whispering evil to you.  it may not even be his own whisper.  He may be plagurizing it from the whispering of HIS shaytan.
