now the complication in this word naas. In the arabic language there is a word called نفر nafar. which is commonly used for a group of people. and then there is also the word رجال which is typically used for a group of people.
Quran says.
قُلْ أُوحِىَ إِلَىَّ أَنَّهُ ٱسْتَمَعَ نَفَرٌۭ مِّنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَقَالُوٓا۟ إِنَّا سَمِعْنَا قُرْآنًا عَجَبًۭا
a group of people from among the jinn. the word nafar typically is not used for jinn. it is used for human beings. but in this ayah it is used for jinn. Similarly we have
وَأَنَّهُۥ كَانَ رِجَالٌۭ مِّنَ ٱلْإِنسِ يَعُوذُونَ بِرِجَالٍۢ مِّنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَزَادُوهُمْ رَهَقًۭا
There used to be men from among the human beings who sought refuge from men among the jinn. so now rijaal is being used for men as well as jinn.

Now in one of the narrations it is said. that some men met a group of people who were very strange looking. so they asked themm من القوم who are you guys> What nation do you come from? they replied. أناسٌ من الجن . very interesting language. they said we are people from the jinnn. but what word did they use for themselves? the plural of naas. unaas.

So another interpreation of this ayah is that. allah says الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس . the one who whispers into the chest of the naas. من الجنۃ و الناس . those naas. those people can be from among the jinn as well as the human beings.  So this surah is not just a protection for believers from among human beings. it is also a protection for believers among the jinn. So the word naas in this interpretations encompasses both. the human beings as well as the jinn.  So the same ayah can be taken in two completely contrasting ways.

So these are the two categories of the whisperERS mentioned in this surah. We now understand the waswasa of the jinn. that it manifests in the form of thoughts and desires in our heads. But what about the whisperings of the human devil? Or someone who is being used as a vehicle by a jinn? How do those whispering manifest? Because this ayah mentions both.

Whisper
The first thing to realize is that it is a whisper. So we normally think of whisper.  as someone sitting next to us and saying something to us under their breadth. wswswswsws.  We think that is whispering. But there is another form of whispering that is WAY more common. And that happens all the time on the phone. in the form of texts. We do it all the time. and it is constantly done to us as well.  It sounds something like this. Hey! I'll tell you something about this person. but just don't tell anyone I told you OK?. Blah blah blah blah blah. Does that sound familiar? Be very careful of that.

Now if this person is telling you something in confidence. with the intention of protecting you.  or helping you. for example if someone is trying to warn you about the evil intentions of someone. who is trying to harm you. that is a different thing. That is not waswasa. that is hamasa. It is not being done with evil intent. That kind of whispering is being done with good intentions. in order to protect you. There's a difference.  that is NOT waswasa. that is hamasa. I explained the difference between the two words last time.

But more than often times. what is being done is waswasa. especially when its about a third person. Someone fills you up with anger and animosity against your friend or your cousin. and then this whisperER retreats by saying "don't tell anyone I told you". And now the next time you meet this person. EVERYTHING seems wrong about him. The way he walks. the way he's dressed. the way he talks. the way he laughs. And you're sitting there wondering. Why did I ever like this person in the first place? . Did that ever happen? .  What suddenly changed? You liked this person before. now suddenly you don't like anything about him . It's because of that silent whispering . that was done to you under the covers of. "don't tell anyone I told you". "I tell you everything because you're my best friend". "I trust you so much that I feel I can tell you anything". wswswswswswsws.  Be very careful of that!

A man once came to one of the sahabas.  and he tried to slander another muslim brother . He said. You know this man. he pretends to be a muslim. He's such a hypocrite.  he drinks alcohol and he gambles. and he does all sorts of evil deeds. and still comes and prays in the masjid.  And the sahaba replied to him. Couldn't Shaytan find a better postman than you? Couldn't he find a better messenger than you to deliver this gossip to me?.
Be very careful of that. Many people in our lives act as messengers of Shaytan. and they don't even know it. Many times WE act as the messengers of Shaytan without realizing it. Be careful! And the recitation of this surah.  gives us the insight and a reminder to recognize that. in ourselves as well as others.

So to summarize.  the protection we are seeking.  is the protection of the master of people who forget. رب الناس. the king of people who forget. ملک الناس . The god of people who forget. الہ الناس. 
And this protection is from the evil entity. الوسواس الخناس . Who attacks through his whispers. الذی یوسوس .  and where does he attack?  فی صدور الناس . in the chests of people. which contains what? . the heart. And these attackers. they belong to which two categories? من الجنۃ و الناس . they are from the jinns.  and human beings.



in the first meaning. the shaytan doing the whispering can be in the spiritual form as well as the physical form.
in the second meaning. the shaytan doing the whispering can whisper TO human beings as well as TO the jinns. Because we know that allah created not just human beings but also jinn for the purpose of worshipping him.
وَمَا خَلَقْتُ ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ
I did not create the jinn and the human beings except to worship me. Now arent' the angels a creation of allah too? So why did he not mention them in this ayah? Aren't they created for his worship too?  why didn't he say
وَمَا خَلَقْتُ الملائکۃ و ٱلْجِنَّ وَٱلْإِنسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ
I did not create the angels and jinn and the human beings except to worship me. because the angles are already doing what they are supposed to do. they are always busy worshipping him. and they are not affected by the whisperings of shaytan. shaytan cannot get to them in any way shape or form. they are always under the protection of allah. it is the human beings and Jinns that falls prey to the whisperings of shaytan. And once shaytan enters their hearts. takes over their hearts. then he uses both of them to further his cause. thats the same concept of a virus. it infects other cells. makes them like itself to furhter the cuase.

Appreciation of protection through danger

That concludes our study of these 2 surahs. Now the question is . how is the Istiaaza and these 2 surahs even related to Surah AlFateha? Why are we studying the Istiaaza instead of studying the Fateha?

Imagine there is a huge storm coming. where would you prefer to be when the storm hits your town? Probably in your house? Your house is a symbol of safety against the storm. But the reason you appreciate that safety.  is because you understand the dangers of the storm.  yes? You cannot appreciate safety. until you understand the danger that you are being protected from. You appreciate the air conditioning in your house. because you've experienced the heat outside. You appreciate the heating in your house. because you've experienced the freezing cold outside. We human beings. we understand things through contrast. The one who truly appeciates and values food. is the one who has a true understanding of hunger. someone who has truly experienced hunger. You know. you can tell. just by looking at someone who wastes food. that this person has never experienced hunger. I'm not talking about the hunger after a tennis match when you come home and the fridge is loaded. I'm not talking about that hunger. I'm talking about the hunger in which you haven't eaten for days.  and there's nothing in the fridge at home. That man. when he gets food. you can see him appreciating the value of that food.

So Surah AlFateha is a fortress. It is a safe haven. But in order to truly appreciate its value. To truly appreciate what it has to offer us in terms of security. what must we first understand? The dangers. We needed to first understand the dangers. the evils that surround this fortress.
The Istiaaza. is the door of that fortress. that keeps the evils out.  and keeps us safe within the fortress.  So we started with the Istiaaza. we started with the dangers of evil. so that we can truly appreciate the comforts within the Fateha. That is why we started with the Istiaaza. and this is what Allah commanded us to do.
فأذا قرأت القرآن فستعذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم
Before you enter the fortress of Quran. seek protection . close the door on Shaytan AlRajeem. But first. understand what the Quran is protecting you from. so that you can truly appreciate its protection.

But then I started with these two surahs. Surah Naas and Surah Falaq. because they are deeply connected with surah AlFateha.  I want to quickly go over some of these connections InshaAllah!

The first connection is the cyclic pattern in the recitation of Quran. When we recite the Quran what surah do we begin with? We begin with the Fateha. And before we begin fateha. what do we recite? The Istiaaza. We say  اعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم .
So we begin with the Istiaaza. then we start Surah AlFateha. which is the essence of the entire Quran. and then we continue reciting the surahs. until we complete the recitation of Quran. But at the end of our recitation. what are the last 2 surahs we encounter? Surah Falaq and Surah Naas. both surahs of the Istiaaza. We start with the Istiaaza and we end with the Istiaaza.

So think of the Quran as a beautiful and comfortable house. a safe haven. Your fortress of solitude.  Before you enter it. you seek protection from evil.  and then you enter the house. Why? so that you can enjoy all the comforts the house has to offer. that is the recitation of the Quran. And then when you're ready to step outside. you again go through the Istiaaza in the form of Surah Falaq and Naas. so that you remain protected while you're outside the house.  So it protects us on both ends. when we enter the fortress of Quran. and when we exit it.

But then once you complete the recitation of the Quran. immediately after that what do you do? You read a dua (the dua recited at the completion of Quran) and then you recite what surah again? Surah AlFateha. You started quran with the Istiaaza. you ended it with the istiaaza. and the end of it you recite the Fateha again. And then you start the entire process again.
When you step out of your house. you go to school or work. where do you end up returning in the evening? Back to your home again. So there is this cyclic pattern in the recitation of Quran with protection on both ends.

There is something really important to understand about this analogy between a house and the Quran. As I said. we always begin our day by leaving our homes.  and at the end of our day. we return back to our homes. But where do we spend our entire day? Outside the house. At school or at work. at tennis or basketball. at tutions. at whatever. We spend most of our time outside the house. Yes?  So home is not a place we spend most of our time. We spend it ouside. But home is a place. where we gather our energies. we eat and drink and relax and sleep. those are all actions that replenish our energy. recharge our battery. correct? These things refresh us. they revitalize us. But where do we actually spend this energy? Outside our homes. Is that clear?
A true believer has the same relationship with the Quran. He enters the fortress of quran. to replenish his energies. to revitalize himself with the teachings of Quran. But where is he going to actually execute those teachings? In the ouside world. in duniya. So the idea is that we as momins. as believers. we keep coming back to the Quran constantly. to remind ourselves of its teachings. and then go back into the world.  to act upon what we have learnt.

But as soon as we step outside. who do we encounter? Our greatest enemy. Who has openely declared his animosity agianst us. We encounter Iblees or one of his shaytans. who openly declared to Allah.
قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ
because you were the one who expelled me from jannah. I will sit waiting for them . to ambush them on your straight path. صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ . Which surah mentions the straight path?
اھدنا الصراط المستقیم.  Surah Fateha mentions the straight path.
We are asking allah to protect us from iblees because he is on a mission to get us off the straight path. We learn the details of how to walk on the straight path in the Quran. but when we step outside and try walking on that straight path. who do we find sitting there. waiting to ambush us? Iblees. And that's why these two surahs of protection. falaq and naas. are so intimately connected with Surah AlFateha. Because we need Allahs protection when we are walking that straight path. because we know that Iblees is going to be there. trying to get us off.

Then from a thematic stand point. the themes of these 2 surahs.  Falaq and Naas. they have a powerful connections with AlFateha. Surah Fatiha is about the استعانۃ . We'll study this term later. But استعانۃ means seeking help. Which is what Surah AlFateha is all about.  . ایاک نعبد و ایاک نستعین . It is you we worship and it is you we turn to for help. So in Fateha. we have two statements for the Istiaana. ایاک نعبد and ایاک نستعین.  and here we have two surahs for the Istiaaza. for protection.  Surah Falaq and Surah Naas. There we ask Allah for help.  here we ask Allah for protection. You've heard of positve and negative reinformcements, right? In Fateha we ask Allah. for help in accomplishign a task. in معوذِتین  we ask Allah for His protection against elements.  that are trying to keep us from completing that task.

Then the words of these surahs. especially Surah Naas. they complement the words of AlFateha.
In Surah Naas we seek protection of the owner and master of all people. رب الناس .  in AlFateha. what do we call him? رب العلمین . owner and master of all worlds.
In fateha we say مالک یوم الدین . In Surah AlNaas we say ملک الناس . both Maalik and Malik. they both have the same root word
In fateha we say ایاک نعبد . It is you we worship.  and who is worship done for? A diety? An Ilah? Right? So in Surah AlNaas we say الہ الناس .

Then we see that the معوذِتین . they are the two surahs of protection. and in Surah AlFateh was ask Allah to keep us away from 2 kinds of people.  or two bad influences. مغضوب علیھم ولا الضالین .
And then in Surah Fateha. just as we have these two negative influences. the مغضوب علیھم ولا الضالین . In Surah Naas. we have two categories of evil that we seek protection from  من الجنۃ و الناس . from the jin and people. SubhanAllah!  There are these incredible connections between these 2 surahs and Surah AlFateha. The way in which quran begins. perfectly complements the way in which it ends.

Then another remarkable thing is the parallel between the singular and plural forms used between the two surahs.  The very word used in the معوذتین  for seeking protection.  is in the singular form. اعوذ . but the words used in the Fateha for seeking guidance. are all in plural. we say ایاک نعبد  not ایاک أعبدُ .  So there is this balance betwen sigular and plural. because the things we ask for in the Fateha. we need them as a group. as a group of muslims. or a group of momins. or a group of sulemanis. Look at it however you will. but fateha has a group theme going on. because our communication with Allah in Fateha.  is as a group. Not as individuals. We speak to him. seeking his guidance. collectively.
But when it comes to the waswas of the shytan.  is it a collective thing or is it an individual thing? It's an individual thing. Therefore in the معوذِتین . the theme is indvidual not collective. because these 2 surahs ask for allahs protection on a very personal and indvidual level. and therefore the verb usage is singular too. 


I misjudged the level of my audience.
These sessions are not for kids

We took a very detailed look at the various pieces and components of the Istiaaza. We studied Surah AlFalaq and AlNaas. We learnt things about the protector. the kind of protection He offers. and the nature of the enemy we are seeking protection from. We also learnt the requirements of seeking that protection.  Now to conclude. I want to tie all these pieces together. We saw the parts. now let's look at how these parts come together to form a complete whole. 

Iblees rebellion

So what I want to talk about today. and in the next couple of sessions. is about this passage from Surah Aale Imran. which talks about the creation of Adam AS and the disobedience and rebellion of Iblees. This passage talks about when it all began. If we truly understand the purpose and the teachings of this passage. it will answer most. if not all of our questions about what Shaytan is trying to do. What his end game is. And what are the things we need to be aware of.

I think I've said this before. but I'll say it again. that the purpose of Quranic stories. is never the story itself. We listen to these bedtime stories like Aladdin. and Cinderella. and all these Once upon a time tales. And then we listen to these Quranic stories.  and sometimes we start thinking of them in the same way. Just like Cinderella is a nice bed time story for children. the story of Adam and Hawwa also becomes a nice story in our minds.  So the first thing is that we need to change our perceptions about these stories. And the first step towards that goal.  is to understand that the purpose of these Quranic stories . is NEVER the story itself. Using these stories. Allah is always trying to explain a principle from His rule book. He is trying to explain a divine law. He's giving us a clear warning and news of how things work in his divine system. There is a system or framework within which we humans operate. and then there is a framework within which Allah operates. And Quran is our window into that divine setup.
So the idea behind these quranic stories is. Allah saying.  Look! This is what happened to the people who came before you. This is how they were confronted with evil. This is how they battled it. or this is how they succumbed to it. This is what they used to say. This is how they used to think. So look where they ended up!.  Learn from it. Don't repeat the same mistakes they made. otherwise what happend to them.  is going to happen to you too. And also study the lives of those who succeeded before you. Because if you make the same smart choices that led them to success. you too will become successful.
That is the purpose of these Quranic stories. to give us working examples and set precedents for us. because as they say. History repeats itself.

And Rasul Allah stated this in a Hadees.
لَتَتَّبِعُنَّ سَنَنَ مَنْ قَبْلَكُمْ شِبْرًا بِشِبْرٍ، وَذِرَاعًا بِذِرَاعٍ، حَتَّى لَوْ سَلَكُوا جُحْرَ ضَبٍّ لَسَلَكْتُمُوهُ
You shall follow the footsteps of those before you, inch by inch and mile by mile, to the degree that if they entered the hole of a lizard.  you will follow them too

Today we are all faced with the exact same challenges. that were faced by prophets and people of their times before us. It's form may be different. it's exterior may be different. even it's intensity may be different. but the principles are still the same. It's still based on the same root evils. greed, arrogance, jealousy, passions, desires. Nothing has changed.  And the Quran presents the solution to all those problems.
So if we truly want to understand the workings and the true mechanations of Shaytan. the only way to do that. is an in-depth study of the story of Adam AS and Iblees . Because this story of Adam AS is in fact our story. The challenges of Adam AS are in fact our challenges. He is the original template.  What happend to him. is what's happening to us.

Story of Adam Iblees
So the story of Adam AS and Iblees. is the story of humility and arrogance.  And this story has three parts. The first part is the creation of Adam and the rebellion of Ibless. We'll look at that first. The second part is the humiliation and revenge of Iblees against Adam AS.  in getting him and his wife Hawwa. cast out of Jannah. And the third part is the response of Adam and Hawwa AS. versues the reaction of Iblees once they get cast out of Jannah.

So let's begin with the first part.  Talking about the creation of Adam AS. Allah says in the Quran.
وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ صَوَّرْنَكُمْ
We created you. we moulded you. In other words Allah says.  I know who you are. what you like.  because I made you. I know how I fashioned you.  I know the things I put inside you. I know every one of your body parts.  and I know every single temptations and craving that you have. and then He says.
ثُمَّ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ
and then I asked all the angles to make sajda to you. I honored you above angels. I created in you the potential that could elevate you above angels.


Linguistic meaning of SAJDAH

Let's understand this word Sajda. It's a beautiful word. The ancient Arabs used the word Sajada. for a camel when it would lower itself before the rider. so that he could mount it. It was used in that sense. سجد الأبل they would say. when the camel would lower itself. and submit its will. to the will of its rider. Meaning the camel would allow its rider to steer it in whatever direction he wants.
So that's what sajda means in the truest sense of the word. To pay respect. or honor. by lowering oneself before a greater being. Just as the camel honors and glorifies its rider. by submitting before him. And that takes extreme humility. Because if you compare a camel to a human being. from a physical stand point. there truly is no comparison. A camel is massive compared to a human being. The strength of a camel is enormous compared to that of a human being. A camel can go for days in the extreme heat of the desert without water. a human would die of thirst. A camel can lift loads.  that would be way beyond the capacity of even the strongest human being. And yet this extremely powerful. extremely capable. this mighty creature lowers itself before a human being. It submits its will to a human being because it understands that it cannot find its path without its master.

When we fall in Sajda before Allah. it is a gesture of surrendering ourselves. surrendering our will. become humble before the will of our master. Because like the camel we too sometimes think we are superior. Our ego is our camel.  Why do I need Allah in my life? . I have money. I have power. I have status. Why do I need to submit to anyone? I am in control of my life. A camel could have the same attitude towards man. but then it would die of thirst wouldn't it? Because no matter how powerful and capable the camel thinks it is. it still needs a human being to guide it to water in a desert. That's why the camel submits itself to its owner. That's the camel's sajda.
Similarly my true sajda to Allah would be to submit the reins of my life. my will . my decisions. in the hands of my master. Letting not MY will. but the will of my master steer me through life. To let him walk me through beautiful pastures of ease.  if He so desires. and to walk me through the dry barren scorching lands of trials and hardships. if He so desires. That is the true meaning of the word Sajda. To give up oneself. to surrender one's will to the will of our master. like the camel gives itself up in the hands of its rider. like the ship that gives itself up in the hands of the wind.  السَّفِینَۃُ تَسجُدُ لِلرِّیحِ . the arabs would say.

Another beautiful meaning of the words sajda. is to bend and lower oneself.  because of the weight of the bounties that are placed upon it. For example the Arabs would say سَجَدَتْ النَّخْلَۃ. The palm tree bent down.  by the abundance of its fruit. The weight of Allah's blessings in our lives should force us fall in sajda before Him. 

So this is what sajda is. and especially during Salaah. Look. Putting our forehead on the ground is just a symbol. The true Sajda is that of the heart. It's not a Sajda.  if after my salaah ends. I am still going to do what I want.
And BTW. even if you think about this physically act of Sajda. what are we doing? we place our forehead on the ground. Head being the most superior part of the body. because it contains the intellect. through which we plan and design and scheme. We place that intellect on the earth. on dirt.  that lies beneath our feet. It is a symbol for surrendering our thoughts. our knowledge of what WE think is best. our plans. our schemes. before our master. It's a symbol of testifying that Ya Allah. even though you have blessed me with this amazing intellect. the greatest gift of all. MY plan. MY desires. My thoughts are nothing more than dirt before you will. That is the true level of obedience that is encapsulated in this symbolic act of Sajda. And therefore the PERFECT symbol of obedience. the PERFECT representation of obedience to Allah. is Sajdah.

So Allah commanded the angels to prostrate before Adam. to honor him. to resepect him. first and foremost in compliance with Allah's command. because Allah commanded them to honor him. But then also as an acknowledgment that Adam had knowledge of that which they did not.
وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا ثُمَّ عَرَضَهُمْ عَلَى ٱلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ فَقَالَ أَنۢبِـُٔونِى بِأَسْمَآءِ هَٓؤُلَآءِ إِن كُنتُمْ صَدِقِينَ
Allah taught Adad all the names. then presented him before teh angels. and asked the angels. Tell me all the names if you are truthful in your claims.  First Allah established the superiority of Adam AS over angels. by his knowledge that they didn't have. THEN he asked the angels to prostrate to him. So the sajda of the angels were for two reasons. First in obedience of Allahs command. and second in the recognition of Adams superiority in knowledge over them.
فَسَجَدُوٓا۟
They all fell in sajda.
إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ
with the exception of iblees.
لَمْ يَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّجِدِينَ
He wasn't going to be from among those who would prostrate. 
Instead of saying  ما سجدَہُ . He did not comply.  Allah says.  لَمْ يَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّجِدِينَ. he was NEVER EVER going to be from among those who would do sajda.SubhanAllah. Allah knew all along he was not going to do it.  Allah knew his intentions all along. And it's very interesting why Allah still commanded Iblees to prostrate. knowing well that he would disobey. But I'll address that a bit later.  So Allah asks Iblees.

قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ
Allah said. what possibly prevented you from doing sajda when I told you? When I commanded you! Why didn't you obey?

Notice here. Allah did not say why did you not do sajda when you clearly saw that Adam is more knowledgable than you!. Why didn't you comply with my command when it made sense to you.  Look what Allah says. This is the part you and I need to pay very close attention to .  قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ. What did you now prostrate when I COMMANDED you to?
Sajda.  has to be done in obedience to the command. You know we sometimes think. I'll do namaaz when I understand it's important. when I understand it's purpose. In other words when I have more KNOWLEDGE about it. right? That's not what Allah questions Iblees about. He gives preference to his command OVER everything else. There is nothing wrong about learning why we should pray. In fact we MUST learn that. But the REASON for Sajda. the ONLY reason for Sajda. has to be because Allah commanded us to do so. Obedience is the FIRST and foremost reason for Sajda. Why? Because the word sajda in and of itself means. that we have already accepted Allah as our master. We have lowered ourselves before Allah so that his commands can ride us. so that his command can steer us in whatever direction He pleases.
And that's why when someone asked Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq AS. یا امام ! ھل الدین ؟؟ . Oh Imam! What is religion? He replied. الا الطاعۃ . nothing except obedience. The guidance of a camel begins when does sajda before its rider. Our guidance begins when we do Sajda before Allah.

Fire vs Clay
So Allah asks Iblees. What possibly prevented you from obeying. when I commanded you? Now listen to what he says. And this is the real topic of today's conversation. Everything else sorta just hinges off of it. Iblees says.

أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ . خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
Iblees finally gives voice to his arrogance and says.I am better than him. You created me from fire and you created him from clay.

Now within this one statement. lies the root cause of disobedience. From a linguistic statement. what Iblees said. is what's called a statement of arrogance.
بیان الاستکبار.  The tone of this statement clearly suggests that Iblees had made up his mind. Had he not used this tone. this statement could have been open for debate. It could have been argued that maybe Iblees didn't understand. maybe he had doubts and he was trying to clear it up with Allah. But this is not what his tone suggests. Look at his words within the context. Who is he speaking to? He is speaking to Allah. He is speaking to the king of kings. He is speaking to his creator. And he says. I am better than him. It's a very definitive statement. It's a very obstinate statement. There is no room for argument or discussion in his statement. In other words. there is ABSOLUTELY no humility in his tone. It has a.  THIS IS HOW IT IS. AND THIS IS HOW ITS GONNA BE. kinda ring to it.

There's nothing wrong about asking questions if we don't understand. There's ABSOLUTELY nothing wrong with questioning things. Trying to seek answers. But the thing to keep in mind.  is to never let go of humility in that line of questioning. Because the way in which a question is presented. reveals everything about the underlying emotion. You can tell immediately if the person is filled with arrogance or if there's humility in that person.
And humility in a question means. considering other possible options. That maybe it is I who doesn't understand. Maybe I am missing something.  That MAYBE this person knows something I don't. Maybe I can learn something from his experience. Just MAYBE my parents actually might know what they're talking about. Arrogance on the other hand is. This is how I see things. this is what I believe. here are the facts. and I don't care what you think. I'm not even going to try to understand what you have to say. because you obviously don't know what you're talking about. It's my way or the highway.

That's the tone Iblees uses. I am better than him! period! You created me from fire. and you created him from clay. fire is better than clay. These are just facts. It's just simple observation. It's basic science! Therefore Allah. I don't know what you were thinking when you asked me to bow down to him. I don't think you know what you're doing. You clearly don't understand the difference between fire and clay. You're asking me to bow down to him??? Are you serious?
All of this arrogance is voiced in this one statement . أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ

Not it all kinda seems ridiculous doesn't it. when we look at it from outside. What a horrible thing to do! Bad Iblees. Bad Iblees. right?  But now put your parents commands and wishes in the position of Allah. Because Allah is Rabb. but so are your parents.  Allah is rabb. but so are our deeni elders. We just studied that in Surah Naas. This passage is about the relationship of a creation with his Rabb. Because what did Shaytan say? خَلَقْتَنِى . You created me. And creator means owner. and the Arabic word for that is Rabb. Allah granted his Rububiyah. to parents over children. Allah granted his rububiyah to teachers over students. When you a child talk back to your parents with arrogance. you put yourself in the same position as Iblees.
Look. there's nothing wrong with having a dialog with your parents if you disagree. that's fine. But arrogance is what's unacceptable. It's OK if you can't see eye to eye with your parents. but it's not OK to think you are better than them. you understand more than them. You don't! You can't! You guys are kids. Most of you haven't even stepped into the real world yet. They have! So they might actually know what they're talking about. Have some trust in them.  Because this ayah is teaching us the importance of humility.  when it comes to dealing with our Rabb. Parents are the closest Rabb. You can't be humble to them. how do you expect to be humble before Allah?

Another very important lesson it teaches us . is that disobedience is not the real problem. It's what leads to disobedience that is the problem. If you notice. the corruption in Iblees took place first in his soul. His statement has two parts. Look at the first part.  أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ. I am better than him. That is the corruption of his soul. That's the arrogance in his soul. And then inevitable what follows is a justification for his disobedience. خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ. You created me from fire and you created him from clay. So what he did was. he justified his arrogance with what he thought were logical facts. with no room for any sort of dialog.

And It's not like Allah was closed to a dialog. because we just saw Allah asked him.
قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ
What stopped you from disobedience when it was I who commanded you. Did Allah need to ask Iblees for his reasons? Does an owner. especially an owner like Allah.  need his property to give an explanation for why it is not behaving as it's supposed to? My pen stops writing. Am I going to ask it to present valid reasons for not writing anymore? No! I would just trash it and move on. So why is Allah asking Iblees for a reason. Because it is a gesture of disappointment. It is a gesture of an extremely loving Rabb being disappointed with his creation. You know I love you. You know who I am. You know my status. You know my knowledge encompasses all. You know I would NEVER EVER give an unjust command to obey. You know these things about me. I honored you by making you the leader and tutor of all angels. What possible reason could you have for disobeying me?
Scholars and linguists say. that this question that Allah asked Iblees. has a tone of humility just by itself. But what makes it EXTREMELY humble is when you look at the context of who is asking who. The creator. The Rabb is asking his creation. The king of kings is asking his slave. That makes this statement. extremely humble. But that also highlights the relationship of our creator with his creation. Allah being the ONLY one worthy of pride. deals with his creation with extreme humility.  SubhanAllah!

Now lets play devils advocate for a second. Is it possible that Iblees was ACTUALLY confused? Is it possible that maybe Iblees. in his ignorance made a mistake. because of his observation of the physical properties of fire and clay? Is that possible?
It's not. He actually knew exactly why Allah had asked him to bow down to Adam. He knew perfectly well that Adam AS was superior to him in knowledge. and there was absolutely no reason for him to disobey. How do we know that? Because of this ayah. where Allah talks about Iblees and says.
وَإِذْ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟ إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ أَبَىٰ وَٱسْتَكْبَرَ وَكَانَ مِنَ ٱلْكَفِرِينَ
And when I commanded the angles . prostrate to Adam. They all did except Iblis. He refused, became arrogant, and was thus amongst the Kaafireen. So the word Kafir is used for Iblis in this ayah. In another ayah Allah says.
وَإِذْ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟ إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ كَانَ مِنَ ٱلْجِنِّ فَفَسَقَ عَنْ أَمْرِ رَبِّهِ
And when I commanded the angles . prostrate to Adam. They all did except Iblis. He was one of the Jinns and he transgressed or broke the Command of his master. So in this ayah the word Fasaqa is used.


Difference between KUFR and FISQ

So let's look at these two words.
Kafir comes from the word Kufr. which means to intentionally hide something. to hide a truth with intent. to deny a reality while realizing it. that's all Kufr. If you accidentally hide something. or you deny because you don't understand. thats not kufur.  that's Nisyaan.  Kufr is when one knows something and intentionally covers it up. You understand?
But Kaafir is the superlative form of the word which means someone who intentionally and constantly hides facts. It's not a one time thing. Kafir is someone who always. continuously. consistently covers things up.  That's why a farmer in Arabic is called a Kafir. because he has the seeds. and he hides them in the ground. He burries them in the ground. he covers it up with soil. and he does that for a living. So he does that over and over again.   So the one who covers up the truth.  constantly. consistently. intentionally is called a Kafir.

Faasiq comes from the word فِسقْ which means to break an agreement. To go out of bounds. But Faasiq. on the same phoenotic pattern as "Kaafir". means someone who ALWAYS goes out of bound. who intentionally and constantly transgresses.

So Iblees is Kafir AND Fasiq. He knew that Allah is his creator. He knew Allah is his Rabb. He understood that he was property and Allah was his owner. He knew the reality that Adam AS is superior to him. He still intentionally rejected his superiority. He knew his boundaries when it came to obeying Allah's commands. He knew his place in relation to the glorious position of Allah. Yet he INTENTONALLY transgressed.

He did both of these things. he rejected the truth. and he trangressed his boundaries. both through one single action. His disobedience.

So the problem was not that Iblees did not believe in Allah as his creator. An athiest does not believe in the existence of Allah. but Iblees did. His belief is clear in his own words.  He said:
خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
You created me! he does not just believe in Allah.  he acknowledges Allah as his creator. He's talking to allah and he is accepting Allah as his creator. His kufr. Listen to this very carefully. His kufr. his disbelief.  is not in.  I don't believe Allah exists.  His disbelief is in his diobedience. I'll say that 3 times. 
His disbelief is his disobedience X3

Why am I saying it 3 times. Because you and I too believe in Allah as our creator. but we still disobey Him all the time.  and we say.  it's not that bad.  At least I still believe in allah. It's not like I'm a Kafir! I know I do some very messed up stuff.  I know.  but its not like I'm a disbeliever.

The disbelief of Iblees was his disobedience.

Iblees doesn't need to get you and me to disbelieve. All he needs to do.  is to get us to disobey. Thats all he needs. That's all he is trying to do. You and I REALLY need to understand this.   Because at the end of the day.  after disobeying allah. all we say is. Hey! at least I believe in allah. that should be good enough for me. then guess what? Iblees believed in Allah too. he did exactly that. that's why I repeated that 3 times. The disbelief of Iblees. The Kufr of Iblees.   was his disobedience.  Because through his disobedience he intentionally rejected and covered up the truth.

And through his disobedience he became Faasiq. He transgressed his boundaries.  and he broke the agreement with Allah. Have we made an agreement with Allah? . Something called Ahad Shareef. A promise we made with Allah. to pray 5 times a day. fast. give zakaat. do good. refrain from evil. Did we make that agreement with Allah?. Iblees broke his agreement with Allah through his disobedience. What are we doing?

And the root cause of it all was arrogance. Once our ego gives birth to arrogance. disobedience will just naturally and inevitably follow. And that's why both the Istiaaza (Falaq and Naas) begin with what? Qul! Declare! Delcare your submission. And as we learnt. our declaration of our need. removes arrogance from our hearts. It humbles the heart! Because that is what we learnt Shaytan attacks.  الذی یوسوس فی صدور الناس . He attacks the chest of mankind. which contains what? . The heart! He instills arrogance and pride in our hearts through his whispers. 

So what got shaytan in trouble.  was not his disbelief in Allah. but his arrogance! His pride. What got him into trouble was his thinking. that he is better than Adam AS. What got him into trouble was his thinking. that he knows more than Allah. Cause Allah obviously doesn't know that fire is better than clay. right! Astaghfirullah!

His arrogance is what got him thrown out of jannah. But the greatest.  and sadly the MOST common sickness of our time. is Arrogance! And that's why you will notice all religious activities are designed around humility. They're are all exercises in humility. That's why when we pray.  what do we consntantly say? Allahu Akbar. Allahu Akbar.Allahu Akbar. Allah is greater!  Allah is greater! Allah is greater!.  Which means.  I am not! I am not! I am not! . And allah says when you disobey me. you are saying that YOU are greater! You think you are greater! that's disobedience! 
 

Attributes of clay and fire

Now scholars have presented  another beautiful dimension of how flawed Iblees was in his logic of fire being superior than clay. So now let's look at the statement in a different light. Iblees said.
خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
Let's first understand the meaning of the word Teen. Teen means damp mud. or damp dirt. It is commonly translated as clay. which is basically damp dirt. or damp soil if you will. In Urdu it would be translated to گیلی مٹی . or گارا .
Now there is another word in Arabic. Turaab. which means dry dirt. or dry mud. You add a bit of water to turaab and it becomes Teen. And BTW this word Turaab is also used in the Quran. On the day of judgment.
وَيَقُولُ ٱلْكَافِرُ يَلَيْتَنِى كُنتُ تُرَبًۢا
the kafir will say on the day of judgment. ٰٰI wish I was dry mud today. We'll look at this ayah in one of the future sessions InshaAllah!

So the first thing I want to understand is that Teen and Turaab are both the same thing. They're both dirt or soil.  Turaab is dry soil and Teen is damp soil. OK?  But we'll just call it clay. OK?

The argument Iblees made was based on a comparison of the external attributes of the substance they were made of. fire and clay. We talked about this earlier in some detail. He said fire is brighter. it is hotter. its flame rises. Clay on the other hand is dull. it is cold. and it falls to the ground. Therefore I am better than him! But what he intentionally chose to reject. what he intentionally chose to ignore and cover up. was that Allah did not ask the angels to prostrate before Adam until he blew his spirit into him. And soul is always greater than body. Spirituality is always superior to physicality. This is what we talked about the last time.

But now if we look at it. even from a physical stand point. Allah was completely JUST in asking fire.  to bow down before clay. Because even if the external attributes of fire may seem superior to that of clay. but the inner attributes.  and the inner qualities of clay.  are far superior to that of fire. The greatest reason is because clay is humble. It submits itself to the farmer who sows seeds within it. And because of its humility towards the farmer. soil allows for growth within it. It allows for new life to develop in its womb. It accepts and absorbs the water given by the farmer. and it uses that water to nurture the seeds.  into a fruit bearing tree. Fire on the other hand completely rejects water. There can be no growth. no development of life through fire.

That's the greatest and most important difference between clay and fire. It is the difference between humility and arrogance. The humility of clay or soil.  allows growth. it is nurturning. it is a source of life. It yields. it submits.
Fire on the other hand. only consumes.  and destroys and kills. It burns and destroys anything and everything that is placed within it. Try sowing a seed within fire. you're not going to get too far with it. But you sow those same seeds in soil. and it will give you back a tree loaded with fruits.

Clay. because of its humility.  can be moulded. it can be shaped into whatever form the creator desires. because it is humble. It submits itself to the hands of the potter. who shapes it in any way he feels is best. Clay is obedient. it does sajda.  because it submits itself to the will of the one its master allowing Him to shape it in whatever way He desires.  
Fire cannot be moulded. It cannot be shaped. Because it is disobedient.  it is arrogant. That's why clay is better than fire. We human beings. we were created from clay. which is supposed to be humble. Evil or sharr. which I told you comes from the word Sharara. a burning flame. its nature is arrogance.

Now is fire bright and luminous and attractive? Of course. that's why there is so much attraction in evil. That's why we are drawn towards evil. because of its bright dancing naked flames. it seduces us. it entices. mesmerizes us. it attracts us towards it. But once we get close. what does fire do? It engulfs us. burns us. destroys us. What happens to the most beautiful thing when it gets burnt? It becomes all black and charred and disfigured and distorted. That's what evil ends up doing to us. But in the beginning is it attractive? . Is it enticing? Absolutely! Partying all the time. drinking. smoking. watching filthy movies on the internet. Is there attraction in all of these things? Sure! Are their rewards immediate? . Do you get to have a good time right now? Sure!!. But where does it lead to? Where does that path end? Look at what alcohol evenutally lead to!. The person ends up being an alcoholic. He started drinking because it looked cool. But the same person. when engulfed and eaten and burnt by it. ends up becoming an alcoholic. What does the so COOL smoking eventually lead to? Cancer. Heart attack. Stroke.  Where does this shamelessness and internet filth lead to? Broken marriages. Where the only kind of relationship a man is capable of with his wife.  is what a moneky has with a female monkey. Honestly. examine any item that is prohibited in Islam. You will find two things in them. They will appear very attractive. and they will always end up in destruction. They all lead to one final destination. Destruction. Because that's what it is. FIRE!!! And fire as attractive and brilliant and beautiful it may seem. It burns. It incinerates. It always ends in pain and horror.

Now in comparison to that look at what soil does. Look at the job of a farmer. How attractive does farming or gardening seem? Not much. Seems pretty dull. pretty boring. tedious. doesn't it?.  The farmer keep investing time and effort. day after day. month after month.  and sees nothing. After months he see's something tiny sprout out of the dirt. It is extremely slow progress.  But when it comes time to harvest. what kind of yield does that soil produce? In tons! right? The fruits that are produced as a result of that slow. dull. hard labor. they have to be weighed in tons. And now what is the weight of those fruits.  in compairson to the weight of the seeds that were initially sown in the soil. No comparison. The reward that the farmer reaps at the end.  has no comparison to the intial trivial value of the seeds he sowed. Isn't that true?

Now do the rules of Islam seem dull? just like soil? Sure! Because Islam is exactly that. soil. And we are farmers planting the seeds of our belief in that soil. It's not the most attractive profession in the world. But when we sow the seeds of our belief and faith into it.and we water it with the knowledge given to us by our elders. our daat. And we farm them. cultivate them.  by striving day in and day out with our taharah, namaaz, fasts, zakaat, hajj.   What does that very dull soil give us back? Beautiful. lush. fruit bearing trees. Rewards that cannot even be compared to the initial investment.  But is it a long tedious. repetitive process? Sure! But look at the quantity and the quality of reward at the end.

The exterior of fire is beautiful. but its interior is destruction and death. The exterior of EVIL is beautiful. it is attractive. it is enticing. it is mesmerizing. But it will always result in pain and suffering and destruction in this life and the after life.
The exterior of clay is dull. but its interior is growth and life. The exterior of Islam. the exterior of Shariah may seem dull. it may seem inconvenient. demanding. but once we submit to it. willingly. in obedience. it's end result is immense growth. its end result is life. ultimate success in this life and the after life.

Fire brings death and destruction. Clay produces eternal life.

And that is what Iblees chose. He chose the external attraction. He preferred the external and immediate brilliance of fire.  to the internal essence of clay. And this is the lesson we have to learn from this story. We have to learn from this terrible mistake of Iblees. He chose the external form. over the internal essence. This duniya is fire. Listen to this very carefully. This duniya. this world we live in. it is FIRE.  for the one who wants immediate rewards. If you want to. what people call. ENJOY your life. Go right ahead! You'll get your immediate rewards. no doubt about it. And it'll feel amazingly good too. So if you are craving to commit those forbidden things. then go ahead. But just know. that it will end up in death and destruction in this life and the after life. Because this duniya is fire for the one who wants immediate rewards.
And this same duniya is clay for the one who is willing to defer his enjoyment. his pleasures for a incomparibly greater reward. This duniya is both fire and clay. It is now up to you and I. what we choose for ourselves. Iblees preferred fire and we know where that led him to. Adam chose clay and we also know where that led him to. Both paths are open for us.

And that's why using the Istiaaza. we declare our humility to Allah by seeking and entering his protection. from what? From the fire of Sharr. from the attractions of evil. because we realize. that even though shaytan's path is attractive. its brilliant. its bright. its mesmerizing. It ONLY ends up in destruction and terrible pain. the pain of heat. the pain of burning.  But once we submit to the protection of Islam. we restrain ourselves within the confines of Shariah. We sow our selves. willingly and in obedience. into the soil of Rabb AlFalaq. Rabb AlNaas. Malik AlNaas. Ilah AlNaas. the end result is magnificent. it is growth. it is beauty. The end result is delicious life giving fruits in the hereafter.




 


We're studying the story of Adam AS and Iblees through this passage from Surah Aeraf (7th Surah which means Hights. Or a place of elevated status). And something to realize is that even though we look at this as a primal story. the reality is that this story is still going on. This story of Adam AS and Iblees is still being played out in our lives.  over and over again. And this story.  is primarily about two characters. or two creatures. Adam AS and Iblees. Even though Hawwa is mentioned. but she is sorta joined in with Adam AS. Every place that Adam is mentioned. the word ھما is used. which is the dual form. implying both of them. So Allah says in Surah A'raaf.

وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ صَوَّرْنَكُمْ
And we created you both and fashioned you both.
ثُمَّ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟ إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ
and then we commanded the angels to bow down to you. They all did except Iblees.
لَمْ يَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّجِدِينَ
He was never going to be from among those who submit. We talked about in great detail what the word Sajda means. It is when the camel sits down . or submits itself. before its rider. and surrenders his control to him. The idea of Sajda being. to give up our will for the will of Allah.
So Iblees refuses to prostrate and so Allah asks him.

قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ
What possibly could stop you from prostrating to Adam when I commanded you to do so?
قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
He said. I am better than him. You created me from fire and you created him from clay. And we talked about the differences between fire and clay in quite depth in the previous session.
The two most important things to take away from this ayah.  is the realization of the fact that it was the arrogance of Iblees that lead to his disobedience. أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ. and then what followed was .خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ  . You created me from fire and you created him from clay. Which was his very logical justification.  for his disobedience.  The disbelief of Iblees was not that he didn't believe in Allah as his creator. The disbelief of Iblees manifested through his disobedience.

So almost in every single case. when we want to disobey Allah. when we want to disobey a command of Allah. which we in our heart of hearts know to be true. we will always come up with a VERY good. VERY logical justification for it. And that justification will almost always be rooted in this physical world. because what Iblees used as his justification were material objects. He said. I am fire and air. and Adam is earth and water. So the elements he used to justify his superiority were all material objects. they were all physical objects. He used مادۃ (material) to justify his disobedience. Which is what we do too if you think about it. All desires and pleasures that lead to the disobedience of Allah.  are all grounded in this physical and material world.  And that's a very powerful realization to have. Because a lot of times we can recognize our own disobedience.  by simply examining our justifications.

So allah says to Iblees... how dare you be arrogant before me...
قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا  ‎. Fall out of here.. Leave! I am casting you out...
فَمَا يَكُونُ لَكَ أَن تَتَكَبَّرَ فِيهَا  . You no longer deserve to stay in this place because of your arrogance. You cannot show pride here. In other words.  you are in the divine presence. This isn't the place for pride.  If you are aware of the glory of Allah. and if you know your place in relation to Allah.  you cannot possibly be in a state of pride before Him.
فَٱخْرُجْ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلصَّغِرِينَ. Get out of here. Because you are from among the Saghireen.  Saghireen comes from صغر or صغیر . which means small. Allah says because of your pride. By being prideful and arrogant. you put yourself UNDER the one you thought you were over. So your very thinking. that you are superior to this other creature.... is what made you inferior to him.  And then Iblees says.

قَالَ أَنظِرْنِىٓ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ
He says... give me some reprieve. Give me time.  till the day these people will be raised again... Give me until the judgment day . Once again. notice that Iblees not only believes in Allah as his creator.  he also believes in judgment day. So this is not an athiest who disobeyed Allah. This is actually a FIRM believer. This is a MOMIN (one who believes) who is disobeying Allah. And this is a VERY scray reality when you think about it. Because we claim to be momins too. we claim to be believers too. don't we?? Well. Iblees was a believer. And what made him Iblees. was his disobedience! . We are Allah's creation just like him. We diobey Allah too just like him. If his arrogance and disobedience turned him into Iblees that got him cast out of Jannah. why would that same justic not apply to us? . So this is a very scary reality if you seriously think about it. How are we any different? .  when we too disobey Allah. and come up with the most logical justifications to do it.

Allah says to him...
قَالَ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنظَرِينَ
Fine! I give you time till the day of judgment!

Wait. What?. What's going on here? Why is Iblees asking for time? and why is Allah giving him time? 

Before we answer these questions. Let's understand something else here. It is a very common misconception that Iblees or Shaytan is standing agianst Allah. That Iblees is somehow Allah's nemesis. (نعوذ باللہ من ذالک). That is ABSOLUTELY incorrect. Nobody can stand against Allah. Nobody has the capability to stand against Allah. Iblees is a creation of Allah. and by his own words he accepts that. And a creation cannot stand against his creator. So that's the first thing we need to understand. Iblees is not standing against Allah. Iblees is standing against Adam and the children of Adam AS. He is standing against us. He is our enemy. our nemesis. He is not Allah's nemesis. The only reason he is even being able to do what he does. is because Allah has allowed him to. He is doing what he's doing WITH Allah's permission.

Let's begin with the second part. Why did Allah allow Iblees this time.  in which he could misguide us. Wouldn't it have been awesome if he had just imprisoned Iblees right there and then?  So what made Allah accept the challenge of Iblees? Let's understand this part first.


Adam was created as vicergent
You See.  Adam AS . and even us.  as the the children of Adam. Banee Adam. we are Allah's very special creation.  That is why he called us his khaleefa... that's why he said to the angels. أنی جاعل فی الارض خلیفۃ. I am going to create my representative on earth... Khalifa comes from the word. Khalaf. or Yakhlufhu.  meaning succeeding someone or  taking one's place..  A person who takes the position or place of another person is called a khaleefa. or a caliph. or deputy. Another meaning of Khalifa is the one who has been fully taught. or fully trained. Because ONLY the one who has been taught. can now take the place of the teacher. I am a software developer. If I train and teach someone everything I know about software development. that person can then take my place. He can then step into my role. He can be my Khaleefa. you understand? Now did Allah teach Adam AS something? He did.وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا. Allah taught Adam AS all the names. Kullaha (EVERYTHING) is VERY important here. It is possible to teach someone some stuff. right? I can teach someone a few things about software development. but then that person cannot be my Khaleefa. He cannot be my representative. For someone to be a true representative. he has to be taught EVERYTHING.. You understand? If Allah had taught Adam AS a few things. He could not have been a khaeefa. The fact that he was taught him EVERYTHING. وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا . And Allah taught Adam ALL the names. is what made him a Khaleefa.

And this is the reason we claim that Maulana Ali was the TRUE KHALEEFA of Rasul Allah (SAS). because of this one fact.  that it was ONLY Maulana Ali that Rasul Allah taught EVERYTHING to. Did he teach things to Hazrat Abu Bakr, Hazrat Umar, Hazrat Usman as well? Sure! But did he teach them EVERYTHING? No! That's why we believe. that they could not be the true Khaleefa. the true successors of Rasul Allah. It was ONLY Maulana Ali that RasulAllah taught EVERYTHING to. And then himself testified to it.
انا مدینۃ العلم و علی بابھا، فمن اراد المدینۃ فلِیَاتَ الباب

And a examplory proof of that is that these 3 caliphs. Hazrat Abu Bakr, Umar and Usman. Each of them turned to Maulana Ali for guidance throughout their lives. Hazrat Umar said at least 70 times. from that which has been recorded in the Sunni books. It has been recorded at least 70 times.  لولا علی ھلک عمر . If it wasn't for Ali.  Umar would have been destroyed. All caliphs turned to Ali for guidance. And not anywhere we find in the seera of Maulana Ali . throughout history. be it the history books of Shias or Sunnis. where Maulana Ali turned to anyone for guidance except Allah. Just as we see we never find one event in which Rasul Allah turned to any human being for guidance except Allah. This was because he was taught EVERYTHING by Rasul Allah. thus making him the true representative. or true replacement of Rasul Allah after him.

Anyway. Returning to our topic. We were talking about why Allah gave Ibless time until judgment day.
Allah created Adam as his khaleefa by teaching him ALL the names. And then He honored him over angels by teaching HIM everything.  علم آدم اسمآء کلھا . And then he honored him again by asking the angels to prostrate to him....  Now you don't give that kind of honor to just anyone....  You don't give that honor to someone you hold to a low standard... So if he made angels bow down to him. And by his association.  to us. And not just bow down...  but prostrate.. Allah made angels prostrate before us.... That means Allah must have had some seriously high expectations from us!

And so when Iblees asked for time ... time to what? To misguide us...  to mislead us....  he granted him that time.. Why? Because Allah knew.  that he created us human beings out of his love. He blessed us with innumerable gifts. Intellect being the greatest gift of all. He surrounded us with His immense mercy. He then also sent us his message. this Quran. His messengers. His true Khulafa. His represntatives.  to expalin the Quran to us. to teach us EVERYTHING we need. And through their holy lives . he set living examples of these messages for us. In addition to all of this. he gave us the gift of free will.  the capability and the strength to stand against shaytann if we CHOSE to do so.... And then his protection on top of that. The Istiaaza.. to call upon Allah when things get difficult.

Think about it. He gave us capability though the intellect. freedom of choice. the guidance of Quran to distinguish between right and wrong. His messengers to explain the Quran to us and set practical working examples for us . And then on top of that. the Istiaaza.  to call upon Allah for His protection. Have you ever seen a more partial examiner than Allah? He's like this principal who sends teachers to teach his students everything. And then puts them in the examination room to take the exam.  and then stands in the room as the invigilator. He makes it an OPEN BOOK exam. Refer to the Quran all you want.  And then on top of that He says.  if you have problems in your exams. let me know. I'll help you. I'll give you the answers. Oh And BTW. When I grade your papers. I will be EXTREMELY lenient with you.  For every correct answer. I'll give you 10 points. and for every wrong answer. I'll deduct only one point.
Where will we find such a merciful. such a kind. such a helpful. such a lenient invigilator? Have you ever heard of an examiner like this?.  SubhanAllah. He literally gave us EVERYTHING. He covered all grounds for us. There's nothing left.

And now. after all this. if I still choose to fail His exam... then I don't deserve his rewards anyway.... just on the simple principle of justice.... Some have this christian mentality where we think ... oh he is Allah... He should be all merciful... He should just give us heaven regardless. Why do we need to prove anything?
How can that make sense?.  Where is the justice in that?
أَمْ نَجْعَلُ ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّلِحَتِ كَٱلْمُفْسِدِينَ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ
Should I make the one who believes and does good deeds.  equal to the one who creates mischief on this earth?
أَمْ نَجْعَلُ ٱلْمُتَّقِينَ كَٱلْفُجَّارِ
Should I make the pious equal to the wretched?

Do you want me to make an alcoholic lying cheating adulterer.  equal to an honest, pious, god loving.  god fearing momin...  Should I give them both the same reward?.  Even OUR sense of social justice would not accept that? Then how can we attribute this trait to the one who is THE MOST just of all? It just doesn't make sense...

So what we fail to understand is that when Allah gave Iblees time. who was Allah putting his trust in? Who was Allah honoring once again? He was honoring US. He was honoring us human being once again. He honored us by putting his trust in us. Just as he had honored Adam AS before us.
More than the ability of Iblee to misguide us. He trusted us MORE.  to NOT be misguided by him. Why? Because he gave us everything we need. It doesn't make any sense why we would choose Iblees over Allah. It makes no sense to Allah. That's why he said to Iblees. Fine! Do whatever you want. You will not be able to misguide my slaves.
What a disappointment we turned out to be!!

So that was the second part. Now the first part of this question. Why is Iblees asking time? Allah actually explains that in the next verse.

قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ
This is SO interesting. Iblees says.  because YOU misguided me. because YOU led me astray. Who is he talking to? He's talking to Allah. And look what he's saying. Because YOU led me astray. فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى . He is blaming Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) for his disobedience. Iblees is blaming Allah for his misguidance. Can you see the psychological state of this guy? Complete lack of responsibility. It's not MY fault. It's YOUR fault. YOU did this to me. You gave me a command that I was not able to obey. It's all YOUR fault. I am in this position today because of what YOU did to me.

Crazy huh?
 

Attack from all directions


Is it? Is it really crazy? Because we do it all the time. don't we? We displace blame all the time. Instead of taking responsibility for our lack of faith. Instead of taking responsibility for our lack of will power. we blame everything else.  and everyone else around us. It's my parents fault. Its my teacher's fault. It's this school system that is so terrible. It is Islam that is so difficult. It is SO inconvenient. Why do I have to pray 5 times a day. Why do I have to fast?.  Why do I have to pay Zakaat. It's MY hard earned money. Why do I have to give it to someone else? If Allah is SO powerful. Why can't he give it to them Himself? See. Always very logical justifications. If Allah is SO powerful. why doesn't he feed the poor. They are after all His creation? Why do I have to spend MY money??
Your money? Who gave you YOUR money? Your job? Why did you get that job? Because of your education? Who got you that education? Your parents? Who gave you those parents? And their jobs and their sustenance to enable them to get your education. which led you getting your job. which led you to make the money you make. ???

So Iblees says.
قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى
Because you led me astray. because of what YOU did to me.
لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ
I will now make sure I get them into trouble with you. I will mislead THEM from your straight path...  I will sit on your straight path... قعد  means to sit. But قعد with a laam... لَأَقْعُدَ . means to sit somewhere.  in order to ambush someboday....  You know like someone waiting behind the bushes with a baseball bat.  for his enemy to come out....  that's لَأَقْعُدَنَّ . So he said I will sit on your right path... waiting for them...  to ambush them.... Now someone who is waiting that way. does he expose himself? No he doesnt. And does he attack all the time... or at the right moment? He waits for the right moment.  and then he attackes... So all of that is captured inside  لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ . I will lurk on your straight path... Which straight path?. The straight path that they constantly seek guidance for. اھدنا الصراط المستقیم . Oh Allah guide me to the straight path. This is what we constantly ask Allah for in Surah Fateha.. Iblees says. I will misguide them from THAT very straight path.  they are asking guidance for. But I will not come out all the time....  I'll find that right moment...   and then I'll slip something in and slip out from there before they can realize what happened...

ثُمَّ لَآتِيَنَّهُم مِّنۢ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِمْ ۖ وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ
I will then come at them from right in front of them.... What is right in front of us? It's the straight path. that leads to jannah....  I will come to them and say don't go here... You don't have to wait so long for jannah man!. That's too far... Its too much of a walk.... Why tire yourself?.   You want pleasures right??...  I'll give them to you right here.... Why do you have to wait that long? I'll give you all of it right now !. And remember what we had talked about earlier... cash vs credit! Are we people of credit or are we people of cash? Iblees says I'll give you the benefits right here... In cash.. Immediately.... Jannah is credit man. Why wait?.  Who knows whether you'll even get the rewards or not! . I'm guaranteeing you all the pleasures right here. right now. You'd be so stupid to leave this visible cash. for that invisible credit. You see? Logic again.
وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ
and I'll come from behind them....  pulling them back.... They'll make progress and I'll pull them back.... Even if a million things are going well for them. when ONE things goes wrong. I'll be there. How could Allah do this to you?. Look you've been SO good. You've been so obedient. Praying 5 times a day. fasting.. giving charity. He took your loved one away? . He took your job away?. You stuided so hard. He got your injured and sick. He made you fail your exam? How could he do this to you? . This is the Allah that claims to love you so much?. Again. Logic!
وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِمْ
I'll come to them from the right and I'll come to them from the left.... Meaning, if they're in good company... doing good things... I'll attack them... If they're in bad company doing bad things I will still attack them.... Right hand is associated with good deeds... Left hand is associated with bad deeds.... He said EVEN when they are doing good things I'll slip myself in...  even when they are reading quran I'll slip myself in... that's why allah says فاذا قرأت القرآن فستعذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم.... when you are reading quran, first seek refuge of allah from shaytan...Why? I'm doing a good deed! Why do I need protection? What has shaytan got to do with a good deed?.  No I'll come at them even then...I'll attack them when they're doing good deeds, and I'll attack them when they're doing bad deeds... I wont' stop... I'll find the opportuntiy!
وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ
And then you'll see... You will see that most of them will be ungrateful to you....  You're not going to find most of them on your side at all...  In other words.  I will get them to obey ME...  and when they obey me...  they will disobey you and that means they are not grateful to you!

Now notice something here. Iblees says.
ثُمَّ لَآتِيَنَّهُم مِّنۢ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِم
I will come upon them from in front of them. and from behind them. and from their right . and from their left. What's interesting is that Iblees mentioned 4 directions. North South East and West. He mentioned 4 directions. But there are 6 directions. There is also top and bottom. But Iblees did not say that. He did not say. ومن فوقھم و من تحتھم . I'll come upon them from above and from below them. Why is that?

The reason for that is. and this is very interesting. what comes from above is revelation. And as long as you and I have a connection with Allah. through this revelation. he will not have access to us. He cannot cut us from Allah. unless we choose to cut ourselves from Allah. And he will not come from under us.  because that is a place of humility. It's a place of Sajdah. And Iblees is arrogant. He will never put himself under us. And so as long as we are humble. in the state of Sajdah. and connected to Allah through his revelation. Ibless cannot gain any access to us.
And BTW when does Shaytan flee according to the hadees? When you're in Sajda. because he cannot bear that. It reminds him of his own disobedience. Our Sajda. is proof of his failure. Because that is the very thing he wants to prevent us from doing. That is his end game. To prevent us from being humble. To prevent us from giving up our will for the sake of Allah's will. So when we do Sajda. He knows he is defeated.

Horiziontal vs vertical directions
So this top and bottom directions are very interesting. What this story is teaching us. is that if we place Allah in the right position. and we place ourself in our right position. which is.  that we see Allah over us. and we see ourselves under Allah . in prostration. in this state of submission. Shaytan has no access to us.
But as long as we're wandering around in this horizontal plain. which is this duniya. This duniya is the horizontal plain. As long as we're wandering in this horizontal plain. Iblees has complete access to us. But as soon as we connect with the vertical plain. Shaitan loses all access to us. That is why Allah created human beings upright. He created human beings.  vertical. on a horizontal plain.  Allah created us vertical. on a horizontal plain.
If you go horizontal. you're lying down on the job. Then Shytan gets in there. And that's why sleep is a very easy time for him to attack. That's why we do wuzu and have all these duas that we recite at the time of sleep.  So the key is. to always operate on this vertical plain. Always keep our actions aligned with the vertical plain. As soon as actions fall into the horizontal plain. for the duniya. Even if it is salaah. or Saum (fasting). as soon as it becomes horizontal. done to impress people. Iblees gets in there. And this is what happens when you decide to make a change in your life. As soon as you try to get vertical. he tries to bring you back to the horizontal plain. What about your friends? What will they say? What about your job? What about money? what about your house? What about kid's tuitions right? All concerns of the horizontal plain.


Iblees blames Adam for his humiliation
So this is what Iblees says to Allah. Now I always imagine.  if I was in the place of Adam AS. What would my reaction be? . My reaction would be like. Dude. What the hell? (Maybe not hell. ) What the heck?. What did I do? It was Allah who taught me EVERYTHING. It was His decision to make me his khaleefa. He taught me everything. He asked the angels to prostrate to me. You disobeyed Him. He's kicking you out. What did I do? What did I do in any of this. Why are you mad at me??? Comeon man. Angels. Adam. Bhai Bhai. You know.. I mean seriously. right? What did poor Adam AS do in all of this. Why is he so mad at him?

I'll give you an example so you can understand this. Let's say you and your sister (or brother) are playing video games... Its your turn to play.... but your sister is not handing you the remote control... You get upset about it and you start fighting about it with her....  Your parents walks into the room....  They find out what happened....  and they yell at your sister. You need to learn to share. You have no responsibility . You're supposed to be kind to your siter.  Shame on you. The whole 9 yards. And then they snatch the remote control from her.  and hand it to you .  and then they walk out...
Now even though your sister got in trouble with your parents... But who does she look at with eyes that are now shooting lasers?.  She blames you! Its all YOUR fault! I HATE you so much! Because of YOU! I got into trouble. Everything was fine before you came in my life!. Everything was great before YOU were born. My life was great!. You screwed up my life!. There is nothing wrong with me... I DONT HAVE AN ANGER PROBLEM. Its YOU that made me look bad.... You understand?

Iblees asks allah for time.... why? Because he got into trouble with Allah BECAUSE of Adam AS. because of this human species... He believes that had it not been for the creation of Adam.. he would always have retained his elevated status.... It doesn't make sense right? . But that's the thing. Iblees is insane. He's in a state of constant. never ending rage. And when you're angry, what happens? . You can't think straight.  So he now has this serious grudge against the human race... In his mind ... he blames us... Iblees was extremely close to Allah...  and now he has been humiliated because of the presence of who? Human beings! So he develops this severe hatred for human beings... so now he says.. Oh Allah... Let me prove to you.  that you made the wrong choice! Let me prove to you ...  you should not have honored them... You should have honored me!. I'll prove to you. that you made a mistake. I should not have been the one in trouble... THEY should be the one in trouble.. Just give me time until judgment day... and I will prove it to you! You will see that MOST of them are not going to be grateful to you.
وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ


And that's why he asks Allah for time.
قَالَ أَنظِرْنِىٓ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ
Give me time until judgment day . and I'll prove it to you. that they are not worthy of this honor you bestowed upon them.  Allah says
قَالَ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنظَرِينَ
Fine! I give you time till that day!

So Iblees challenges Allah. and He accepts his EVERY challenge? And why wouldn't He? It's not like Allah is scared of Iblees. But when Iblees challenges Adam and his children. Allah accepts to put them to the test. Because like I said. He gave them EVERYTHING they will ever need to meet this challenge. Why would they not choose Allah over Iblees?

And you know. in Hadees. this dialog between Iblees and Allah has been much further explained. Syedna Ghulam Hussain Sahab QR. he writes in his book Qatrunnida. He writes that Iblees actually didn't just ask for time. he asked for strength and power from Allah. Iblees said Allow me the power to dominate these human beings through their desires. Allah said.  I'll allow that for you. Iblees said. for every son that Adam has. allow me to have two sons. so that I am double in strength than them.  Allah said I'll allow that.. Iblees said. Allow me to make a home in the chest of the children of Adam. and allow my influences to flow through their lives.  just as their blood flows through their veins. Allah said I'll allow that. Iblees said. Allow me to attack them with my ground as well as air forces. meaning use both humans and jinn to attack them. so that we can mix and mingle into their wealth and to confuse them with false hopes and vain promises. Allah said I will allow that too.

When Adam AS heard all this. He sorta freaked out. Oh Allah. What are you doing? You've allowed Iblees and his army to become SO powerful. I and my children will get crushed under his attack. How are we going to defend ourselves against him?
Allah said. Don't worry Adam. With every child of yours. I will assign a protector. whose only job will be to protect him against the attack of Shaytan.  if he chooses to listen to him. (that's our conscience) . 
Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen. For every good deed that they do. I will record it as 10 good deeds . and every siin they commit. I'll record it only once. and if they repent on it. I will completely erase it.
Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen.Go Tell you children. to never despair in the mercy of their master. My mercy will always accompany them no matter how disobedient they are.
Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen.Go tell them I will never close the door of repentence on them. Till their very last breadth they will have the opportunity to repent and seek my forgiveness and when they do. I WILL forgive them.
