Adam says. Ya Allah give us more. Allah says. OK Listen. Go tell your children. that no matter how many times they repent and seek my forgiveness. I will keep on forgiving them over and over again. and I will not even maintain an account of how many times I've forgiven them for that very same sin. 
That's when Adam AS said. That's enough my master. What you have given us is now more than enough for us to stand our ground against Iblees and his army.

After accepting Iblee's challenge. Allah says.
قَالَ ٱخْرُجْ مِنْهَا مَذْءُومًۭا مَّدْحُورًۭا
Allah says get out of my paradise. with disgrace and as someone who has been expelled. Leave like someone who has been humiliated. and do whatever you want to do to misguide the children of Adam.
لَّمَن تَبِعَكَ مِنْهُمْ
Whoever follows you among them.... Now look. Allah didn't say whoever disbelieves in me....  that's not the condition he palced... The only conditioin he put here is that whoever listens to you... Whoever pays attention to you and follows you from among them..
لَأَمْلَأَنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنكُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ
I will fill hellfire with all of you together.

Wait. What???. Fill hellfire with all of you???? . Where did that come from? . Allah is talking about Iblees and his army. He should have said. I will fill hellfire with them. But he didn't say.  منھم اجمعین... . He said. منکم اجمعین. He doesnt' say all of THEM... he says all of YOU!.  This is actually لی الطوعیۃ to scare you.. لی التحدید  to challenge you ...  The one reading quran is like.. wait!. Where did YOU come from? I thought allah is going to say...  I will fill hell fire with THEM....  he says I will fill hell with you!.  You're reading the book and all of a sudden its pointing at you! Its pointing at you and me! Wait ME???? OMG I better not follow Iblees! Because the only way its pointing at me.. is if I follow Iblees.... So this switch in subject.  is actually a means of warning and terrifying us.... And its used all over the place in Quran.

Allah giving Adam everything

Now after expelling Iblees. Allah addresses Adam and Hawwa. and says

وَيَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ
Adam, you and your wife settle down in Jannah. Now notice this word Zawj. The word Zawj. actually means "companion". or partner. Allah referred to Adam and Hawwa as partners. The reason I'm pointing this out is because some men have this thinking. Some mother in laws have this thinking for their sons. that when it comes to their perfect sons. that husband wife relationship is a master slave relationship. It's not. If it were.  Allah would have said.  وَيَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَعَبدُک. Oh Adam. You and your slave settle down in Jannah.  He didn't say that. He used the word Zawj. partner. a companion.

Anyway. Allah says. ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ . And Allah did not even say Fil Jannah. meaning he did not point to a specific place or a location in Jannah. He said AlJannah... Meaning all of heaven.... Allah says your new home is Jannah itself..  You're not moving into one house. inside a city. within a state of Jannah. The whole thing is your house..  Every building there, every house there, every location there, all of it is your house. Adam and Hawwa. take it. Take all ofit !. And then he says .

فَكُلَا مِنْ حَيْثُ شِئْتُمَا
Eat and drink from whatever you desire! You don't have to check the label on any thing! Everything is haalal..  Eat and enjoy. And it's not like.  one thing is going to be like.. ahh..  That was not so good..  We should go to that one! That's us and restaurants..  Sometimes the biryani comes out good sometimes it doesn't. But in Jannah, eat whatever you want.. Everything is going to be AWESOME. ALL THE TIME. But then he says:
وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةَ فَتَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلظَّلِمِينَ
But do not go near this one tree or you will be from among the wrong doers.  Allah forbids them to go near one tree.... Not much attention is paid to the word هَذِهِ ... THIS tree! Allah did not say: تلک شرجۃ ... That tree! He did not say THAT tree.  He said THIS tree. What's the difference between this and that?.  This is near... So the harraam is always near ... the haraam. the forbidden.  is ALWAYS near.... Allah said to them. You have a LOT of options. in what is permissible.  But don't think the forbidden is far.  it's always going to be near..  And if it is near.  you have to watch out for it..  So you can never say I'm far from the haraam...  As big as this universe of Jannah is.  BTW how big is jannah? Allah says...
وَجَنَّةٍ عَرْضُهَا ٱلسَّمَوَتُ وَٱلْأَرْضُ
It's size is something like all seven heavens and the earth combined... The Size of jannah.  is the size of all seven heavens and the earth combined! And that would be something that compared to Jannah but not exactly... Today we have telescopes that provide us with magnification into the universe that humanity has never seen before....  And Allah says. this huge expanse still does not compare to the size of Jannah. And even though Jannah is so huge. Allah uses the word THIS to indicate the forbidden tree. He made this closeness. this accessibility to the forbidden. a part of the challenge for humanity.  That the forbidden will ALWAYS be close to you. It will ALWAYS be accessible to you.  and it will pique your curiosity!

I know it's Haraam ....I'm just curious! I'm not doing anything.  I'm just wondering! I wonder when beer tastes like? I'm never going to drink it! I just want to know what it tastes like!. I want to know what smoking feels like. I'll give it up after one. I'm just curious.  You know.  just wondering. Just wanna try it once.  So this is: وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةَ
And by the way.... something very interesting. Allah did not say. لا تأكل من هذه الشجرة.  He did not say. Do not EAT from this tree. He said. do not go near this tree. The command is not . Because it's not the tree we're interested in, right? We're interested in eating the fruit. Allah says don't even go near the tree. My command is not about the fruit. My command is for the tree. Do not even go near the tree. You know what that means? . It's not don't drink alcohol. It means don't even go near alcohol. It doesn't mean don't do drugs. It means don't even go near drugs. It's not don't get involved in shameless. It means don't even go near shamelessness.
And if you do. what happens?
 فَتَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلظَّلِمِينَ
You will become from among the wrong doers.
Look. We can't wrong Allah. We can't harm Allah. It's not like there is anything we can do to hurt Allah. But we can transgress on a Haqq. On a right of Allah. we can transgress on what is due to Allah. And what is due. is that Allah is obeyed when he tells us to do something. That is his right on us as our creator. and that is His right on us as our master and benefactor.

how did Iblees humiliate Adam?

فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ
Now this is the verse that I actually want to share with you. If we understand this.  then we understand the true intentions of Iblees.  Now so far.  we've established that he is our worst enemy.. Iblees or Shaytan hates us. and he is out for revenge. Now what was the worst thing that happened to him? He got kicked out? Yes!.  But getting kicked out of Jannah was the half of it!. The real thing is. when that happened.... how do you think he felt inside?.  He felt humiliated... and humiliation is one of the greatest pains that creation can suffer.... Any creation with dignity can feel humiliation.... Animals don't feel humiliated because they don't have any digntity....  Apparently Iblees had dignity too.... He had a sense of resepect for himslef.... And when he was thrown out of jannah.  he felt humiliated.... And for that humiliation he wants to take revenge against humanity...
Now what would be the ultimate revenge against humanity? Because if some how.  he could get human beings to get humiliated... If he could somehow do that... He can feel he has accomplished something...  So how does he do that? Through waswasa...

فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ
So shaytan does waswas to both of them....  Now what Allah could have said here is. فَوَسْوَسَ الیہم . Shytan whispered To them. But instead he said.فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا .  and the usage of lahuma . indicates a very specific intent. In other words Shaytan had a very specific goal here.فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا . He whispered to them for a very particular reason. I told you earlier. He does waswasa in SO many ways. In uncontable ways. Anger. jealousy. greed. pride.. contempt. so many different ways. But ultimate he has ONLY one single goal. What is that? Allah tells us as the ayah continues.    لی.... لِيُبْدِیَ لَھُمَا  ...

You notice this Laam before يُبْدِیَ . This Laam with a zer. This word لی has a mountain within it....  It tells us everything.... It tells us the ULTIMATE goal of shaytann...  Allah says.. فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ   Shaytan whispered to both of them... LEE.  for the reason....
Why do you think Shaytan whispered to them? What do you think was his ultimate agenda? Now I would guess.  Because he wanted them to disobey allah.... or Because he wanted to get them both kicked out from janna... or Because he wanted them to disbelieve.... or Because he wanted them to go to hell fire....  or because because because... right?
But Allah says let me tell you what his ultimate agenda was....

لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا

So that.  he could expose to them ... THAT which was covered of their ugliness. . .  Shaytans ultimate agenda.  was to get clothes removed from Adam and Hawwa AS....  That's what he wanted.... We really have to stop and think here.... I was thinking that Allah would say.... Shaytan wanted them to eat from the tree... right? Because Allah had said don't go near this tree! . Therefore I thought shaytan would want them to eat from the tree.... Allah says.. NO!.  That was not shaytan's real agneda....  His real agneda was humiliation... And he knew.  through his own personal expreience.  that disobeying allah would end up in humiliataiton.... And what would be the ULTIMATE form of humiliation? The ultimate humiliation would be....  that the greatest gift of jannah... The libaas... the clothes of jannah be removed from them.  Because if you are disqualified from jannah... What are you no longer qualified for? The clothes of jannah! 

The clothes that adam and Hawwa were wearing.  were the clothes of jannah...  Clothing was a gift from allah... It was the FIRST gift given to Adam AS to honor him.  because before him no one had ever worn clothes. Allah did not create us with clothes... When we come into the world... we do not have clothes on.... Animals are born with their clothes. Animals are born with their fur or leather or whatever. We are not. Clothing is the first GIFT our parents give us... by covering us and our private parts.... Because when Allah created human beings. you know what he said to the angels?.

وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ إِنِّى خَلِقٌۢ بَشَرًۭا. And when their master said to the angels. I am creating bashar. You know what the word bashar comes from? It comes from bishar... meaning skin....  Allah created a creature that was just skin... But then Allah clothed that creature... He gave him a gift of his own... that human beings were not originally created with... so clothing itself is a divine gift... and Shaytan wants those clothes removed...  Now let's look at the ayah. word by word...

لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا

لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا. so he could expose to both of them... مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا. what was covered up .. wrapped up .. and kept a secret... مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا. This word just bafles me... Allah could have used so many different words... من جسمیھما ، من اعضائھما ، من بدنیھما.. from their bodies.. from their body parts... but he said  مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا

سوئا is used in arabic for something that is ugly... Something that is disgusting... Something that is evil....  Humans beings explosed without clothes...  in public...  is something evil, something ugly...  something disgusting ...  It is something indecent inherently...  You know.. سوئا is also used in the Quran for a decaying corpse... Allah says..

فَبَعَثَ ٱللَّهُ غُرَابًۭا يَبْحَثُ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ لِيُرِيَهُۥ كَيْفَ يُوَرِى سَوْءَةَ أَخِيهِ

When qabeel killed habeel AS... Allah sent a crow to show qabeel how to hide the سوئا the decaying corpse of habeel AS...  A corpse is not something you wanna look at... It is someting that is inherently ugly...

And what better revenge. than to humiliate human beings by getting them to disboey Allah... Because what happens when we disobey Allah. What does it result in? وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ صَوَّرْنَكُمْ ثُمَّ قُلْنَا لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ ٱسْجُدُوا۟ لِآدَمَ فَسَجَدُوٓا۟ إِلَّآ إِبْلِيسَ لَمْ يَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّجِدِينَ
قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ ۖ قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
قَالَ فَٱهْبِطْ مِنْهَا فَمَا يَكُونُ لَكَ أَن تَتَكَبَّرَ فِيهَا فَٱخْرُجْ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلصَّغِرِينَ
قَالَ أَنظِرْنِىٓ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ يُبْعَثُونَ
قَالَ إِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنظَرِينَ
قَالَ فَبِمَآ أَغْوَيْتَنِى لَأَقْعُدَنَّ لَهُمْ صِرَطَكَ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ
ثُمَّ لَآتِيَنَّهُم مِّنۢ بَيْنِ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ وَعَنْ أَيْمَنِهِمْ وَعَن شَمَآئِلِهِمْ ۖ وَلَا تَجِدُ أَكْثَرَهُمْ شَكِرِينَ
قَالَ ٱخْرُجْ مِنْهَا مَذْءُومًۭا مَّدْحُورًۭا ۖ لَّمَن تَبِعَكَ مِنْهُمْ لَأَمْلَأَنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنكُمْ أَجْمَعِينَ
وَيَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ فَكُلَا مِنْ حَيْثُ شِئْتُمَا وَلَا تَقْرَبَا هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةَ فَتَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلظَّلِمِينَ
فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا


Deception of IBLEES - through Logic

وَقَالَ مَا نَهَىٰكُمَا رَبُّكُمَا عَنْ هَذِهِ ٱلشَّجَرَةِ
Iblees said to them. The only reason Allah prevented you from approaching this tree.  is because if you did that.  two things could happen.
إِلَّآ أَن تَكُونَا مَلَكَيْنِ
Either you would turn into angels. 
أَوْ تَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلْخَلِدِينَ
or you will become people who live in the janah forever.  And Allah obviously doesn't want that for you.

This logic sound familiar? The only reason my parents are stopping me from doing this is because. dot dot dot. Obviously they don't understand. Obviously they don't love me. right?

Now let's try to understand, what tempted both of them.  We already learned in Surah Baqarah.  Allah said :
وَإِذْ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلْمَلَٓئِكَةِ إِنِّى جَاعِلٌۭ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةًۭ
And Allah said to the angels, I am going to create a representative that is going to live on earth. Live where? . Earth. That was Allah's declaration right from the start. That I am creating a representative. a caliph for the earth. not for the heavens. not for Jannah. .  But Adam was living currently where? In Jannah.  And in Jannah, you would think that they would live forever.  But Allah said:
وَقُلْنَا يَٓـَٔادَمُ ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ
And Allah said to Adam, Settle! Settle here! ٱسْكُنْ . Allah did not say اُخلُد فیھا.  Those of you who read the quran. You know how when Allah describes a Jannah, he does not say فیھا ساکنین ،  instead what does He says فیھا خالدین .khalid means to live for ever! .

So when Allah described the creation of Adam to the angels. He said I'm creating him for the earth. And also when he spoke to Adam and Hawwa about their stay in heaven. He said. Settle here!. ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ ٱلْجَنَّةَ and the word sakana actually comes from sukoon. Not the urdu sukoon. بڑے سکون سے بیٹھے ہوئے ہیں۔ . not that sukoon.  When you learn to read the quran.  there is fatha, kasra, damma, shadda and sukoon.  what is sukoon? When you temporarily stop moving.  you stop temporarily on the letter that has sukoon on it.  so sukoon means to stop temporarily.  So there was motion before as you were reading.  and then you stop.  That does not indicate necessarily.  that the stop is permanent. If the stop was permanent.  than the word used would have been: خُلد. You understand?
Instead of saying. ٱسْكُنْ أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ . Allah would have said أُخلُد أَنتَ وَزَوْجُكَ. So when Allah announced to adam AS and his wife Hawwa. Settle down here.  He said stop here.  But he did not say stop here forever.  And He already did announce to the angels earlier.  that I am creating Adam for where? for the earth.  إِنِّى جَاعِلٌۭ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ خَلِيفَةًۭ
 
So the ANGELS. actually knew.  that Adam AS was created.  not for Jannah.  but for the earth.  They knew that he is going to play that role until he finally makes it back to Jannah.  This was all part of Allah's original plan.  Now even though the angels knew. Did Adam AS know that? . NO!. Because all this dialog. between Allah and the angels.  happened BEFORE Adam was created. So the specific details about their eventual residence. the angels knew. Iblees knew. But Adam and Hawwa did not know. Because when Allah made this announcement to the angels, they hadn't been created . But when Allah spoke to both of them. and told them to settle temporarily in jannah. they knew that their stay in Jannah is temporary. and not permanent.  You understand? . They knew their stay is temporary. but they had no idea that they were never created for Jannah in the first place.  And that is what Iblees took advantage of.
 
So Iblees came to Adam, and said.  Hey guys! Listen.  The two conditions for people who get to live in jannah forever are. إِلَّآ أَن تَكُونَا مَلَكَيْنِ  . either you are angels.  OR  أَوْ تَكُونَا مِنَ ٱلْخَلِدِينَ you need to have permanent residence.  You need to have a green card in order to live here.  Now you are clearly not any Angels!.  Therefore the only way that you can live here.  is that if you get a green card.  And the way to get that green card.  the way to get that permanent residence.  is to eat from this tree. Because the permanent residents are called Khalideen.  So if you're not an angel.  and I'm pretty sure you're not going to become an angel anytime soon. so the ONLY other option you have. the only play you have.  is that you apply for a green card.  And the way to do that is what? . Eat from the tree.  That is IF you like Jannah!. That's all I'm sayin.  I'm sure you enjoyed a little bit here didn't you? .  Look man!. I mean well! I'm your friend! and I really like you guys.  I want you to stay in Jannah! . But unfortunately.  the only two options that you guys have.  is to either be an angel.  which is obviously not gonna happen .  or you eat from the tree . So the way I see it. you guys really don't have a choice.

So this is how Iblees approached them. With logic of survival. You see. This is the greatest challenge of all. Iblees comes with perfect logic that is grounded in the seen. and he makes that conflict with faith that exists in the UNSEEN. He makes us choose between cash and credit. making CASH. the only SMART choice. That's a REALLY CRAZY challenge. a REALLY CHALLENGING test we as human beings are put into.

So this is how Iblees tries to confuse them. But they both don't believe him. So what does Iblees do? He swears to both of them.
وَقَاسَمَهُمَآ إِنِّى لَكُمَا لَمِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ
And then he swore to both of them that I am from your well-wishers. Iblees swore to them by Allah. اُقسِم باللہ.
Now you see. this is Iblees. He'll go to any lengths to do what he needs to do. So he lies to both of them. And you have to understand something here. Adam and Hawwa. they did not have any concept of lies. All they ever knew was the truth.  Because they had never heard anyone lie before. And also in this ayah. Iblees says.
إِنِّى لَكُمَا لَمِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ
Now in balagha. in Arabic rheoteric. when you say أِنی. انی یقول ھذا. That's called مُترَدِّد. means you're speaking to someone who is doubting you. He's not sure. maybe he believes you . maybe he doesn't. So when you use انی . It's like saying. I know you doubt me. but I'm assuring you that I'm telling you the truth. But when you use a Laam. the second time along with Inni. .إِنِّى لَكُمَا لَمِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ.  He didn't say. مِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ . He said. لَمِنَ ٱلنَّصِحِينَ . That's for someone who does not believe you AT ALL. So Iblees used that to say. I know you don't believe me AT ALL. but I'm swearing to the utmost. that I'm telling you the truth. That's the language he's using. In other words. believe me. I swear I'm sincere with you.
Now here's two people who don't even know what a lie is. because they're in that pure state. and then they see this creation of Allah. swearing by his creator. وَقَاسَمَهُمَآ. It was simply unthinkable to them . that somebody could swear by Allah and lie. That was something that was completely unthinkable to them. . that's what they fell for. Iblees tempted them for the longest time.  as we'll learn in the next ayah. They did not immediately fall into temptation.  But when Iblees swore by Allah.  they believed him. That's how he got to them. The point is Iblees will go to any extremes.

We think. how could he deceive me. How could she wanna hurt me?. She's my best friend. He's my best friend. NO. You can't put anything past Shaytan. Or someone who is under the control of Shaytan.  He'll go to the most extreme ends to do what he needs to do.

فَدَلَّىٰهُمَا بِغُرُورٍۢ

دلا in arabic is a verb.  تدلیۃ . the infinitive verb is actually used when you have a bucket.  and you have a rope attached to that bucket.  and then you pull the bucket slowly. little by little by little. If you pull it immediatley. if you pull it hard and fast.  it's ادلا.  if you pull it slowly. then its دلا . In the story of Yusuf AS when his brothers left him in a well. a caravan passed by and put a buket in the well for water.  and when they pulled it out.  a boy came out sitting in the bucket. in that ayah what did Allah says.
وَجَآءَتْ سَيَّارَةٌۭ فَأَرْسَلُوا۟ وَارِدَهُمْ.  فَأَدْلَىٰ دَلْوَهُ
Here the word Adlaa is used. implying that they pulled the rope hard and fast. and the bucket.  with the boy in it came up rather quickly. Now you and I know a boy is not that light. so it must still have taken some time to pull it up right? But that is still ادلا. . But when Iblees is described figuratively.  that when he took adam and hawwa AS . and he yanked them out of jannah.  like a bucket is pulled out of a well.  Allah uses the word دلا . meaning.  he took his sweet time.

You guys are like modern age kids.  I don't know if you ever watched old school cartoons like Tom and Jerry!. Tom is a cat. Jerry is a mouse. Tom has a piece of cheese in a bucket.  and there is a rope tied to the bucket.  Jerry smells the cheese and then as he approaches the bucket.  Tom slowly pulls the bucket towards him.  and then a little more, and a little more. and a little more. And Jerry does what?. He keep walking towards Tom until he finally catches jerry.  So Tom is using the bucket.  to lure Jerry. very very slowly. very unnoticable.    That in Arabic is called دلا

In other words. Iblees didnt just walk up to them and say Hey! That fruit on that tree. .aaaa haa haaa haaa. so tasty man!!. Eat it . Do it! Do it!. It didn't happen that way. And it's also not like he walked up to them and said. Hey you! Eat from that tree. and they both said.  Ahh OK! No no no no no. He did waswassa to them over and over and over again. he came in the morning. he came in the evening.  he came at night. Hey! You hungry? you guys hungry? I know this one tree. Now jannah has countless trees . right? Jannah is way bigger than the earth. so how difficult would it have been to find this one haraam tree? Think about that!. Of all the trees in the entire universe of jannah. there is one that is haraam. And shaytan had to first GPS them back to that one haraam tree.  little by little.  Hey why don't you take this turn? why don't you go over here? Hey check those strawberrys out. they look pretty yummy. don't they?. Drink from this river. it's so sweet. 
So دلا  suggests.  he didn't immediately call them to the haraaam.  He got them to it very slowly.  in a calculated manner. Hey. checkout this water fall. go to that mountain. taste this mango. then go over here. then go over here.  And they're listening to him. and they're thinking this has nothing to do with what? Tasting the tree
Then Allah says.

فَلَمَّا ذَاقَا ٱلشَّجَرَةَ
So they eventually. BTW. اذا when they did it. حین when they did it. .  فلما Eventually when they did it. so again.  this didn't happen immediately.  ذَاقَا ٱلشَّجَرَةَ both of them tasted the tree .  Now a lot has been said about not going near the tree!.  Don't go near the tree!.  And now allah says they both eventually tasted the tree.  Have any of you tasted a tree before? Have any of you been tempted ever to taste a tree.  What is on a tree that you are tempted by? It's the fruit! The fruit of the tree. Not the tree itself!. And typically is the fruit easily accessible? No it's not! Fruit is usually hanging on a branch.  The tree itself may be accessible.  You can touch the bark of a tree.  But to get to the fruit, you've got to climb a tree. And then get to the fruit.  Did Allah tell Adam. Do not eat the fruit? Did he say, do not approach the fruit? No! . Did he say, do not climb up on the tree? No! . He said do not go NEAR the tree! فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ

In Surah Isra we learn that  فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ turns for humanity into ولا تقرب الزنا.
لا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ turns into لا تقرب الزنا. We will inshallah talk about that later.

So when Allah says. فَلَمَّا ذَاقَا ٱلشَّجَرَةَ. So they tasted the tree. Meaning they didn't even get to the fruit. The implication is just by reaching out to the tree. they diobeyed Allah. because the command of Allah was not to approach the tree. And Iblees made them approach the tree. This is VERY important to understand!. You know why? Because as revelation proceeds. فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ . turns into

وَلَا تَقْرَبُوا۟ ٱلزِّنَىٰٓ.  إِنَّهُۥ كَانَ فَحِشَةًۭ وَسَآءَ سَبِيلًۭا
Do no go near Zina. Indeed it is the most extreme form of shamelessness. and the ugliest path to walk on. Do you see the usage of the word Saa'a here? Ugly? Remember what Iblees wants?. To remove our clothes and expose our what? Ugliness.  ?? Allah does not say do not commit zina. do not commit adultry. He says. Do not go near Zina. Do not go near adultry. What does that mean? Don't even take the first step that will eventually. Falamma. lead you to zina.

So they both tasted the tree. and then what happened?
بَدَتْ لَهُمَا سَوْءَتُهُمَا
their ugliness got exposed. Iblees completed his mission. What did Allah say Iblees wanted?. Why did he do waswas? What was his ultimate goal?
فَوَسْوَسَ لَهُمَا ٱلشَّيْطَنُ لِيُبْدِىَ لَهُمَا مَا وُۥرِىَ عَنْهُمَا مِن سَوْءَتِهِمَا
He whispered to them IN ORDER TO expose their ugliness to them. And now Allah says. He was sucessful in doing what he intended to do. He got their clothes removed. He got them dishonored before Allah. Iblees got their ugliness exposed. The clothes of Jannah is what made them look beautiful.  and the removal of those clothes.  exposed their underlying skin.  which is referred to as ugliness. سوئا .  Because it is unnatural for human beings to be naked. especially After Allah honored them with the gift of clothes.

وَطَفِقَا يَخْصِفَانِ عَلَيْهِمَا مِن وَرَقِ ٱلْجَنَّةِ
So now they are trying to wrap themselves using the leaves of Jannah. A state of desperate humiliation.

And Allah calls upon them.
وَنَادَىٰهُمَا رَبُّهُمَا
أَلَمْ أَنْهَكُمَا عَن تِلْكُمَا ٱلشَّجَرَةِ وَأَقُل لَّكُمَآ إِنَّ ٱلشَّيْطَنَ لَكُمَا عَدُوٌّۭ مُّبِينٌۭ
Did I not forbid both of you from that tree? Did I not tell you both.  that no doubt. Shaitan is your clear enemy?. Did I not tell you that?  Why did you go back there? . Notice how Allah says here. THAT tree.  What did he say before? فلا تقرب ھذہ الشجرۃ. he used the word THIS. ھذہ .  He said this tree! But now Allah says that tree. تلک الشجرۃ . Did I not forbid you from THAT tree.  In other words. you both were doing so good. you were getting further and further away from the forbidden. Why did you let Iblees rope you back to it? . Why did you have to come close to that tree again?.  You had gotten away from it.  You weren't even tempted by it. Why did you go back? And had I not said to you, that Shaytan is your clear enemy? Why did you believe him? . Even if he swore to you. Even if he gave you all the rational logical explanations of the world. Why did you choose to believe him over MY command? . Why did you choose to trust HIM over ME??. What we're learning here.  is that Allah's command supercedes ALL of Iblees's logic.

Now does this mean we don't use logic? . Of course not. Use All the logic you need to come to the conclusion that Allah is your master. Take all the time you need. Make use of ALL the signs Allah has created. both inside and outside of this book. Use your intellect. Use you heart.
Allah says. Take as much time as you need.  to come to the conclusion that I am your master!. But once you've come to that conclusion. then submit to me. And what does submission mean? . Giving up MY logic. to the will and command of my MASTER. That's true submission. Ya Allah. I accept.  I admit. that nobody else is my master. You are my one and only master. لا الہ الا اللہ . I have NO master except you!. And now I submit my intellect. my logic. my will. to YOUR logic. to YOUR intellect. to YOUR comamnd. That is true submission. That is true Sajdah. Just as the camel submits to its master. I will not longer go wherever I want to go. Once you're on my back. I will go wherever. YOU want me to go. That's sajdah. But that requires immense amount of trust. So study the message. Study the miracles. Understand how and why all this is beneficial ONLY for you. That's why I sent this message in the first place. That's why I sent my messengers. to explain everything to you. But once you submit. then give up your logic to go aginst my commands.

You know. when you join college. and you have multiple offers. you have options. You can pick which school you want to join. When you apply for jobs and you get multiple offers. You have options. You can pick which job you want. You can take the tour. You can visit your college. Look at the class rooms. meet the teachers. look at the acedemic structure. You can talk to other graduates. With a job. you can visit the building. meet with other employees. Find out what's what. You have that option. But once you accept an offer. Once you join the school. or accept the job. Once you sign the dotted line. do you still continue investigating? No. Because you made a very conscious choice before you joined that institution. Now you happily do whatever is required of you. Isn't that true? . Same with religion. It's really not such a difficult thing to understand.

The thing with Iblees is. He will not prevent you from joining Islam. Once you've joined. He will force you to use YOUR own logic. against the commands of Allah. He'll make you think of the most perfect arguments.  based on your incomplete knowledge of the facts. mixed in with your experential biases. and he will make you submit to your desires. and your passions and your caprice. that will go against the commands of Allah.
This is what he did with Adam and Hawwa علیھم السلام . He got them to disobey Allah AFTER they signed the dotted line. He got them to lose their clothings. He got them to get dishonored before Allah.  He brought them down from the ultimate honor. where angels are prostrating before them. to this level of humiliation where they are patching themselves up with leaves. There is remarkably imagery here.  Look at their state of desperation. Trying to patch themselves with leaves. Can you imagine that helplessness.  Allah didn't put them in that state did He? NO. He was the one who robed them with beautiful garments of jannah.  He put clothes on them. And then he also warned them! Look don't follow Shaytan! He's your enemy. He's going to try to get you out of jannah. Don't let him fool you!

But they didn't listen.  they disobeyed allah.  The natural consequence of which was their honor being removed from them.  and now they're helpless . trying to hide themselves again. with leaves. How can the inferior leaves compare with the robes and beautiful garments of jannah.  A picture of intense desperation is illustrated here. How desperate we as creations are in need of our creator. If he takes his blessings away. look at what pathetic state we would fall to. SubhanAllah!  And look at what state Iblees wants to bring us down to. (نعوذ باللہ من الشیطان الرجیم)

And so Allah repremands them. Did I not ask you to stay away from that tree? Did I not warn you that Shaytan is your clear enemy?

 

Difference between reactions of Adam and Iblees

قَالَا رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَآ أَنفُسَنَا
They said, master we have wronged ourselves. Now they are both crying.  they're repenting and they're saying.

Master . we have wronged ourselves.
وَإِن لَّمْ تَغْفِرْ لَنَا وَتَرْحَمْنَا لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ ٱلْخَسِرِينَ
and if you don't forgive us. for OUR mistake.  and you don't have mercy on us. we will definitely become from the losers.

Now in this ayah.  we also learn about this staunch difference between Adam and Iblees.  They both disobeyed Allah. They both disobeyed Allah. They both disappointed Allah. Iblees was asked to do something. that he didn't do. Adam and Hawwa were asked NOT to do something. which they did. Both forms of disobediences occurred in this story. What we learn from this story is that disobedience to Allah. happens in both forms. There is disobedience of commission. and there is disobedience of omission. There's disobedience. when we don't do what we are commanded to do by Allah . And there is disobedience when we DO . what we are are commanded NOT to do. That's the first thing.

But the greatest lesson in this story. is their response to their disobedience. It's an incredible lesson. Iblees disobeys Allah. Allah asks him why did you disbelieve?
قَالَ مَا مَنَعَكَ أَلَّا تَسْجُدَ إِذْ أَمَرْتُكَ
Why did you now prostrate. when I commanded you to do so?. What was his reply?
ۖ قَالَ أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ
I am better than him. You created me from fire and you created him from clay. right? Arrogance was his reply. Justifications for his disobedience was his reply. Rationalization was his reply. Coming up with justifications to continue a life in sin. THAT is what's disasterous.  It's not possible for us human beings NOT to sin! It's part of our nature. it's part of our very fabric. That's what it all boils down to.  Do we choose to persist in that act or not. That's the measuring stick.
If we choose to persist. If we choose to justify. If we choose to rationalize. If we choose to NOT take responsibility and blame others.   then that's arrogance. That's the path of Ibless. So what if I smoke? Everybody smokes! So what if I drink? Everybody drinks! وَلِبَاسُ ٱلتَّقْوَىٰ ذَلِكَ خَيْرٌۭ. ذَلِكَ مِنْ آيَتِ ٱللَّهِ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَذَّكَّرُونَ
That is from the great signs of allah.  so that they can make an effort to remember allah. To remember Allah. EVERY single time we put on clothes. EVERYTHING I have shared with you about the Istiaaza. EVERYTHING is supposed to flash through our minds.لَعَلَّهُمْ يَذَّكَّرُونَ . So that you can remember Allah through clothing. When I put on my clothes. I am supposed to remember this is an HONOR for me from Allah. Just as I am covering up my shame. my ugliness with clothes. I need to cover up my soul in piety. I have to protect myself from Shaytan. who is going to try to remove my clothes. Not directly by taking my clothes off. But by putting me on a path. that will result in my clothes being removed before Allah. SubhanAllah.


then he says.
 
يَبَنِىٓ آدَمَ لَا يَفْتِنَنَّكُمُ ٱلشَّيْطَنُ كَمَآ أَخْرَجَ أَبَوَيْكُم مِّنَ ٱلْجَنَّةِ
Oh children of adam. don't let shaytan do to you. what he did to your parents. In other words. learn the lesson from the story of your parents that happened before you. The arabs say.
السَّعِیدُ مِنَ الطَّعَتْ بِغَیرِہِ
True happiness is for the one who learns his lessons from other people. They don't have to prove those lessons for themselves. This is the idea that those who don't know their history. are condemned to repeate it over and over again.
This is why we're being told this story. because with us on this earth. there is this struggle that is going on. And there are two components of this struggle. YOUR desire. Because if you didn't desire the thing in the first place. then nobody could convince you to even try it. So YOU and I have this thing called ھوی. Caprice or desire. and then there is an unseen element working in the world . which is suggesting to us. to explore that hawa. to test it. to try it. That's ذوق. or ذاق. The desire to check it out. see what it is like. That's what got our parents expelled from Jannah.

You see they had the desire in them to live in Jannah forever. If they did not have that desire. they would never have listened to Iblees. EVEN when he swore before them. they wouldn't have listened. If they had NO desire. But they DID have that desire. and Shaytan made them explore it. But it was just the taste. the Zawq. that constituted as their disobedience.

And then Allah says.
يَنزِعُ عَنْهُمَا لِبَاسَهُمَا لِيُرِيَهُمَا سَوْءَتِهِمَآ
He pulled off their clothes. so that he could expose their ugliness . Look at these words. يَنزِعُ .  he pulled off their clothes. The word نزع means to pull out. You know how when someone is about to die.  in their last moments . they say he is in the state of نزع .  It means his soul is being pulled out of their body.  This ayat says.  Shaytan pulled their clothes off of them. Now that would indicate that Shaytan had more power over them! Yes or no?.  Suggesting to take off clothes is something else.  pulling off clothes is something else.  So how come Allah says Shaytan pulled off their clothes?
This ayah is teaching us. and please listen to this very carefully. This ayah is teaching us that diobeying allah.  grants authority to shaytan. Disobeying allah.  grants power to shaytan over us. Evertime you and I dress inappropriately. in both the physical and spiritual sense.  we give more and more power to shaytan.  Shaytan gets more power over you and me. 
EVERY single time we disobey allah.  the more we disobey Allah.  the more shaytan gets power over us.  until the point where he can simply tell us what to do.  and we comply like his slave. He will simply command and we will obey. 

The only power Allah had gave shaytan ORIGINALLY. was to do waswasa. to whisper.  but WE give him the real power of command.  by accepting.  listening to and complying with his whisper. And the more we do it. the more power he gets over us. He keeps getting strong and stronger and stronger. until he gains complete authority over us. He can now simply command us to do something. Because Allah says.

ٱلشَّيْطَنُ يَعِدُكُمُ ٱلْفَقْرَ وَيَأْمُرُكُم بِٱلْفَحْشَآءِ
Shaytan promises you bankrupcy . bankrupcy where? Before allah!.  He promises that by the time you stand before Allah.  I promise.  you will not have a single good deed to your name.
   يَعِدُكُمُ ٱلْفَقْرَ    and how does he do that?  وَيَأْمُرُكُم بِٱلْفَحْشَآءِ ۖ  . He commands you to ludeness. to shamelessness. Allah didn't say
یُوَسوِسُ لکم الفحشاء . یَنسِحُو لکم ان تفشحو  .
He suggested ludeness to you. He whispered to you. No no no no no.  Allah says. He said he COMMANDS you to shamelessness.  How does he command you? People have come to me and said. I can't stop watching porn.  I can't stop smoking.  I know you can't!.  Because shaytan is commanding you! Cause you keep disobeying Allah. You have to cut it off. That's the only way for shaytan to let go of you.  is you've got to stop. You and I have to take back that control. by giving that control to Allah. where it belongs.  because Allah said to the shaytan.
‏إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ
You will have no authority over my slaves. what does that mean?. If they're not really MY slaves. you will have complete authority over them.  ‏إِنَّ عِبَادِى لَيْسَ لَكَ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَنٌ. this is our legacy in this world.

Then Allah says.

إِنَّهُۥ يَرَىٰكُمْ هُوَ وَقَبِيلُهُۥ مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا تَرَوْنَهُمْ
He is constnatly watching you. He and his tribe of followers.   Did he not say to allah that he will sit on the straight path. waiting to ambush us?. And when somebody is waiting to ambush can you see them or no? Allah says I made that part of your test! He is watching you! He and his entire tribe.  مِنْ حَيْثُ لَا تَرَوْنَهُمْ. from a place wher eyou can't even see them.
إِنَّا جَعَلْنَا ٱلشَّيَطِينَ أَوْلِيَآءَ لِلَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ
All the devils. and legions of them have made friends with people who don't believe.  People who don't believe will accept that whisper. and they will enjoy that whisper.  The guy will say.  my parents aren't home right now. I can watch whatever I want. I can do whatever I want. Nobody will ever know. I can smoke. I can take a tic tac later. Nobody will know.  Allah will know.

So after narrating the entire story of Adam and Iblees. Allah talks to us. the children of Adam. and warns us. Don't repeat the same mistake your parents made. Don't listen to Shaytan. He got your parents kicked out of jannah. He will do the same to you. So be careful. don't repeat the same mistake. I warned them too. they didn't listen. I'm warning YOU now. Be careful!. Don't disobey me. And if you do end up disobeying me. then follow the pattern of your parents. by accepting your fault. by accepting accountability for your actions. and then after taking complete responsibility for your action. repent before Allah. Don't follow the pattern of Iblees and come up with logical reasonings to justify your disobedience. Because he will entice you. He will attack you. And once you give him power by your constant disobedience to me. and your constant obedience to him. he will then make you his slave. He will command you to sin. and you will comply. Because he wants to dishonor you before Allah. He wants to take off your clothes. Clothing. that I have equated with revelation. Clothing for your body as well as your soul. I have made physical clothing. not just a covering for your ugliness. but also means of adornment for you. So that you can look beautiful. And I have made piety. taqwa. a clothing for your soul. so that it not only covers up your sins . but also adorns your personality and makes you respectable before Allah and his creation. And this spiritual clothing of taqwa is better between the two. وَلِبَاسُ ٱلتَّقْوَىٰ ذَلِكَ خَيْرٌۭ . Why? Because in order to be pious. you will need to dress appropriately. You will need to dress modestly. You can't dress in a lude manner and be pious. That's why it is better between the two. Also because it adorns your soul. which is going to return to me. Your body is going to decay in the dirt. So what's more important is the clothing of the soul. But you can't have one without the other.

And how do you create this spritual clothing? What's the raw material for you to create this spiritual clothing?. this taqwa. It is this revelation. That's why I sent down revelation. and I sent down clothing.

Nothing has to happen overnight. Farmer and seed.

we are toddlers in the eyes of Allah.

Allah created us in comfort

Allah says in the Quran to human beings.
وَلَقَدْ مَكَّنَّكُمْ فِى ٱلْأَرْضِ وَجَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَعَيِشَ.  قَلِيلًۭا مَّا تَشْكُرُونَ
We settled you down on the earth. and we gave you good housing. Makanna means good housing.  and especially for you وَجَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ . especially for you.  we put all means on this earth so that you could live well.  معایش  is actully from معیشۃ which means life that is well lived.  in urdu we use this word عیش . .
بڑے عیش سے رہ رہے ہیں. That's an arabic word.  means to live very well. العیش have is a good life. Allah say we put means of a good life for you on this earth. So that's the first misconception addressed. People think Islam has so many rules.  it doesnt want us to live a good life. Allah doesn want us to enjoy ourselves. Allah is telling us. that he created us on this earth in order for us to have a good life.
You know this same word عیش is used to describe the paradise. فھو فی عیشۃ راضیۃ. They will live a great life in jannah. And there is a glimpse of that even in this world. There are glimpses of معائش  . means of living really really well on this earth. enjoying ourselves.

And by the way.  where does enjoyment come from? Enjoyment happens when you get what you desire. X2.
It's very simple.  you have a craving.  and you fulfill that craving and that is what enjoyment is. I'm really craving to play some tennis. I got to play. I enjoyed myself. I'm craving playing a video game.  I got to play.  I enjoyed myself. right? I'm craving some chocolate icecream. I was able to have it. I enjoyed myself. cravings!  When cravings are fulfilled. that's when enjoyment happens. You have an itch. you scratch it. that's enjoyment. enjoyment does not happen outside of that.
And so our temptations are also a cravings. The attraction a man has towards a woman is also a craving. And allah says in this world. I gave you means by which you CAN enjoy yourselves. You can fulfill all your craving in a legitimate way. I've given you provisions for all of that. All of that is covered.
وَجَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَعَيِشَ
